# Welcome | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This is the wiki for the 1.21 version of Custom Machinery.

For the 1.19 version go [herearrow-up-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.19)
.

For the 1.18 version go [herearrow-up-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.18/)
.

For the 1.16 version go [herearrow-up-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.16/)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21#creating-a-custom-machine)

Creating a custom machine

circle-info

Since 1.21 Custom Machinery now features a nice editor gui to let you create and edit machines on the fly.

Open the game, join a world, type **/cm create** and begin the creation of your own custom machine.

Custom machines can also be created in json files (datapack).

[Creating custom machineschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21#creating-machine-recipes)

Creating machine recipes

There are 3 ways to create custom machine recipes :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21#json-datapack)

Json (datapack)

[Machine recipechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21#javascript-kubejs)

Javascript (KubeJS)

[Recipeschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/recipes)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21#deprecated-zenscript-crafttweaker)

_Deprecated -_ Zenscript (Crafttweaker)

circle-exclamation

Crafttweaker support is deprecated in 1.21, it is recommended to switch to KubeJS instead.

[Recipeschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21#crafting-your-machine)

Crafting your machine

[Crafting your machinechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/crafting-your-machine)

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21#datapacks)

Datapacks

Custom machinery make heavy use of datapacks, if you're not familiar about datapacks see :

[Datapackchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/datapack)

# Creating a custom machine with datapack | Custom Machinery 1.21

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#the-json-file)

The json file

Custom Machines json files should be located in `datapacks/<datapack>/data/<namespace>/machine/<machine>.json`

*   <datapack> : The name of your datapack, can be whatever you want.
    
*   <namespace> : The namespace of your machine, must be lowercase without spaces or special characters.
    
*   <machine> : The id of your machine, must be lowercase without spaces or special characters except "\_" and "/".
    

Each machines loaded in the game should have a different ID, in the example above the machine Id is : `namespace:machine`

You can put any number of machines under the same namespace or separate them.

You can also use subfolders like : `datapacks/datapack/data/namespace/machine/tier1/machine.json` so the machine ID will be `namespace:tier1/machine`

Just remember that all the machines json files should be under the `machine` folder.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#machine-properties)

Machine properties

The machine json has 1 mandatory property and 7 optional properties.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

chevron-rightName[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#name)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#name-name)

Name : `name`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#description)

Description :

The name of the machine, not to be confused with the ID of the machine (which is the path to the machine json).

It will be the name of both the machine item and the jei category for this machine recipes.

It will also be displayed in The One Probe when the player is pointing the machine block.

The specified name must be a string, any characters are allowed (as long as Minecraft can parse it), it can also be a lang key or a [Text Component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 to add more customization options.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#examples)

Examples :

Copy

    //Raw string
    "name": "My cool machine"
    
    //Lang key
    "name": "machine.example.cool"
    
    //Text component
    "name": {
        "text": "My cool machine",
        "color": "red"
    }

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#optional-properties)

Optional properties

[Machine appearancechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance)
chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#description-1)

Description :

A list of tooltips that will be displayed when the player cursor hover the machine item in a gui.

The tooltips can be a raw string or a [Text Component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
.

Each tooltips of the list will be displayed in a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#examples-1)

Examples :

[Machine componentschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components)
[Machine GUIchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui)
[JEI Recipe GUIchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/jei-recipe-gui)
[Catalystschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/catalysts)
[Processorchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#empty-template)

Empty template

An empty template of a machine json with all it's properties.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack#examples-2)

Examples

circle-info

You can download the test datapack [herearrow-up-right](https://download-directory.github.io/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2FFrinn38%2FCustom-Machinery%2Ftree%2F1.21%2Ftest_datapack)
.

See a few examples of custom machines in [the test datapackarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Frinn38/Custom-Machinery/tree/1.21/test_datapack/data/custommachinery/machine)
.

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    //Raw string
    "tooltips": "That machine is really cool"
    
    //List of strings
    "tooltips": ["That machine is really cool", "Try it and see"]
    
    //Text component
    "tooltips": {
        "text": "That machine is really cool",
        "color": "red"
    }
    
    //List of text components
    "tooltips": [\
        {\
            "text": "That machine is really cool",\
            "color": "red"\
        },\
        {\
            "text": "Try it and see",\
            "bold": true\
        }\
    ]

machine.json

Copy

    {
        "name": "",
        "appearance": {},
        "tooltips": [],
        "components": [],
        "gui": [],
        "jei": [],
        "catalysts": []
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Creating an upgraded machine | Custom Machinery 1.21

Upgraded machines are a type of custom machine that inherit all properties from another existing custom machine.

circle-exclamation

The "parent" machine (which serves as the basis for the upgraded machine) must be an existing custom machine, from the Custom Machinery mod.

You can't make an upgraded machine out of vanilla or other mods machines.

To define an upgraded machine, simply add `"parent": "namespace:machine_id"` in the upgraded machine json.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-an-upgraded-machine#base-example)

Base example

This is the full content of an upgraded machine json file, that inherit all properties from the machine with id `custommachinery:power_crusher`.

Copy

    {
        "parent": "custommachinery:power_crusher"
    }

If not overridden the machine name will show as "Upgraded <name>" where `<name>` is the name of its parent machine, in the example above the upgraded machine's name will be "Upgraded Power Crusher".

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-an-upgraded-machine#overriding-properties)

Overriding properties

Upgraded machines can override properties of its parent machine, by specifying the same property in the upgraded machine json.

In the following example the upgraded machine will **not** inherit the `gui` property from its parent machine.

Copy

    {
        "parent": "custommachinery:power_crusher",
        "gui": [\
            //put some gui elements here\
        ]
    }

All properties from the parent machine can be overridden, a list of all properties that a custom machine can have is available [here](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-an-upgraded-machine#recipe-modifiers)

Recipe modifiers

Upgraded machines can include a list of recipe modifiers, that will be automatically applied when the machine is processing a recipe.

In the example below all recipes processed by the upgraded machine will require 1.5x more energy but half the time to complete the recipe.

More info about recipe modifiers can be found [here](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-an-upgraded-machine#about-recipes)

About recipes

By default all recipes that can be processed by the parent machine can also be processed by the upgraded machine.

This can be disabled by adding the following property in the upgraded machine json :

circle-info

If you want to make a recipe that is processable by only the upgraded machine, simply use the upgraded machine id in the recipe json/script instead of the parent machine id.

[PreviousCreating a custom machine with datapackchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-a-custom-machine-with-datapack)
[NextMachine appearancechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Base example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-an-upgraded-machine#base-example)
    
*   [Overriding properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-an-upgraded-machine#overriding-properties)
    
*   [Recipe modifiers](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-an-upgraded-machine#recipe-modifiers)
    
*   [About recipes](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/creating-an-upgraded-machine#about-recipes)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    {
        "parent": "custommachinery:power_crusher",
        "modifiers": [\
            {\
                "requirement": "custommachinery:speed",\
    	    "mode": "input",\
    	    "operation": "multiplication",\
    	    "modifier": 0.5\
    	},\
    	{\
                "requirement": "custommachinery:energy_per_tick",\
    	    "mode": "input",\
    	    "operation": "multiplication",\
    	    "modifier": 1.5\
    	}\
        ]
    }

Copy

    "allow_parent_recipes": false

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# Block appearance | Custom Machinery 1.21

Machine block appearance is defined using the `block` property inside the `appearance` property.

This property is optional and will use the default machine model if not specified.

There is 2 way of using this property :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/block-appearance#using-a-blockstate)

Using a blockstate

The `block` property can take a blockstate using the format : `namespace:block_id[state1=value,state2=value...]`

The blockstates properties are optional, you can just use `namespace:block_id` and the machine will use that block default state.

You don't have to use all the block's state properties, if some are not specified their default value will be used instead.

Example :

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "block": "minecraft:furnace[lit=true]"
    }

That way the machine will use the appearance of a vanilla lit furnace.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/block-appearance#using-a-custom-model)

Using a custom model

If you don't want to mimic an existing block you can use the block property to point a custom model that the machine will use.

The model must be a Minecraft type json model, if you are not familiar with this type of model see the official MC Wiki (note : you need only the model and texture file but not the blockstates file)

The model **MUST** be loaded in-game using either a ResourcePack or a Resource Loader mod like Open Loader.

The model **MUST** be located in `assets/namespace/models/machine` any other model location such as assets/namespace/models/block will not work.

Example : A model located in `assets/namespace/models/machine/my_machine.json` must be defined as `namespace:machine/my_machine`, the model loader will search for files in the models folder and it's subfolders and will also add the .json so you don't have to.

Example :

That way the machine will use the file located in `assets/custommachinery/models/machine/my_model.json` as the machine model.

circle-exclamation

**Adding a new custom model inside that directory will require a game restart**

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/block-appearance#notes)

Notes

If you use a custom minecraft json model for your machine you can color some faces using the `tintIndex` property (inside the json model).

Available `tintIndex` values are:

*   1 : color the face using the biome water color
    
*   2 : color the face using the biome grass color
    
*   3 : color the face using the biome foliage color
    
*   4 : color the face using the Machine Appearance color property value
    

If you don't specify a tintIndex in the json model the face will use it's texture and not color it.

[PreviousMachine appearancechevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance)
[NextItem appearancechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/item-appearance)

*   [Using a blockstate](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/block-appearance#using-a-blockstate)
    
*   [Using a custom model](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/block-appearance#using-a-custom-model)
    
*   [Notes](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/block-appearance#notes)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "block": "custommachinery:machine/my_model"
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Item appearance | Custom Machinery 1.21

By default the machine item will have the same appearance that the machine block, you can change it by using the Item Property.

There is 2 way of using the `item` property :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/item-appearance#using-an-item)

Using an item

The `item` property can take an item using the format : `namespace:item_id` and will mimic its model and textures.

Example :

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "item": "minecraft:diamond"
    }

That way the machine item will show as a vanilla diamond.

Note: for items with animated textures (bow/compass/watch...) that may not work or cause issues. For items with more complex rendering (trident, chest, armor stand...) that will just not works.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/item-appearance#using-a-custom-model)

Using a custom model

If you don't want to mimic an existing item you can use the `item` property to point a custom model that the machine will use.

The model must be a Minecraft type json model, if you are not familiar with this type of model see the official MC Wiki.

The model MUST be loaded in-game using either a ResourcePack or a Resource Loader mod like Open Loader.

The model MUST be located in assets/namespace/models/machine any other model location such as assets/namespace/models/item will not work.

Example : A model located in assets/namespace/models/machine/my\_machine.json must be defined as namespace:machine/my\_machine, the model loader will search for files in the models folder and it's subfolders and will also add the .json so you don't have to.

Example :

That way the machine will use the file located in assets/custommachinery/models/machines/my\_model.json as the machine item model.

circle-exclamation

**Adding a new custom model inside that directory will require a game restart.**

[PreviousBlock appearancechevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/block-appearance)
[NextSound (Ambient)chevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient)

*   [Using an item](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/item-appearance#using-an-item)
    
*   [Using a custom model](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/item-appearance#using-a-custom-model)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "item": "custommachinery:machines/my_model"
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Machine appearance | Custom Machinery 1.21

The machine appearance is what will define the in-game appearance (model/texture/sound/etc) of the machine block and item.

A machine appearance can be defined for each status of the machine : `idle`, `running`, `errored` and `paused` independantly.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance#json-structure)

Json structure

circle-info

All properties are optional and have default values.

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "property1": "defaultValue",
        "property2": 1,
        "idle": {
            "property1": "value",
            "property2": 42
        },
        "running": {
            "property1": "some_value",
            "property2": 23
        },
        "errored": {
            "property1": "another_value",
            "property2": 666
        },
        "paused": {
            "property1": "again_another_value",
            "property2": 56487
        }
    }

*   If a property is not specified for a status, the property defined directly inside the `appearance` block is used as default.
    
*   Basically the properties defined for a specified machine status override the properties defined for the whole appearance, which themselves override the default values for this property.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance#properties)

Properties

Machine appearance currently have 10 optional properties :

[Block appearancechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/block-appearance)
[Item appearancechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/item-appearance)
[Sound (Ambient)chevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient)
[Sound (Interaction)chevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-interaction)
[Lightchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/light)
[Colorchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/color)
[Hardnesschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/hardness)
[Resistancechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/resistance)
[Tool typechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/tool-type)
[Mining levelchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/mining-level)
[Requires toolchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/requires-tool)
[Shapechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/shape)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance#default-machine-appearance)

Default machine appearance

This is what will be used by default for properties that are not specified :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance#examples)

Examples

chevron-rightExample 1[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance#example-1)

The machine with this machine appearance will have the appearance of a TNT block and when running it will make the sound of an anvil and emit a light level of 10.

chevron-rightExample 2[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance#example-2)

This machine will have the appearance of an unlit furnace when idle, errored or paused, and the appearance of a lit furnace and emit light when running.

    "appearance": {
        "block": "custommachinery:block/custom_machine_block",
        "item": "custommachinery:block/custom_machine_block",
        "ambient_sound": "",

        "block": "minecraft:tnt",
        "sound": "minecraft:block.anvil.place",
        "light": 10
    }

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "block": "minecraft:furnace",
        "running": {
            "block": "minecraft:furnace[lit=true]",
            "light": 15
        }
    }

# Sound (Ambient) | Custom Machinery 1.21

You can define a sound that will play when the machine is in a specific status (corresponding of where you put the property in the appearance json).

The sound must be a OGG file and must be loaded in-game. Sounds are different than models and textures and must be registered to be usable so for using custom sounds you will have either to use a mod that let you add sounds to the game or replace an existing sound with a resource pack and use it's name in the property.

circle-info

If no sound property is set the machine will just make no sound.

Ambient sound has 1 mandatory property and can be configured with 7 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#mandatory-property)

Mandatory property :

chevron-rightSound[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#sound)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#name-sound)

Name : `sound`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#description)

Description :

The id of the sound to play while the machine is in the specified status.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#example)

Example :

Use the vanilla furnace sound :

Copy

    "ambient_sound" : {
        "sound": "minecraft:block.furnace.fire_crackle"
    }

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#optional-properties)

Optional properties :

chevron-rightVolume[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#volume)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#name-volume)

Name : `volume`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#description-1)

Description :

A positive float value used to calculate the volume of the played sound.

Values higher than 1.0 will increase the volume and values between 0.0 and 1.0 will lower it.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#default-1.0)

Default : `1.0`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#example-1)

Example :

The sound's volume will be doubled :

Copy

    "ambient_sound": {
        "volume": 2.0
    }

chevron-rightPitch[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#pitch)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#name-pitch)

Name : `pitch`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#description-2)

Description :

A positive float value used to calculate the pitch of the played sound.

Values higher than 1.0 will increase the pitch and values between 0.0 and 1.0 will lower it.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#default-1.0-1)

Default : `1.0`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#example-2)

Example :

The sound's pitch will be doubled :

Copy

    "ambient_sound": {
        "pitch": 2.0
    }

chevron-rightSource[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#source)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#name-source)

Name : source

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#description-3)

Description :

One of Minecraft sound sources :

*   master
    
*   music
    
*   record
    
*   weather
    
*   block
    
*   hostile
    
*   neutral
    
*   player
    
*   ambient
    
*   voice
    

The player can adjust any of these sound sources in sound options.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#default-block)

Default : `block`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#example-3)

Example :

The machine's ambient sound will be played as "music" source :

Copy

    "ambient_sound": {
        "source": "music"
    }

chevron-rightLoop[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#loop)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#name-loop)

Name : `loop`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#description-4)

Description :

A boolean value which set if the sound should be looped or not.

If set to false the machine will still play the sound continuously but there will be a short blank between each loop.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#default-true)

Default : `true`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#example-4)

Example :

Set the loop to false :

chevron-rightAttenuation[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#attenuation)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#name-attenuation)

Name : `attenuation`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#description-5)

Description :

A boolean value which set if the sound should be attenuated or not.

If set to true, the sound's volume will decrease as the player moves away the machine.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#default-true-1)

Default : `true`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#example-5)

Example :

Set the attenuation to false :

chevron-rightDelay[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#delay)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#name-delay)

Name : `delay`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#description-6)

Description :

A positive integer value that sets the amount (in game ticks) that will be waited before playing the sound.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#default-0)

Default : `0`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#example-6)

Example :

Set the delay to 20 ticks (1 second) :

chevron-rightRelative[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#relative)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#name-relative)

Name : `relative`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#description-7)

Description :

Not sure of what this property does.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#default-false)

Default : `false`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient#example-7)

Example :

# Sound (Interaction) | Custom Machinery 1.21

The `interaction_sound` property can be used to customize which sound the machine will make when the player place/break/hit/step on/fell on it.

There are 2 ways of using this property :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-interaction#copying-another-block)

Copying another block

Simply specify a block id to the property and the machine will copy all sounds it make.

You can also use the `namespace:block[property1=value1,property2=value2]` syntax here as some blocks may have different sounds depending on their state.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-interaction#example)

Example

This machine will make the same sound than a netherite block.

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "interaction_sound": "minecraft:netherite_block"
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-interaction#tweaking-sounds-individually)

Tweaking sounds individually

The 5 interaction sounds `break`, `place`, `hit`, `fall` and `step` can be defined independently.

You can define them using either :

*   A block : `namespace:block_id`
    
*   A blockstate : `namespace:block_id[property=value, property2=value2]`
    
*   A sound : `namespace:sound_id`
    

circle-info

Look at the suggestions given by the `/playsound` command in game to see all available sound ids. You can also add your own sounds.

You can also specify a `volume` and `pitch` that will be used when playing the sound.

Default value for both `volume` and `pitch` is 1.0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-interaction#example-1)

Example

This machine will have the sound of the stone when placed, the grass when broken, and the npc hurt sound when step on.

[PreviousSound (Ambient)chevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-ambient)
[NextLightchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/light)

Last updated 11 months ago

*   [Copying another block](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-interaction#copying-another-block)
    
*   [Tweaking sounds individually](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-interaction#tweaking-sounds-individually)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "interaction_sound": {
          "volume": 1.0,
          "pitch": 1.0,
          "place": "minecraft:stone",
          "break": "minecraft:grass",
          "step": "minecraft:entity.villager.hurt"
        }
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# Hardness | Custom Machinery 1.21

Hardness is a float value used to calculate the breaking speed of the machine block.

The higher the hardness the longer the breaking time.

The default hardness is 3.5.

circle-info

A hardness of -1 will make the block unbreakable (like bedrock).

Some comparisons with vanilla blocks :

*   Wool : 0.8
    
*   Stone : 1.5
    
*   Dirt : 0.5
    
*   Obsidian : 50
    
*   Netherrack : 0.4
    
*   End stone : 3
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/hardness#example)

Example

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "hardness": 42
    }

[PreviousColorchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/color)
[NextResistancechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/resistance)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# Color | Custom Machinery 1.21

You can specify a color property to apply to a custom machine model.

This property must be specified inside the `appearance` property.

The color must be an integer of type: 0xRRGGBB: go [herearrow-up-right](https://www.shodor.org/stella2java/rgbint.html)
 if you don't know how to calculate an integer color from RGB values.

The color will only be applied to faces of the model that have `"tintIndex": 4` specified, all other faces will be ignored and not be colored.

circle-info

You can find some infos about `tintIndex` face property on the [Minecraft Wikiarrow-up-right](https://minecraft.fandom.com/wiki/Model#Block_models)

Default : 16777215 Full white color, this will not change the texture color.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/color#example)

Example:

This will apply a full red color to all faces of the machine model that have `"tintIndex": 4` property.

Copy

    {
        "appearance": {
            "color": 16711680
        }
    }

[PreviousLightchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/light)
[NextHardnesschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/hardness)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# Light | Custom Machinery 1.21

Custom machines support light emission, to make your machine emit light you will need to define the `light` property inside the machine `appearance` property.

The `light` property define the light the machine will be emitting.

The light level must be an integer between 0 and 15 (defined by vanilla, a torch emit 14 and a redstone torch 7 for example).

Example :

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "light": 15
    }

circle-info

The default light is 0.

[PreviousSound (Interaction)chevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/sound-interaction)
[NextColorchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/color)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Machine components | Custom Machinery 1.21

Machine components are what allow the machine to use the different systems the game provide.

These components must be defined in the machine json, under the `component` property.

circle-info

There is no limit to how many components you can add.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components#available-components)

Available components

There are currently 4 available components :

[Energy componentchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component)
[Fluid componentchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component)
[Item componentchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component)
[Redstone componentchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components#template)

Template

Copy

    {
        "name": "Machine",
        "appearance": {},
        "components": [\
            {\
                //First component\
            }, \
            {\
                //Second component\
            }\
        ]
    }

circle-info

Machine Components are optional, if you don't want it just don't put it in the machine json.

[PreviousKeep inventorychevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/keep-inventory)
[NextChemical component (Mekanism)chevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism)

# Resistance | Custom Machinery 1.21

Resistance is a float value used to calculate the explosion resistance of the machine block.

Blocks with higher resistance won't be destroyed when near an explosion.

The default resistance is 3.5.

Some comparisons with vanilla blocks :

*   Wool : 0.8
    
*   Stone : 6
    
*   Dirt : 0.5
    
*   Obsidian : 1200
    
*   Netherrack : 0.4
    
*   End stone : 9
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/resistance#example)

Example

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "resistance": 42
    }

[PreviousHardnesschevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/hardness)
[NextTool typechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/tool-type)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# Requires tool | Custom Machinery 1.21

The `requires_tool` property define whether the player need the tool defined in the [Tool type](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/tool-type)
 property to harvest the machine.

If set to true, the machine block will drop only when broken by the defined tool. Otherwise the machine will be destroyed and won't drop.

If set to false, the machine block will always drop when broken, even by hand. Tools specified in the `tool_type` property will still be faster to break the machine than other tools.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/requires-tool#default-true)

Default : true

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/requires-tool#example)

Example :

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "requires_tool": false
    }

[PreviousMining levelchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/mining-level)
[NextShapechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/shape)

Last updated 1 year ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Mining level | Custom Machinery 1.21

The required mining level to break the machine block can be defined using the `mining_level` property.

The machine will still be breakable with lower tools or bare hands but it will be much slower and will not drop the machine block (its contents will still be dropped).

The specified mining level must be a block tag.

Default : `minecraft:needs_stone_tool`

Available values :

*   `minecraft:needs_stone_tool`
    
*   `minecraft:needs_iron_tool`
    
*   `minecraft:needs_diamond_tool`
    
*   `forge:needs_netherite_tool`
    

circle-info

If a mod or a datapack add another mining level tag, it can be used here.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/mining-level#example)

Example

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "mining_level": "minecraft:needs_diamond_tool"
    }

[PreviousTool typechevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/tool-type)
[NextRequires toolchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/requires-tool)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# Shape | Custom Machinery 1.21

The machine shape is used for collisions with entities and particles, as well as to define the clickable area of the block (for using or mining).

The default machine shape is 1 full block.

A custom machine shape shouldn't be bigger than 1 block.

circle-info

You can use `"shape_collision"` instead of `"shape"` to only change the collision shape of the machine block.

There are 2 way of defining a custom machine shape :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/shape#mimic-the-shape-of-another-block)

Mimic the shape of another block

Use :

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "shape": "mod:block[property1=value1,property2=value2]"
    }

to mimic the shape of another block, the \[\] is used to specify block properties and can be omitted. Example :

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "shape": "minecraft:repeater"
    }

The machine shape will be the same as the vanilla repeater.

**NOTE :** Not every block shape can be used, for some advanced blocks that don't have a consistent shape, defined by their block properties it just won't work.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/shape#making-the-shape-yourself)

Making the shape yourself

You can specify an array of box, defined by their min and max values on the 3 axis. The resulting shape will be the addition of all these box.

A box is defined like this : `[minX, minY, minZ, maxX, maxY, maxZ]`

All the box values must be between 0.0 and 1.0, a full block box is \[0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 1\].

Example : A lower slab shape.

[PreviousRequires toolchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/requires-tool)
[NextKeep inventorychevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/keep-inventory)

*   [Mimic the shape of another block](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/shape#mimic-the-shape-of-another-block)
    
*   [Making the shape yourself](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/shape#making-the-shape-yourself)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "shape": [[0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0, 0.5, 1.0]]
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# Tool type | Custom Machinery 1.21

The required tool type to break the machine can be defined using the `tool_type` property.

The machine will still be breakable with other tools or bare hands but it will be much slower and will not drop the machine block unless the `requires_tool` property is set to false (its contents will still be dropped).

The specified tool type must be a block tag.

You can specify a list of tags to make several tools able to break the machine.

Default : `minecraft:mineable/pickaxe`

Available values :

*   `minecraft:mineable/shovel`
    
*   `minecraft:mineable/pickaxe`
    
*   `minecraft:mineable/axe`
    
*   `minecraft:mineable/hoe`
    

circle-info

If a mod or a datapack add another tool type tag, it can be used here.

circle-info

If you want the machine to be breakable by hand (and drop itself) you must put the [Requires Tool](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/requires-tool)
 property to false.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/tool-type#example)

Example

Only axe will be able to break the machine.

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "tool_type": "minecraft:mineable/axe"
    }

Both axe and hoe will be able to break the machine.

[PreviousResistancechevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/resistance)
[NextMining levelchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/mining-level)

Last updated 1 year ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "tool_type": ["minecraft:mineable/axe", "minecraft:mineable/axe"]
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# Keep inventory | Custom Machinery 1.21

The `keep_inventory` property define whether the machine will keep its inventory when broken, or will drop it on ground.

If set to true, everything stored inside the machine (items, fluids, energy, xp, addons components...) will be saved inside the machine item when the machine block is broken by a player.

circle-exclamation

If the `requires_tool` property is set to true and player breaking the machine doesn't use the correct tool defined in the `tool_type` and `mining_level` properties, the machine won't drop and everything will be lost.

circle-info

Machines with a saved inventory won't stack with other machines.

If set to false, only items and xp will drop on ground, everything else will be lost.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/keep-inventory#default-false)

Default: false

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/keep-inventory#example)

Example:

Copy

    "appearance": {
        "keep_inventory": true
    }

[PreviousShapechevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance/shape)
[NextMachine componentschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components)

Last updated 1 year ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Contraption component (Create) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This component requires [Custom Machinery Createarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-create)
 to be installed.

The contraption machine component is used to customize which sides of the machine are able to connect with Create kinetic network (shafts, gears, motors etc...).

This component is fully optional, if not present the machine will still be able to interact with Create kinetic network on all sides.

This component can also be used to make the machine bring a kinetic stress impact on the network by default when the machine is idle, errored or paused. If the machine is running the kinetic stress impact defined on the recipe takes priority over the value defined in this component.

circle-info

Only one contraption component must be added per machine.

Contraption component is defined with `"type": "custommachinery:contraption"` in the json.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#properties)

Properties

The contraption component has 1 mandatory property and 2 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#mandatory-property)

Mandatory property

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:contraption" //Mandatory to define a contraption component.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightStress impact[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#stress-impact)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#name-stress_impact)

Name : `stress_impact`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#description)

Description :

A positive decimal value that define the kinetic stress impact the machine will bring to the network when idle, errored or paused.

If the machine is running the kinetic stress impact defined on the recipe takes priority over the value defined in this component.

Note : if the machine currently has a rotation speed of 64 rpm and a stress impact of 2 that means it will take a total of 64 \* 2 = 128 SU from the kinetic network, of course if the network doesn't have enouh SU capacity it will overstress and stop rotating.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#example)

Example :

The machine will add a kinetic stress impact of 2 by default :

Copy

    "stress_impact": 2

chevron-rightConfig[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#config)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#name-config)

Name : `config`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#description-1)

Description :

An I/O side config specified the same as any other sided components (item, fluid, energy...). See [its dedicated wiki page](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config)
 for more info about usage and syntax.

The difference here is that input, output and both modes does exactly the same. As long as the side mode is not "none" the machine will accept kinetic network on that side.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#default)

Default :

The "both" side mode will be used as default on all sides, which mean the machine will accept kinetic network on all sides by default.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#example-1)

Example :

The machine will accept kinetic network only on the top side :

Copy

    "config": {
        "default": "none",
        "top": "both"
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#example-2)

Example

An example of a contraption component that will allow the machine to interact with a create shaft only on the left and right sides and bring a kinetic stress impact of 4.

You just have to put that in the `components` array in the machine json.

[PreviousChunkload componentchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component)
[NextEnergy componentchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component)

*   [Properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#properties)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create#example-2)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:contraption",
        "config": {
            "default": "none",
            "left": "both",
            "right": "both"
        },
        "stress_impact": 4
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# Chunkload component | Custom Machinery 1.21

The chunkload component can be used to make the machine always load an area around it.

The chunkloaded area will be a square of chunks, centered around the chunk that contains the machine block.

The radius of the chunkload area is limited to 32 chunks max (which means a square of 63 chunks on each sides, or 3969 loaded chunks).

The chunks will be loaded as long as the machine block is placed, when removed the chunks will be unloaded (unless something else load them).

circle-info

You can also make the machine chunkload an area **only if** a recipe is processing.

See [Chunkload requirement](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chunkload)
.

Chunkload component is defined with `"type": "custommachinery:chunkload"` in the json.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component#properties)

Properties

The chunkload component only has 1 mandatory property and 1 optional property :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component#mandatory-property)

Mandatory property

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:chunkload" //Mandatory to define a chunkload component.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component#optional-property)

Optional property

chevron-rightRadius[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component#radius)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component#name-radius)

Name : `radius`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component#description)

Description :

The radius (in chunks) of the chunkloading area. The radius include the center chunk (where the machine is placed) so a radius of 2 means an area of 3x3 chunks.

Must be between 1 and 32.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component#default-1)

Default : `1`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component#example)

Example :

The machine will chunkload an area of 3x3 chunks.

Copy

    "radius": 2

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component#example-1)

Example

A machine with this chunkload requirement will always chunkload an area of 3x3 chunks around it :

[PreviousChemical component (Mekanism)chevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism)
[NextContraption component (Create)chevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component#properties)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component#example-1)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:chunkload",
        "radius": 2
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# Energy component | Custom Machinery 1.21

This is the component that let your machine interact with the Forge Energy system, it is compatible with most modern mods (IC2 excluded) so any mods that use FE or RF will be able to insert or extract energy to and from your machine.

circle-exclamation

Energy component is defined as a **unique** machine component, meaning that you can only have 1 per machine.

If you try to define more than 1 energy component only the last will be used.

Energy component is defined with `"type": "custommachinery:energy"` in the json.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#properties)

Properties

The energy component has 2 mandatory property and 5 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:energy" //Mandatory to define an energy component.

chevron-rightCapacity[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#capacity)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#name-capacity)

Name : `capacity`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#description)

Description :

A positive long that represent the amount of energy the machine can store.

Max value : 9,223,372,036,854,775,807

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#example)

Example :

Copy

    "capacity": 10000 //The machine can store 10000FE.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightMax input[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#max-input)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#name-maxinput)

Name : `maxInput`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer that represent the max FE that can be input in the machine during a single tick.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#default)

Default :

The `capacity` of the machine.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#example-1)

Example :

Copy

    "maxInput": 1000 //The machine can accept 1000FE/tick.

chevron-rightMin input[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#min-input)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#name-mininput)

Name : `minInput`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#description-2)

Description :

A positive integer that represent the min FE that can be input in the machine during a single tick.

If something (a pipe or the machine's auto-input) try to insert less than the specified amount the transfer will fail and nothing will be inserted.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#default-0)

Default : `0`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#example-2)

Example :

chevron-rightMax output[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#max-output)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#name-maxoutput)

Name : `maxOutput`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#description-3)

Description :

A positive integer that represent the max FE that can be output from the machine during a single tick.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#default-1)

Default :

The `capacity` of the machine.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#example-3)

Example :

chevron-rightMin output[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#min-output)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#name-minoutput)

Name : `minOutput`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#description-4)

Description :

A positive integer that represent the min FE that can be output from the machine during a single tick.

If something (a pipe or the machine's auto-output) try to extract less than the specified amount the transfer will fail and nothing will be extracted.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#default-0-1)

Default : `0`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#example-4)

Example :

[I/O Configchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#example-5)

Example

An example of an Energy Component that will allow the machine to store 100000FE, input 1000FE and output 666FE.

You just have to put that in the `components` array in the machine json.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component#notes)

Notes

The energy generated/consumed by a recipe is not counted in the maxInput/maxOutput value and will bypass it.

Only energy inserted/extracted by a cable or another machine will be counted.

If the `maxOutput` property is greater than 0 the machine will try to send its stored energy to any energy receiver next to it.

[PreviousContraption component (Create)chevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create)
[NextExperience componentchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component)

    "minInput": 1000 //The machine will accept at least 1000FE/tick.

Copy

    "maxOutput": 1000 //The machine can give 1000FE/tick.

Copy

    "minOutput": 1000 //The machine will extract at least 1000FE/tick.

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:energy",
        "capacity": 100000,
        "maxInput": 1000,
        "maxOutput": 666
    }

# Catalysts | Custom Machinery 1.21

The machine json have a `catalysts` property, used to tell jei that other machines can craft the same recipes that this machine.

This is only used for display and navigating through the jei recipe gui.

The machines must be specified by their ID, a machine json located in `data/mymod/machines/mymachine.json` will have an ID of `mymod:mymachine`.

The `catalysts` can be 1 machine ID or an array.

circle-info

The current machine is already specified by default, you don't need to put it again in that list.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/catalysts#example)

Example

Add the following property to the Power Crusher in the test datapack, now when checking a Power Crusher recipe jei will also display the Stone Generator and Magic Spawner at the left of the GUI.

Copy

    {
        "catalysts": ["custommachinery:magic_spawner", "custommachinery:stone_generator"]
    }

![](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2FFrinn38%2FCustom-Machinery%2Fraw%2F1.16.5%2Fwiki%2Fcatalysts.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6004319c&sv=2)

example

[PreviousJEI Recipe GUIchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/jei-recipe-gui)
[NextProcessorchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor)

# JEI Recipe GUI | Custom Machinery 1.21

All your machines recipe are displayed in jei without you having to do anything (beside the machine and recipe json).

The jei recipe gui will be a copy of the [Machine Gui](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui)
 you created.

circle-info

A few types of elements such as text and texture are not displayed in jei unless their own "jei" property is set to true.

But in some cases you may want to have a different gui for your recipes than the machine one, with more or less elements.

To do that you can make your own jei recipe gui. By simply using the `"jei"` property in the machine json and putting here a list of elements you want to be displayed in jei.

The syntax and elements are exactly the same as in the `"gui"` property :

Copy

    "jei": [\
        {\
            "type": "custommachinery:slot",\
            "x": 0,\
            "y": 0\
        },\
        {\
            "type": "custommachinery:progress",\
            "x": 20,\
            "y": 20\
        }\
    ]

**NOTE** : As soon as you use the `"jei"` property in the machine json, all elements defined in the `"gui"` property will not be used by the jei recipe gui. You have to copy the elements you want to keep.

The machine gui itself will not change if you use this property, only the jei one will be affected.

[PreviousTexture elementchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element)
[NextCatalystschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/catalysts)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Craft | Custom Machinery 1.21

The craft processor is used to make the machine process [Craft recipes](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/craft#properties)

Properties

There is no additional properties for this processor.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/craft#example)

Example

Make the machine use the craft processor instead of the machine processor :

Copy

    {
        "name": "Name of the machine",
        "appearance": {},
        "processor": {
            "type": "custommachinery:craft"
        }
    }

# Processor | Custom Machinery 1.21

A processor is the part of the machine that process recipes.

Each processor type target a specific recipe type.

Specifying a processor is optional, if not specified the `machine` processor will be used.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor#available-processors)

Available processors

[Machinechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine)
[Craftchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/craft)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor#default)

Default

Default processor, if the property is not specified :

Copy

    "processor": {
        "type": "custommachinery:machine"
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor#example)

Example

If you want to use the [Craft processor](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/craft)
 instead :

Copy

    "processor": {
        "type": "custommachinery:craft"
    }

[PreviousCatalystschevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/catalysts)
[NextMachinechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine)

# Machine | Custom Machinery 1.21

The machine processor is used by default to process [Machine recipes](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe)
.

If the `"processor"` property is not specified in the machine json, this processor will be used by default.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#properties)

Properties

There are 2 optional properties for this processor :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightAmount[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#amount)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#name-amount)

Name : `amount`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#description)

Description :

A positive integer that define the amount of cores the processor can use.

Each core will be able to process a recipe in parallel, so the amount of cores define the amount of recipes that can be processed at a time by the machine.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#default-1)

Default : `1`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#example)

Example :

The machine will be able to process 2 machines at the same time :

Copy

    "amount": 2

chevron-rightCooldown[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#cooldown)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#name-cooldown)

Name : `cooldown`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#description-1)

Description :

The time in ticks between two recipe checks for a machine. When a machine using this processor fail to find a recipe to process (in idle mode) the machine will wait for a bit of time before checking the recipes again.

Decreasing this cooldown will make the machine start the process faster, but can also increase the lag generated by idle machines. Use with caution.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#default-20-ticks-1-second)

Default : 20 ticks (1 second)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#example-1)

Example :

The machine will now check recipes every ticks instead of every second :

Copy

    "cooldown": 1

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#example-2)

Example

Make the machine use the machine processor with 4 cores :

Copy

    {
        "name": "Name of the machine",
        "appearance": {},
        "processor": {
            "type": "custommachinery:machine",
            "amount": 4
        }
    }

[PreviousProcessorchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor)
[NextCraftchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/craft)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#properties)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine#example-2)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon
