# Experience component | Custom Machinery 1.21

The experience machine component can be used to make a machine able to store xp.

circle-exclamation

This component must be unique, as there is only one "type" of xp in vanilla Minecraft it wouldn't make sense to have several storage of xp in the same machine.

If you try to add more than 1 experience component only the last will be used.

There are 3 ways to change the amount of xp stored in an experience component :

*   Using a recipe with an experience requirement.
    
*   From the machine GUI by using an [experience gui element](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element)
    .
    
*   By setting the `"retrieve"` property (see below) to true a player will receive all the stored xp when taking an item out the specified slots (like in a vanilla furnace).
    

Experience component is defined with `"type": "custommachinery:experience"` in the json.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#properties)

Properties

The experience component has 2 mandatory properties and 2 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:experience" //Mandatory to define an experience component.

chevron-rightCapacity[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#capacity)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#name-capacity)

Name : `capacity`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#description)

Description :

An integer positive value that define the amount of xp points that can be stored in the machine's buffer.

This value is in literral xp points instead of xp levels, you can go [herearrow-up-right](https://minecraftxpcalculator.com/)
 to convert levels to xp values.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#example)

Example :

The machine will be able to store 100 levels worth of xp.

Copy

    "capacity": 30970

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightRetrieve[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#retrieve)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#name-retrieve)

Name : `retrieve`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#description-1)

Description :

A boolean value (true/false) that define if the player will get all the stored xp when taking an item from a slot in the machine gui, like it does in a vanilla furnace.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#default-false)

Default : `false`

The player will not recieve the stored xp when taking an item from any slots of the machine.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#example-1)

Example :

The player will get all the stored xp when taking xp from an item slot in the machine gui.

chevron-rightslots[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#slots)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#name-slots)

Name : `slots`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#description-2)

Description :

A single or list of slot id(s) that will make the player get all the stored xp when taking an item out of one of these slots. Only if the `retrieve` property is set to true.

An empty list mean any slot will be valid.

The slot id must be exactly the same as defined in the [item component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component)
 `id` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#default-empty)

Default : `empty`

Any slots can give the stored xp to the player.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#example-2)

Example :

Only the slot named "output" will give the xp to the player.

Both "output1" and "output2" slots will give the xp to the player.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#examples)

Examples

A very basic experience component that can store 100 levels worth of xp.

An experience component that can store 100 levels worth of xp and will give all the stored xp when the player take an item from the slot with id "output".

[PreviousEnergy componentchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component)
[NextFluid componentchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component)

Last updated 11 months ago

*   [Examples](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component#examples)

Copy

    "retrieve": true

Copy

    "slots": "output"

Copy

    "slots": ["output1", "output2"]

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:experience",
        "capacity": 30970
    }

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:experience",
        "capacity": 30970,
        "retrieve": true,
        "slots": "output"
    }

# Heat component (Mekanism) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This component requires [Custom Machinery Mekanismarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-mekanism)
 to be installed.

This is the component that let your machine interact with the Mekanism heat system, it is also compatible with any mods that make use of Mekanism heat.

circle-exclamation

Heat component is defined as a **unique** machine component, meaning that you can only have 1 per machine.

If you try to define more than 1 heat component only the first will be used.

The heat component make use of the Config property (same as items, fluid, energy, gas etc...) to configure which sides of the machine can transfer heat.

By default all sides of the machine will be in `enabled` mode.

Heat component is defined with `"type": "custommachinery:heat"` in the json.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#properties)

Properties

The heat component has only 1 mandatory property and 5 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:heat" //Mandatory to define a heat component.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightCapacity[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#capacity)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#name-capacity)

Name : `capacity`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#description)

Description :

A positive double that represent the amount of heat (in Kelvin) needed to heat up the machine from 1K.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#default-1.0k)

Default : 1.0K

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#example)

Example :

Copy

    "capacity": 10 //The machine need 10 heat to heat up 1K.

chevron-rightBase temperature[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#base-temperature)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#name-base_temp)

Name : `base_temp`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#description-1)

Description :

The ambient temperature (in Kelvin) of the machine, if the machine is not heated nor cooled its temperature will slowly return to this value.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#default-300k-27-c)

Default : 300K (27°C)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#example-1)

Example :

The machine ambient temperature will be 373K or 100°C

Copy

    "base_temp": 373

chevron-rightInverse conduction coefficient[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#inverse-conduction-coefficient)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#name-conduction)

Name : `conduction`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#description-2)

Description :

I don't really know what it does, so here is the definition from Mekanism API :

_"This value defines how much heat is allowed to be dissipated. The larger the number the less heat can dissipate. The trade-off is that it also allows for lower amounts of heat to be inserted."_

It's a decimal value that must be greater than 0.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#default-1)

Default : 1

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#example-2)

Example :

The machine's inverse conduction coefficient will be 0.5

chevron-rightInverse insulation coefficient[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#inverse-insulation-coefficient)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#name-insulation)

Name : `insulation`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#description-3)

Description :

I don't really know what it does, so here is the definition from Mekanism API :

_"The larger the value the less heat dissipates into the environment."_

It's a decimal value.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism#example-3)

Example :

The machine's inverse insulation coefficient will be 1

# Upgrade | Custom Machinery 1.21

Use this variant to make an upgrade slot.

The slot will be able to hold [Machine upgrades](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades)
 and apply them to recipes.

circle-exclamation

The ["mode"](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#name-mode)
 property of an item component with upgrade variant must be `"input"` or `"both"` to let the player place upgrade items inside the slot.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/upgrade#id)

ID

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:item_upgrade"

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/upgrade#accepted-items)

Accepted items

Any item that are defined as machine upgrade and match the filter defined in the item component "whitelist" and "blacklist" properties.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/upgrade#example)

Example

A simple upgrade slot :

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:item_upgrade",
        "id": "upgrade",
        "mode": "input"
    }

[PreviousFuelchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fuel)
[NextResultchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/result)

# Pressure component (PNC) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This component requires [Custom Machinery Pneumaticcraftarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-pneumaticcraft)
 to be installed.

This is the component that let your machine interact with the PneumaticCraft pressure system, it is also compatible with any mods that make use of PneumaticCraft pressure.

circle-exclamation

Pressure component is defined as a **unique** machine component, meaning that you can only have 1 per machine.

If you try to define more than 1 pressure component only the first will be used.

The pressure component make use of the `config` property to configure which sides of the machine can handle pressure.

By default all sides will enable pressure.

Pressure component is defined with `"type": "custommachinery:pressure"` in the json.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#properties)

Properties

The pressure component has 4 mandatory properties and 1 optional property :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:pressure" //Mandatory to define a pressure component.

chevron-rightVolume[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#volume)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#name-volume)

Name : `volume`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#description)

Description :

An positive integer property that define the air volume available in the machine.

PneumaticCraft calculate the pressure using the amount of air stored in the defined volume.

The higher the volume, the longer it will take to increase or decrease pressure.

Note : The machine can store an unlimited amount of compressed air, if the stored amount is over the specified volume then the pressure will increase.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#example)

Example :

Set the volume to 10000mL.

Copy

    "volume": 10000

chevron-rightDanger[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#danger)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#name-danger)

Name : `danger`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#description-1)

Description :

A positive decimal value, between 0.0bar and 25.0bar.

The start of the "red" pressure on the gauge, if the machine reach a pressure higher than this danger pressure it has a chance to explode.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#example-1)

Example :

Set the danger pressure to 3bar.

Copy

    "danger": 3.0

chevron-rightCritical[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#critical)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#name-critical)

Name : `critical`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#description-2)

Description :

A positive decimal value, between 0.0bar and 25.0bar.

The highest pressure on the gauge, if the machine reach this danger pressure it will explode.

For practical reasons the critical pressure must be superior to the danger pressure.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#example-2)

Example :

Set the danger pressure to 3bar.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#optional-property)

Optional property

[Toggle Configchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/toggle-config)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#example-3)

Example

A basic pressure component :

[PreviousPNC Heat component (PNC)chevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc)
[NextRedstone componentchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#properties)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc#example-3)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    "danger": 3.0

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:pressure",
        "volume": 10000,
        "danger": 3,
        "critical": 5
    }

# Energy | Custom Machinery 1.21

Use this variant to make the slot able to fill/drain energy from the machine internal buffer to/from an energy container item placed in that slot.

The fill/drain behavior is determined by the "mode" property of the item component :

*   "input" will transfer the energy from the item to the machine buffer.
    
*   "output" will transfer the energy from the machine buffer to the item.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/energy#id)

ID

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:item_energy"

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/energy#accepted-items)

Accepted items

Any energy container items (most mods cells or batteries) that match the filter defined in the item component "whitelist" and "blacklist" properties.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/energy#example)

Example

A simple energy slot that transfer the energy from the item to the machine internal buffer :

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:item_energy",
        "id": "energyInput",
        "mode": "input"
    }

[PreviousFluidchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fluid)
[NextFilterchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/filter)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Accepted items](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/energy#accepted-items)

# PNC Heat component (PNC) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This component requires [Custom Machinery Pneumaticcraftarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-pneumaticcraft)
 to be installed.

This is the component that let your machine interact with the Pneumaticcraft heat system, it is also compatible with any mods that make use of Pneumaticcraft heat.

circle-exclamation

Heat component is defined as a **unique** machine component, meaning that you can only have 1 per machine.

If you try to define more than 1 heat component only the first will be used.

The heat component make use of the Config property (same as items, fluid, energy, gas etc...) to configure which sides of the machine can transfer heat.

By default all sides of the machine will be in `enabled` mode.

Heat component is defined with `"type": "custommachinery:pnc_heat"` in the json.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#properties)

Properties

The heat component has only 1 mandatory property and 3 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:pnc_heat" //Mandatory to define a PNC heat component.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightCapacity[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#capacity)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#name-capacity)

Name : `capacity`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#description)

Description :

A positive double that represent the amount of heat the machine needs to store to heat 1°C

Increasing that value means that the machine will need more heat to heat, and also will takes more time to cool down.

Most of Pneumaticcraft machines use **100** here.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#default-1)

Default : 1

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#example)

Example :

Copy

    "capacity": 100 //The machine heat capacity will be 100

chevron-rightResistance[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#resistance)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#name-resistance)

Name : `resistance`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#description-1)

Description :

A positive double, here is the description of what it does (copied from PNC code):

`The higher the thermal resistance, the slower the heat disperses. The effective resistance is the sum of this resistance plus the neighbour's resistance; if both exchangers have a resistance of 1, heat will equalize in a single tick under normal circumstances.`

In PNC the refinery and etching tanks use **10**. The advanced compressor use **200**.

Machine that needs to transmit their heat instantly, like the vortex tube use **0.01**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#default-1-1)

Default : 1

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#example-1)

Example :

The machine resistance will be 10.

Copy

    "resistance": 10

[Toggle Configchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/toggle-config)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#example-2)

Example

The most basic PNC heat component :

A heat component that will allow transfer heat on all sides but front :

[PreviousFilterchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/filter)
[NextPressure component (PNC)chevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc)

Last updated 7 months ago

*   [Properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#properties)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc#example-2)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:pnc_heat"
    }

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:pnc_heat",
        "config": {
            "default": "enabled",
            "front": "disabled"
        }
    }

# Fluid | Custom Machinery 1.21

Use this variant to make the slot able to fill/drain fluid from one or many machine's internal tanks to/from a tank item (including buckets) placed in that slot.

The fill/drain behavior is determined by the "mode" property of the item component :

*   "input" will drain the fluid container item content to the machine internal tank.
    
*   "output" will fill the fluid container item from the machine internal tank.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fluid#id)

ID

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:item_fluid"

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fluid#optional-property)

Optional property

A `"tanks"` property can be specified directly inside the item component json.

This property can define a tank id or an array of tank id that the item can be filled/drained from/to.

The id of the tanks must be the same as defined in the [fluid component "id" property](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#name-id)
.

If the `"tanks"` property is not specified the item will be filled/drained from/to all the machine internal tanks.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fluid#accepted-items)

Accepted items

Any fluid container items (including buckets) that match the filter defined in the item component "whitelist" and "blacklist" properties.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fluid#example)

Example

A simple fluid slot that transfer the fluid from the item to the machine internal tank :

A fluid slot that transfer the fluid from the machine internal tank with id "water" to the item :

[PreviousResultchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/result)
[NextEnergychevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/energy)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [ID](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fluid#id)
    
*   [Optional property](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fluid#optional-property)
    
*   [Accepted items](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fluid#accepted-items)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fluid#example)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:item_fluid",
        "id": "fluidInput",
        "mode": "input",
    }

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:item_fluid",
        "id": "fluidOutput",
        "mode": "output",
        "tanks": "water"
    }

# Result | Custom Machinery 1.21

Use this variant to make a craft recipe result slot.

A machine using the [craft processor](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/craft)
 to process [craft recipes](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe)
 must have at least one result slot.

When a craft recipe is processed its result item will appear in the result slot, and the player will be able to take it like in any crafting table.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/result#id)

ID

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:item_result"

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/result#accepted-items)

Accepted items

No items can be put in that slot, hoppers/pipes can't interact with it either.

Only a player can take the item outside this slot to process a craft recipe.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/result#example)

Example

A simple result slot :

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:item_result",
        "id": "result"
    }

[PreviousUpgradechevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/upgrade)
[NextFluidchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fluid)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [ID](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/result#id)
    
*   [Accepted items](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/result#accepted-items)

# Redstone component | Custom Machinery 1.21

Redstone component let you interact with the vanilla redstone logic system. It doesn't store anything on the machine, instead it can be used to define the redstone behavior of the machine.

This component is fully optional, if not added the machine won't react or emit redstone signal.

circle-exclamation

Redstone component is defined as a **unique** machine component, meaning that you can only have 1 per machine.

If you try to add more than 1 redstone component only the last will be used.

circle-info

Use the `config` property to specify which sides will input or output redstone signal.

Redstone component is defined with `"type": "custommachinery:redstone"` in the machine json.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#properties)

Properties

The redstone component has 1 mandatory property and 7 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#mandatory-property)

Mandatory property

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:redstone" //Mandatory to define a redstone component.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#optional-property)

Optional property

chevron-rightPower to pause[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#power-to-pause)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#name-powertopause)

Name : `powertopause`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#description)

Description :

Define the redstone signal power needed to pause the machine.

Put a number greater than 15 if you want the machine to never pause on redstone signal (since vanilla max redstone power is 15).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#default-1)

Default : 1

The machine will pause at any redstone signal.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#example)

Example :

The machine will pause if a redstone signal of 5 or more is applied to it.

Copy

    "powertopause": 5

chevron-rightCrafting power output[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#crafting-power-output)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#name-craftingpoweroutput)

Name : `craftingpoweroutput`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#description-1)

Description :

Define the redstone signal power emitted when the machine is processing a recipe.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#default-0)

Default : 0

The machine never emit redstone signal.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#example-1)

Example :

The machine will emit a redstone signal of 15 when processing.

Copy

    "craftingpoweroutput": 15

chevron-rightIdle power output[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#idle-power-output)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#name-idlepoweroutput)

Name : `idlepoweroutput`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#description-2)

Description :

Define the redstone signal power emitted when the machine is idle.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#default-0-1)

Default : 0

The machine never emit redstone signal.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#example-2)

Example :

The machine will emit a redstone signal of 15 when idle.

chevron-rightErrored power output[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#errored-power-output)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#name-erroredpoweroutput)

Name : `erroredpoweroutput`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#description-3)

Description :

Define the redstone signal power emitted when the machine is errored.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#default-0-2)

Default : 0

The machine never emit redstone signal.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#example-3)

Example :

The machine will emit a redstone signal of 15 when errored.

chevron-rightComparator input type[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#comparator-input-type)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#name-comparatorinputtype)

Name : `comparatorinputtype`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#description-4)

Description :

A component type that will be used to determine the redstone signal emitted by a vanilla comparator. All currently supported component types are :

*   `custommachinery:item` Will output a signal corresponding to the item in it's slot, the same way the vanilla chest does.
    
*   `custommachinery:fluid` Will output a signal corresponding to the amount of fluid in it's tank, 0 empty, 15 full, 8 half...
    
*   `custommachinery:energy` Will output a signal corresponding to the amount of energy in it's buffer, 0 empty, 15 full, 8 half...
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#default-custommachinery-energy)

Default : `custommachinery:energy`

The comparator will output a redstone signal based on the machine energy buffer (if present), or 0 if the machine doesn't have an energy component.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#example-4)

Example :

The comparator will output a redstone signal based on one of the machine internal fluid tank. Define the used fluid tank with the `comparatorinputid` property.

chevron-rightComparator input id[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#comparator-input-id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#name-comparatorinputid)

Name : `comparatorinputid`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#description-5)

Description :

Used with the `comparatorinputtype` property, define which component will be used in case of the component type specified is not single (so for items and fluid).

The id provided must be the same than the id defined in the component json. If no component can be found for this type and with this id, the comparator will output a redstone signal of 0.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#default-nothing)

Default : nothing

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#example-5)

Example :

The comparator will search for a component of the type defined in the `comparatorinputtype` property and with the id `input` and if found, will output a redstone signal based on this component.

[I/O Configchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/redstone-component#example-6)

Example

A redstone component that will make the machine :

*   Output a redstone signal of 0 when idle
    
*   Output a redstone signal of 7 when crafting
    
*   Output a redstone signal of 14 when errored
    
*   Pause when a redstone signal of 15 is received
    
*   Nearby comparators will output a signal based on an item in a slot with id "input"

[NextMachine GUIchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Filter | Custom Machinery 1.21

A filter slot is a slot that can be set to a specific item by clicking on it with the item.

The items won't be placed in the slot and will remain in the player inventory, instead the slot will display a ghost (transparent) version of the item.

Clicking the slot with an empty mouse cursor will clear it.

The "mode" property of a filter item component doesn't matter.

circle-info

To make a recipe requires the filter slot to be set to a specific item use an [Item filter](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/item-filter)
 requirement.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/filter#id)

ID

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:item_filter"

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/filter#accepted-items)

Accepted items

Any items that match the filter defined in the item component "whitelist" and "blacklist" properties.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/filter#example)

Example

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:item_filter",
        "id": "filter1"
    }

[NextPNC Heat component (PNC)chevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc)

# Craft recipe | Custom Machinery 1.21

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#description)

Description

Custom craft recipes can be used to make the machine behave like a crafting table.

The machine must have one Item Component with `"type": "custommachinery:item_result"`.

When all requirements checks, like time, weather, biome etc... are passed, the output item will appear in the result slot.

When the output item is taken out of the result slot by a player (this can't be automated) all requirements are processed, i.e. energy/fluid/items are consumed etc...

circle-exclamation

All "per\_tick" requirements can't be used with this recipe type.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#location)

Location

Custom craft recipe jsons must be located in `(my_datapack)/data/(namespace)/recipe/` (the same place as the vanilla recipes).

The (namespace) is a folder that can have any name, but must be all lowercase without spaces or special characters.

The machine name must be all lowercase with no spaces or any other characters than letters and numbers but you can use "\_" or "/". The file must be a .json file.

Example : `my_datapack/data/namespace/recipe/my_recipe.json`

Each recipes loaded in the game must have a different ID, in the example above the recipe Id is : namespace:my\_recipe

You can put any number of recipes under the same namespace or separate them.

You can also use subfolders like : `(my_datapack)/data/(namespace)/recipe/machine1/my_recipe.json` so the recipe ID will be `namespace:machine1/my_recipe`

Just remember that all the recipe json should be under the recipes folder.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#properties)

Properties

The recipe json has 3 mandatory properties and 5 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

chevron-rightMachine[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#machine)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#name-machine)

Name : `machine`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#description-1)

Description :

The machine this recipe is for.

You can set only one machine here so if you want the same recipe to work for different machines you must write the recipe for each machine and change this property.

**You must use here the Machine ID and not the machine name.**

If the machine ID is wrong or the machine doesn't exist the recipe will still load but it will be unusable in-game.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#example)

Example :

This recipe will be set for the machine with ID "namespace:my\_machine".

Reminder : "namespace:my\_machine" is the machine located in `(datapack)/data/namespace/machines/my_machine.json`

chevron-rightOutput[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#output)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#name-output)

Name : `output`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#description-2)

Description :

The item that will be output by this recipe.

This can just be the id of the item to output, or an object with both the `id` and the `Count` of items to craft.

A `tag` property can also be added to define the nbt of the output item.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#example-1)

Example :

The recipe will output 1 vanilla diamond.

The recipe will output 4 vanilla gold ingots.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#optional-properties)

Optional properties

[Requirementschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements)
chevron-rightJei[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#jei)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#name-jei)

Name : `jei`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#description-3)

Description :

An array of Requirements.

The requirements are specified exactly as in the `requirements` property above.

Requirements specified here will not be processed by the machine, they will just display in the jei recipe.

**The requirements specified here will override the requirements specified in the "requirements" property, so if this property is specified only its requirements will show in jei**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#default-empty)

Default : `empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#example-2)

Example :

Define 2 recipe requirements that won't be processed by the recipe, but will be the only 2 shown in the jei recipe gui.

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#description-4)

Description :

An integer between -2147483648 and 2147483647 that define which recipe will be used by the machine if several recipes pass all requirement checks.

The recipe with the highest priority will be used.

If several recipes pass the requirement checks and have the same priority the first loaded recipe will be used, this depends of the datapack order and can be a bit random so if you want to be sure of which recipe will be used first you must use the priority property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#example-3)

Example :

This recipe will be loaded before any recipe with a priority < 1000.

chevron-rightJei priority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#jei-priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#name-jeipriority)

Name : `jeiPriority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#description-5)

Description :

An integer between -2147483648 and 2147483647 that define which recipe will show first in jei, recipes with higher values will show before recipes with lower values.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#default-0-1)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#example-4)

Example :

This recipe will show in jei before any recipes with a priority < 1000.

chevron-rightHidden[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#hidden)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#name-hidden)

Name : `hidden`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#description-6)

Description :

If true the recipe will be hidden in JEI recipe gui.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#default-false)

Default : `false`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#example-5)

Example :

The recipe will be hidden in JEI :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#template)

Template

A default recipe template with all properties specified :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/craft-recipe#example-6)

Example

A recipe that takes 64 coals and 1000FE and output a diamond :

[PreviousMachine recipechevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe)

# Fuel | Custom Machinery 1.21

Use this item component variant to make the slot a fuel slot.

A fuel slot will burn the items inside it to process recipes that have a [Fuel requirement](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/fuel)
.

circle-exclamation

The ["mode"](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#name-mode)
 property of an item component with fuel variant must be `"input"` or `"both"` to let the player place fuel items inside the slot.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fuel#id)

ID

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:item_fuel"

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fuel#accepted-items)

Accepted items

Any item that have a burn time (like wood and coal) and match the filter defined in the item component "whitelist" and "blacklist" properties.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fuel#example)

Example

A simple fuel slot :

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:item_fuel",
        "id": "fuel",
        "mode": "input"
    }

[PreviousItem componentchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component)
[NextUpgradechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/upgrade)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [ID](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fuel#id)

# Machine GUI | Custom Machinery 1.21

The Machine GUI is the main tool to interact with the machine in-world. It will be used to display the current status of the machine as well as the different components and their contents.

A machine GUI is not mandatory, if you don't want it just don't put it in the machine json.

A Machine GUI is composed of various GUI Elements, there is no limit of how many elements you can put.

The Machine GUI and it's Elements must be defined as such in the machine json :

Copy

    "gui": [\
        {\
            //Element 1\
        },\
        {\
            //Element 2\
        }\
    ]

circle-info

By default the machine gui has no background, to change that and/or change the size of the gui see the [background element](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element)
 wiki page.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui#gui-elements)

GUI Elements

There are currently 17 available GUI elements :

[Background elementchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element)
[Bar elementchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element)
[Button elementchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element)

[Energy elementchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element)
[Experience elementchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element)
[Fluid elementchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element)
[Fuel elementchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element)

# Machine recipe | Custom Machinery 1.21

Custom machine recipe jsons must be located in `(my_datapack)/data/(namespace)/recipe/` (the same place as the vanilla recipes).

The (namespace) is a folder that can have any name, but must be all lowercase without spaces or special characters.

The machine name must be all lowercase with no spaces or any other characters than letters and numbers but you can use "\_" or "/". The file must be a .json file.

Example : `my_datapack/data/namespace/recipe/my_recipe.json`

Each recipes loaded in the game must have a different ID, in the example above the recipe Id is : namespace:my\_recipe

You can put any number of recipes under the same namespace or separate them.

You can also use subfolders like : `(my_datapack)/data/(namespace)/recipe/machine1/my_recipe.json` so the recipe ID will be `namespace:machine1/my_recipe`

Just remember that all the recipe json should be under the recipes folder.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#recipe-properties)

Recipe properties

The recipe json has 3 mandatory properties and 10 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:custom_machine" //Mandatory for defining a custom machine recipe.

chevron-rightMachine[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#machine)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#name-machine)

Name : `machine`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#description)

Description :

The machine this recipe is for.

You can set only one machine here so if you want the same recipe to work for different machines you must write the recipe for each machine and change this property.

**You must use here the Machine ID and not the machine name.**

If the machine ID is wrong or the machine doesn't exist the recipe will still load but it will be unusable in-game.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#example)

Example :

Copy

    "machine": "namespace:my_machine"

This recipe will be set for the machine with ID "namespace:my\_machine".

Reminder : "namespace:my\_machine" is the machine located in `(datapack)/data/namespace/machines/my_machine.json`

chevron-rightTime[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#time)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#name-time)

Name : `time`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer that define the duration of the recipe **in ticks**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#example-1)

Example :

Copy

    "time": 200

The recipe will takes 10 seconds to be completed since there is 20 ticks in 1 second (if the server doesn't lag).

Note : Increasing the recipe time will increase any per-ticks input costs and outputs.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#optional-properties)

Optional properties

[Requirementschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements)
chevron-rightJei[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#jei)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#name-jei)

Name : `jei`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#description-2)

Description :

An array of Requirements.

The requirements are specified exactly as in the `requirements` property above.

Requirements specified here will not be processed by the machine, they will just display in the jei recipe.

**The requirements specified here will override the requirements specified in the "requirements" property, so if this property is specified only its requirements will show in jei**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#default-empty)

Default : `empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#example-2)

Example :

Define 2 recipe requirements that won't be processed by the recipe, but will be the only 2 shown in the jei recipe gui.

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#description-3)

Description :

An integer between -2147483648 and 2147483647 that define which recipe will be used by the machine if several recipes pass all requirement checks.

The recipe with the highest priority will be used.

If several recipes pass the requirement checks and have the same priority the first loaded recipe will be used, this depends of the datapack order and can be a bit random so if you want to be sure of which recipe will be used first you must use the priority property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#example-3)

Example :

This recipe will be loaded before any recipe with a priority < 1000.

chevron-rightJei priority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#jei-priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#name-jeipriority)

Name : `jeiPriority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#description-4)

Description :

An integer between -2147483648 and 2147483647 that define which recipe will show first in jei, recipes with higher values will show before recipes with lower values.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#default-0-1)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#example-4)

Example :

This recipe will show in jei before any recipes with a priority < 1000.

chevron-rightError[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#error)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#name-error)

Name : `error`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#description-5)

Description :

A boolean that determine whether the recipe will error, or reset the machine when a requirement of the recipe cannot be fulfilled.

Note : When the machine reset its inventory remains the same but all already consumed inputs are lost.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#default-true)

Default : `true`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#example-5)

Example :

The machine will be reset if any requirement error.

chevron-rightHidden[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#hidden)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#name-hidden)

Name : `hidden`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#description-6)

Description :

If true the recipe will be hidden in JEI recipe gui.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#default-false)

Default : `false`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#example-6)

Example :

The recipe will be hidden in JEI :

chevron-rightAppearance[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#appearance)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#name-appearance)

Name : `appearance`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#description-7)

Description :

Allows to set a custom [Machine appearance](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-appearance)
, such as a block model, light, hardness... while this recipe is processing.

All appearance properties specified here will override the default "running" properties specified in the machine json but only while this recipe is processing.

Once the recipe process finish or is stopped the machine appearance will revert to its default values.

This is only available for machine recipes and not craft recipes as their process is instantaneous.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#default)

Default :

No custom appearance specified, fallback to the "running" appearance specified in the machine json.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#example-7)

Example :

The machine will look like a bedrock block and be unbreakable while this recipe is processing :

chevron-rightGui[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#gui)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#name-gui)

Name : `gui`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#description-8)

Description :

Allows to set some recipe specific gui elements, this can be an array or a single element.

Any gui element from CM and its addons can be used here.

When a machine process this recipe, all gui elements defined here will be added to the machine gui.

If a gui element defined here has the same id than another element defined in the machine json then it will replace it.

It is impossible to remove a gui element defined in the machine json, but you can replace it with an [empty gui element](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/empty-element)
 instead.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#default-empty-1)

Default : empty

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#example-8)

Example :

Change the position of a slot gui element with id "input1", and replace the gui element with id "texture" by an empty gui element :

chevron-rightCores[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#cores)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#name-cores)

Name : `cores`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#description-9)

Description :

A list of cores that can run this recipes, in case the machine processor for this machine has more than 1 core.

If this list is empty the recipe will be able to run on any cores of the processor.

Each core is defined by an integer, 1 being the first core and <amount> being the last core.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#default-empty-2)

Default : `empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#example-9)

Example :

The recipe will run only on the first core :

chevron-rightSingle core[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#single-core)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#name-single_core)

Name : `single_core`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#description-10)

Description :

A boolean value (true/false).

If set to true the recipe will run only on one core of the machine processor at a time.

The recipe will still run only on the cores specified using the "cores" property (see above) but only on 1 core at a time.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#default-false-1)

Default : `false`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#example-10)

Example :

Make the recipe run on only 1 core at a time :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/machine-recipe#template)

Template

A default recipe template with all properties specified :

###

Example

A recipe that takes a diamond and turn it into energy :

circle-info

.

            "x": 10,\
            "y": 10,\

        "machine": "custommachinery:my_machine",
        "time": 1000,
        "requirements": [\
        {\
            "type": "custommachinery:item",\
            "mode": "input",\
            "item": "minecraft:diamond",\
            "amount": 1\
        },\
        {\
            "type": "custommachinery:energy",\
            "mode": "output",\
            "amount": 1000\

# Fluid component | Custom Machinery 1.21

This is the component that will let your machine interact with the Forge Fluid system (like tanks, pipes and so).

It is compatible with any other mods that use the same system (so about all of them) so any pipes will be able to pump fluids in and out of the machine.

Basically adding this component to the machine json will add a fluid tank to the machine.

circle-info

You can add as much as you want fluid components to your machine.

Each component will act as a separate fluid tank.

Fluid component is defined with `"type": "custommachinery:fluid"` in the json.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#properties)

Properties

The fluid component has 3 mandatory properties and 9 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:fluid" //Mandatory to define a fluid component.

chevron-rightCapacity[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#capacity)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#name-capacity)

Name : `capacity`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the amount of fluid that can be stored in the tank (Volume in Forge mB, with 1000mB being 1 Bucket of fluid)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#example)

Example :

Copy

    "capacity": 10000 //This component will be able to store 10000mB.

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#desccription)

Desccription :

A string that define the id of the tank (used in the gui element and recipes), the String must be all lowercase with letters and numbers only (no spaces or special characters).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#example-1)

Example :

Copy

    "id": "tank1"

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightMax input[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#max-input)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#name-maxinput)

Name : `maxInput`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer that represent the max mB that can be input in the tank during a single tick.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#default)

Default :

The `capacity` of the tank.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#example-2)

Example :

chevron-rightMin input[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#min-input)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#name-mininput)

Name : `minInput`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#description-2)

Description :

A positive integer that represent the min mB that can be input in the tank during a single tick.

If something (a pipe or the machine's auto-input) try to insert less than the specified amount the transfer will fail and nothing will be inserted.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#default-0)

Default : `0`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#example-3)

Example :

chevron-rightMax output[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#max-output)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#name-maxoutput)

Name : `maxOutput`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#description-3)

Description :

A positive integer that represent the max mB that can be output from the tank during a single tick.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#default-1)

Default :

The `capacity` of the tank.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#example-4)

Example :

chevron-rightMin output[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#min-output)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#name-minoutput)

Name : `minOutput`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#description-4)

Description :

A positive integer that represent the min mB that can be output from the tank during a single tick.

If something (a pipe or the machine's auto-output) try to extract less than the specified amount the transfer will fail and nothing will be extracted.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#default-0-1)

Default : `0`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#example-5)

Example :

chevron-rightWhitelist[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#whitelist)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#name-whitelist)

Name : `whitelist`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#description-5)

Description :

A list of fluids that the tank can accept.

The fluids must be referenced by their registry name like `minecraft:water` or `minecraft:lava`.

By default the blacklist is empty so all fluids are accepted.

You can also use tag here with the # prefix like `#c:water`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#default-2)

Default :

No filter, so all fluids are accepted by the tank.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#example-6)

Example :

chevron-rightBlacklist[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#blacklist)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#name-blacklist)

Name : `blacklist`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#description-6)

Description :

A blacklist of fluids that the tank can't accept.

The fluids must be referenced by their registry name like `minecraft:water` or `minecraft:lava`.

By default the blacklist is empty so all fluids are accepted.

You can also use tag here with the # prefix like `#c:water`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#default-3)

Default :

No filter, so all fluids are accepted by the tank.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#example-7)

Example :

chevron-rightMode[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#mode)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#name-mode)

Name : `mode`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#description-7)

Description :

The IO mode of the tank, used only by recipes to know which tanks are inputs and outputs.

Available modes are (input/output/both/none).

While crafting the machine will search for fluids to consume in input tanks and put the recipe results in the output tanks.

For changing I/O mode of a tank for external interaction, such as buckets and pipes see the [Config](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config)
 property below.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#default-both)

Default : `both`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#example-8)

Example :

[I/O Configchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config)
chevron-rightUnique[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#unique)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#name-unique)

Name : `unique`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#description-8)

Description :

A boolean property (true/false) that define if the fluid component can accept a fluid that is already in another fluid component in the same machine.

If the component is set as "unique" a player won't be able to insert a fluid that is already in another tank, even if that tank is full (basically prevent overfill).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#default-false)

Default : `false`

The fluid component won't care if the fluid is already in another tank.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#example-9)

Example :

The fluid component won't accept fluids that already are in another component.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#example-10)

Example

An example of Fluid Component that can store 10000mB of lava only, send 1000mB/tick and receive 666mB/tick.

    "maxInput": 1000 //The machine can accept 1000mB/tick.

Copy

    "minInput": 1000 //The machine will accept at least 1000mB/tick.

Copy

    "maxOutput": 1000 //The machine can give 1000mB/tick.

Copy

    "minOutput": 1000 //The machine will extract at least 1000mB/tick.

Copy

    "whitelist": "#c:water" //The tank will accept all fluids that are not in the water tag.

Copy

    "unique": true

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:fluid",
        "capacity": 10000,
        "id": "lavatank",
        "maxInput": 666,
        "maxOutput": 1000,
        "filter": ["minecraft:lava"],
        "whitelist": true
    }
