# Custom Block/Item | Custom Machinery 1.21

By default all machines share the same block (id: `custommachinery:custom_machine_block`) and the same item (id: `custommachinery:custom_machine_item`) and are differentiated by their NBT tag (like enchanted books for example).

This can cause issue when some mod can't differentiate blocks/items by NBT (questing mods, guidebook, ponders...).

However you can use [KubeJSarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/kubejs)
 to create a custom block and custom item for the machine.

circle-exclamation

The following script MUST be put on the `startup_scripts` folder and be the same on both the server and the client.

Copy

    //Subscribe to the block registry event.
    //No need to use the item registry event, the item will be created automatically.
    StartupEvents.registry('block', event => {
    	//Syntax : event.create("namespace:block_id", "custommachinery:custom_machine").machine("namespace:machine_id)
    	event.create("kubejs:stone_generator", "custommachinery:custom_machine").machine("custommachinery:stone_generator")
    	
    	//If the block id is the same than the machine id you don't have to use .machine()
    	event.create("custommachinery:power_crusher", "custommachinery:custom_machine")
    	
    	//Add .occlude() to make the machine block full opaque (block light)
    	//This may cause rendering issues
    	event.create("custommachinery:power_crusher", "custommachinery:custom_machine").occlude()
    })

[PreviousKubeJSchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs)
[NextRecipeschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/recipes)

Last updated 5 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Upgrades | Custom Machinery 1.21

Custom Machine upgrades can be made with Crafttweaker.

Create a .zs file in the script folder (ex: custom\_machine\_upgrades.zs) and look at the example below to see all the available methods to create a Custom Machine upgrade with Crafttweaker.

If you're not familiar about custom machine upgrades see [the wiki pagearrow-up-right](https://github.com/Frinn38/Custom-Machinery/wiki/Machine-Upgrade-Items)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/upgrades#creating-custom-machine-upgrade-with-crafttweaker)

Creating custom machine upgrade with Crafttweaker

Copy

    //Create the upgrade builder and give it the item that will act as upgrade and the max amount of this upgrade that can be used in a machine.
    mods.custommachinery.CMUpgradeBuilder.create(Item item)
    //If maxAmount is not specified the default is 64.
    mods.custommachinery.CMUpgradeBuilder.create(Item item, int maxAmount)
    
    //Add a machine or a list of machines that will accept this upgrade, 
    //the machine ID must be "namespace:id" like "custommachinery:my_machine" if the json is located in (my_datapack)/data/custommachinery/machines/my_machine.json
    .machine(String... machineID)
    
    //You can add a custom tooltip to the machine upgrade item.
    .tooltip(String... tooltips)
    //Use component for more formatting options,
    //See https://docs.blamejared.com/1.18/en/vanilla/api/text/Component
    .tooltip(Component... tooltips)
    
    //Add a modifier to this upgrade.
    //See below for modifier syntax.
    .modifier(CMRecipeModifierBuilder modifier)
    
    //Finish (don't forget the semicolon ';')
    .build();

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/upgrades#making-a-modifier)

Making a modifier

See below the various methods used to build a recipe modifier and pass it to the upgrade.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/upgrades#zenscript-syntax)

Zenscript syntax

circle-info

Find all requirement types and targets that can be modified [here](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#list-of-properties-that-can-be-modified)
.

*   If not specified the target will be empty and the chance will be 1.0
    
*   CTRequirementType is specified with: `<requirementtype:namespace:requirement_type_id>` ex: `<requirementtype:custommachinery:item>`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/upgrades#example)

Example

A gold ingot put inside the Power Crusher will double it's energy consumption with a maximum of 1000FE but also half its duration time with a minimum of 100 ticks.

[PreviousStructurechevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/structure)
[NextKubeJSchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs)

*   [Creating custom machine upgrade with Crafttweaker](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/upgrades#creating-custom-machine-upgrade-with-crafttweaker)
    
*   [Making a modifier](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/upgrades#making-a-modifier)
    
*   [Zenscript syntax](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/upgrades#zenscript-syntax)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/upgrades#example)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    //Import the modifier builder class as a constant for convenience.
    import mods.custommachinery.CMRecipeModifierBuilder as Builder;
    
    //Create a modifier that add/multiply a value to any input/output requirement of the specified type.
    //requirement must be specified using brackets : <requirementtype:custommachinery:requirement>
    //Value can be any numerical value.
    //Pick one of the 6 methods below :
    Builder.addInput(requirement, value)
    Builder.mulInput(requirement, value)
    Builder.expInput(requirement, value)
    Builder.addOutput(requirement, value)
    Builder.mulOutput(requirement, value)
    Builder.expOutput(requirement, value)
    
    //All methods below are optional
    
    //Specify a target, in case the requirement have several values that can be modified.
    //Only 1 target can be defined for a modifier, default is none.
    .target(String target)
    
    //Specify a chance for this modifier to be applied.
    //Must be a value between 0 and 1, 0 is never applied and 1 is 100% chance to be applied.
    //Default is 1.
    .chance(double chance)
    
    //Specify the maximum value that can be obtained after applying this modifier.
    //It can be any numerical value.
    //Default is POSITIVE_INFINITY.
    .max(double max)
    
    //Specify the minimum value that can be obtained after applying this modifier.
    //It can be any numerical value.
    //Default is NEGATIVE_INFINITY.
    .min(double max)
    
    //Change the tooltip displayed when holding shift while hovering the upgrade item.
    //Default : a short string that describe the effect of this modifier.
    .tooltip(String tooltip)
    //Use a component for more formating options.
    .tooltip(Component tooltip)

Copy

    import mods.custommachinery.CMRecipeModifierBuilder as Builder;
    
    mods.custommachinery.CMUpgradeBuilder.create(<item:minecraft:gold_ingot>)
    .machine("custommachinery:power_crusher")
    .modifier(Builder.mulInput(<requirementtype:custommachinery:energy>, 2).max(1000))
    .modifier(Builder.mulInput(<requirementtype:custommachinery:speed>, 0.5).min(100))
    .build();

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# Chemical component (Mekanism) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This component requires [Custom Machinery Mekanismarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-mekanism)
 to be installed.

This components is used to make the machine able to hold Mekanism chemicals.

It is compatible with Mekanism pressurized pipes and any other mods that use the same system.

Basically adding this component to the machine json will add a chemical tank to the machine.

circle-info

You can add as much as you want chemical components to your machine.

Each component will act as a separate chemical tank.

circle-info

Starting from 1.21.1 all 4 Mekanism chemicals (gas, infusion, slurry and pigment) are now merged into a single "chemical" type.

Chemical component is defined with `"type": "custommachinery:chemical"` in the json.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#properties)

Properties

The chemical component has 3 mandatory properties and 10 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:chemical" //Mandatory to define a chemical component.

chevron-rightCapacity[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#capacity)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#name-capacity)

Name : `capacity`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the amount of chemical that can be stored in the tank (Volume in Forge mB, with 1000mB being 1 Bucket)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#example)

Example :

Copy

    "capacity": 10000 //This component will be able to store 10000mB.

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#desccription)

Desccription :

A string that define the id of the tank (used in the gui element and recipes), the String must be all lowercase with letters and numbers only (no spaces or special characters).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#example-1)

Example :

Copy

    "id": "tank1"

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#name-whitelist)

Name : `whitelist`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#description-5)

Description :

A list of chemicals that the component can accept.

The chemicals must be referenced by their registry name like `mekanism:steam` or `mekanism:redstone`.

You can also use a tag here using the # prefix like `#mekanism:dirty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#default-empty)

Default : empty

All chemicals are accepted by the component.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#example-6)

Example :

The component will accept only steam gas and chemicals in the mekanism:dirty tag.

Note : The blacklist (see below) takes priority over the whitelist. If a chemical is in both the blacklist and whitelist it won't be accepted by the component.

chevron-rightBlacklist[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#blacklist)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#name-blacklist)

Name : `blacklist`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#description-6)

Description :

A blacklist of chemicals that the component can't accept.

The chemicals must be referenced by their registry name like `mekanism:steam` or `mekanism:redstone`.

You can also use a tag here using the # prefix like `#mekanism:dirty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#default-empty-1)

Default : empty

All chemicals are accepted by the component.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#example-7)

Example :

The slot will accept all chemicals but steam gas and chemicals in the mekanism:dirty tag.

Note : The blacklist takes priority over the whitelist (see above). If a chemical is in both the blacklist and whitelist it won't be accepted by the component.

chevron-rightMode[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#mode)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#name-mode)

Name : `mode`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#description-7)

Description :

The IO mode of the tank, used only by recipes to know which tanks are inputs and outputs.

Available modes are (input/output/both/none).

While crafting the machine will search for chemicals to consume in input tanks and put the recipe results in the output tanks.

For changing I/O mode of a tank for external interaction, such as buckets and pipes see the [Config](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config)
 property below.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#default-both)

Default : `both`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#example-8)

Example :

[I/O Configchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config)
chevron-rightUnique[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#unique)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#name-unique)

Name : `unique`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#description-8)

Description :

A boolean property (true/false) that define if the chemical component can accept a chemical that is already in another chemical component in the same machine.

If the component is set as "unique" a player won't be able to insert a chemical that is already in another tank, even if that tank is full (basically prevent overfill).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#default-false)

Default : `false`

The chemical component won't care if the fluid is already in another tank.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#example-9)

Example :

The chemical component won't accept chemical that already are in another component.

chevron-rightRadiations[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#radiations)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#name-radiations)

Name : `radiations`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#description-9)

Description :

A boolean property (true/false) that define if the chemical component will emit radiations when the machine is broken.

If set to true, radiations will be emitted when the machine is broken only if that chemical component contains a radioactive chemical.

The amount of radiations released depends of the chemical and the amount stored.

It works the same as when a Mekanism tank/pipe/machine is broken while containing radioactive chemicals.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#default-false-1)

Default : `false`

The radioactive chemicals will be voided without releasing radiations.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#example-10)

Example :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism#example-11)

Example

An example of gas chemical component that can store 10000mB of sulfuric acid only, send 1000mB/tick and receive 666mB/tick.

    "maxInput": 1000 //The machine can accept 1000mB/tick.

Copy

    "minInput": 1000 //The machine will accept at least 1000mB/tick.

Copy

    "maxOutput": 1000 //The machine can give 1000mB/tick.

Copy

    "minOutput": 1000 //The machine will extract at least 1000mB/tick.

    "whitelist": ["mekanism:steam", "#mekanism:dirty"]

Copy

Copy

    "unique": true

Copy

    "radiations": true

        "type": "custommachinery:chemical",
        "capacity": 10000,
        "id": "tank1",
        "maxInput": 666,
        "maxOutput": 1000,
        "whitelist": "mekanism:sulfuric_acid"
    }

# Crafting your machine | Custom Machinery 1.21

All the machines share the same item, with Id : `custommachinery:custom_machine_item` the machine the item will be linked to is defined with an item component (new system from Minecraft 1.21 that replace old nbt system).

The component id is `custommachinery:machine` and its value should be the machine id like: `custommachinery:power_crusher` (the namespace should always be included).

Vanilla json recipes, KubeJS have different ways to handle items components so I will put an example of each below.

The recipe will be: ![recipe](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2FFrinn38%2FCustom-Machinery%2Fraw%2F1.16.5%2Fwiki%2Fmachine_recipe.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1458ffb2&sv=2)

Forge json

KubeJS script

recipe.json

Copy

    {
        "type": "minecraft:crafting_shaped",
        "pattern":
        [\
            "xxx",\
            "x x",\
            "xxx"\
        ],
        "key":
        {
            "x":
            {
                "item": "minecraft:diamond"
            }
        },
        "result":
        {
            "id": "custommachinery:custom_machine_item",
            "count": 1,
            "components": {"custommachinery:machine":"custommachinery:power_crusher"}
        }
    }

[PreviousToggle Configchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/toggle-config)
[NextDatapackchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/datapack)

Last updated 1 year ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

script.js

Copy

    ServerEvents.recipes(event => {
        event.shaped('custommachinery:custom_machine_item[custommachinery:machine="custommachinery:tester"]'), [\
            'DDD',\
            'D D',\
            'DDD'\
        ], {
            'D': 'minecraft:diamond'
        })
    })

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Item component | Custom Machinery 1.21

This is the component that let your machine interact with items, basically it add an inventory to your machine.

Each Item Component add 1 slot to the machine inventory and each slot can held 1 stack of item but you can add as many components as you want.

circle-info

You can add as much item component as you want.

Item Component can have different types depending on the desired behaviour.

The type for a default item component is: `"type": "custommachinery:item"`

Here is a list of all available item component types with their dedicated wiki pages :

*   [`custommachinery:item_fluid`](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fluid)
    
*   [`custommachinery:item_energy`](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/energy)
    
*   [`custommachinery:item_upgrade`](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/upgrade)
    
*   [`custommachinery:item_result`](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/result)
    
*   [`custommachinery:item_fuel`](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/fuel)
    
*   [`custommachinery:item_filter`](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/filter)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#properties)

Properties

The item component has 2 mandatory properties and 6 optional properties.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:item" //Mandatory to define an item component.

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#description)

Description :

A string that define the id of the slot (used in gui element and recipes), the string must be all lowercase with letters and numbers only (no spaces or special characters).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#example)

Example :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightCapacity[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#capacity)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#name-capacity)

Name : `capacity`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the maximum number of item that you can put in the slot.

This does not override the item stack size (if you set the slot capacity to 100 items will still stack by 64 or less). This is used to decrease the available stack size, not increase it.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#default-64)

Default : 64

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#example-1)

Example :

chevron-rightWhitelist[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#whitelist)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#name-whitelist)

Name : `whitelist`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#description-2)

Description :

A list of items that the slot can accept.

The items must be referenced by their registry name like `minecraft:diamond` or minecraft:stone.

You can also use a tag here using the # prefix like `#minecraft:logs`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#default-empty)

Default : empty

All items are accepted by the slot.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#example-2)

Example :

The slot will accept only Minecraft diamond and items in the minecraft:logs tag.

Note : The blacklist (see below) takes priority over the whitelist. If an item is in both the blacklist and whitelist it won't be accepted by the slot.

chevron-rightBlacklist[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#blacklist)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#name-blacklist)

Name : `blacklist`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#description-3)

Description :

A blacklist of items that the slot can't accept.

The items must be referenced by their registry name like `minecraft:diamond` or minecraft:stone.

You can also use a tag here using the # prefix like `#minecraft:logs`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#default-empty-1)

Default : empty

All items are accepted by the slot.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#example-3)

Example :

The slot will accept all items but Minecraft diamond and items in the minecraft:logs tag.

Note : The blacklist takes priority over the whitelist (see above). If an item is in both the blacklist and whitelist it won't be accepted by the slot.

chevron-rightMode[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#mode)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#name-mode)

Name : `mode`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#description-4)

Description :

The IO mode of the slot, used only by recipes to know which slots are inputs and outputs.

Available modes are (input/output/both/none).

While crafting the machine will search for items to consume in input slots and put the recipe results in the output slots.

For changing I/O mode of a slot for external interaction, such as hoppers and pipes see the [Config](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config)
 property below.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#default-both)

Default : `both`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#example-4)

Example :

[I/O Configchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config)
chevron-rightLocked[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#locked)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#name-locked)

Name : `locked`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#description-5)

Description :

A boolean value, if true the player won't be able to place and remove items from this slot.

Recipes and hoppers/pipes will still be able to place/remove items from this component (as long as they match the filter, mode and config properties).

The locking of a slot can be changed using KubeJS or Crafttweaker integration.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#default-false)

Default : `false`

The player will be able to place items in the slot.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#example-5)

Example :

The player won't be able to place or remove items from the slot.

# Text component | Custom Machinery 1.21

Text Components are used to display strings to the player, with more formatting options than a default string (color, bold, etc...)

Custom Machinery use these components in various places such as the machine name or tooltips properties.

circle-info

The [Minecraft wikiarrow-up-right](https://minecraft.fandom.com/wiki/Raw_JSON_text_format#Java_Edition)
 have a full documentation of how to make text components using json. Be sure to follow the "Java edition" part.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component#available-properties)

Available properties :

*   `text` (The text to display)
    
*   `bold` (true/false)
    
*   `italic` (true/false)
    
*   `underlined` (true/false)
    
*   `striketrough` (true/false)
    
*   `obfuscated` (true/false)
    
*   `color` ("colorID" or "#RRGGBB" hex format)
    
*   `font` (custom font id, minecraft only provide "minecraft:default")
    
*   `children` Not supported !
    

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component#example)

Example :

Display `Hello !` in red and bold.

Copy

    {
        "text": "Hello !",
        "bold": true,
        "color": "red"
    }

[PreviousRequirement display infochevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/requirement-display-info)

*   [Available properties :](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component#available-properties)
    
*   [Example :](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component#example)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Requirement display info | Custom Machinery 1.21

A requirement display info is a small icon that show up in jei recipe jei to provide the player various information about the recipe.

The display info can use any item, texture or sprite and have a list of tooltips that will be displayed when the player hover it with its mouse cursor.

Example : The [Structure requirement](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/structure)
 add by default a structure block icon with a tooltip indicating the list of required blocks to build the structure.

![](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FZznnGu8KvEhqjN3qmLqp%2Fblobs%2FnNOenj5skmta9ocyfwJa%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fafe363&sv=2)

You can override the default display info of any requirements, or create a new one for requirements that doesn't have a default one.

A custom display info won't override the click behavior of a default display info, like the structure requirement that let you click on the icon to show the structure.

circle-exclamation

Each requirements can have only 1 display info.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/requirement-display-info#tooltip)

Tooltip

A display info can have a list of tooltips specified. If the requirement have a default tooltip it will be overriden.

The tooltip is essentially a list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
. Each component in the list will be a new line in the tooltip.

Copy

    "info": {
        "tooltips": [\
            "Some tooltips",\
            {"text": "Some tooltip in red", "color": "red"}\
        ]
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/requirement-display-info#icon)

Icon

There are 3 ways to define a display info icon : item, texture and sprite (animated texture).

If you don't specify an icon this default green + icon will be used.

![](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FZznnGu8KvEhqjN3qmLqp%2Fblobs%2FGXAOvACIulUqdH9hdb5Z%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4d25a14f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/requirement-display-info#item)

Item

Simply provide the id of the item to show as icon.

Example : Show a diamond as icon

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/requirement-display-info#texture)

Texture

Simply provide the path to the texture file, the texture MUST be in a loaded resourcepack (Openloader or KubeJS work well for that) and the .png extension is necessary.

You can also specify the width/height of the texture (default 10px) and the u/v of the texture (default 0).

Example :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/requirement-display-info#sprite)

Sprite

A sprite is essentialy a texture that is stitched into a Minecraft texture atlas, allowing the use of animated textures.

Simply specify the id of the atlas and the id of the texture.

Example : Use the purple nether portal block

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/requirement-display-info#example)

Example

Add a diamond icon with a tooltip :

![](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FZznnGu8KvEhqjN3qmLqp%2Fblobs%2FcyhZBi1Zm0lVb7Fey6TD%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd6f524c&sv=2)

[PreviousRangechevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/range)
[NextText componentchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)

*   [Tooltip](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/requirement-display-info#tooltip)
    
*   [Icon](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/requirement-display-info#icon)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/requirement-display-info#example)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    "info": {
        "item": "minecraft:diamond"
    }

Copy

    "info": {
        "icon": "custommachinery:textures/gui/creation/create_icon.png"
    }

Copy

    "info": {
        "atlas": "minecraft:textures/atlas/blocks.png",
        "sprite": "minecraft:block/nether_portal"
    }

Copy

    {
        //other requirement properties
        "info": {
            "item": "minecraft:diamond",
            "tooltips": ["This recipe make diamonds"]
        }
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Range | Custom Machinery 1.21

A few recipe requirements such as [Time](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/time)
 or [Position](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/position)
 need a range to function properly.

The range can be an unique number (in that case just specify it) or a range of values starting from negative infinity (**\-2147483648**) to positive infinity (**2147483647**).

Several ranges can also be specified, in that case the tested value must match at least one of the specified range to pass.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/range#syntax)

Syntax :

The range must be specified with the following syntax :

1.  Start with `[` (lower bound included) or `(` (lower bound excluded).\
    \
2.  A number which will be the lower bound of the range, or nothing if you want no lower bound.\
    \
3.  A `,` to separate the lower bound from the upper bound.\
    \
4.  A number which will be the upper bound of the range, or nothing if you want no upper bound.\
    \
5.  End with `]` (upper bound included) or `)` (upper bound excluded).
    
6.  If you want to specify another range
    

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/range#special-cases)

Special cases :

*   Use `""` or `"*"` to make a range that accept any values.
    
*   Use `"1"` to make a range that accept only the number 1.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/range#examples)

Examples :

Some range examples are:

Spec

Description

`"1"`

Accept only 1

`"[1,42)"`\
\
Accept 1 (included) to 42 (not included)\
\
`"[1,42]"`\
\
Accept 1 to 42 (both included)\
\
`"[1,)"`\
\
Accept 1 and higher\
\
`"(,1],[42,)"`\
\
Accept up to 1 (included) and 42 or higher\
\
[PreviousDatapackchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/datapack)\
[NextRequirement display infochevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/requirement-display-info)\
\
*   [Syntax :](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/range#syntax)\
    \
*   [Special cases :](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/range#special-cases)\
    \
*   [Examples :](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/range#examples)\
    \
\
sun-brightdesktopmoon\
\
sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Empty element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The empty gui element does nothing on it's own, it's useless to add it in a machine json.

It's only use is for replacing another gui element when a recipe is processing, that way it is possible to 'remove' a machine gui element by replacing it by an empty element with the same id.

Empty elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:empty"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/empty-element#properties)

Properties

The empty element has 1 mandatory property and 1 optional property :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/empty-element#mandatory-property)

Mandatory property

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:empty" //Mandatory to define an empty element.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/empty-element#optional-property)

Optional property

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/empty-element#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/empty-element#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/empty-element#description)

Description :

The id of the element.

If used in a custom machine recipe, this element will replace another element with the same id.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/empty-element#example)

Example :

The element will replace another element with the id "input".

Copy

    "id": "input"

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/empty-element#example-1)

Example

A simple empty gui element :

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:empty",
        "id": "input"
    }

[PreviousDump elementchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element)
[NextEnergy elementchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/empty-element#example-1)

# Upgrades | Custom Machinery 1.21

Machine upgrades are items that can be used to change the behaviors of a custom machine when inserted in an [upgrade item component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component/upgrade)
.

Upgrade items can change the following behaviours :

*   Recipe requirements (items, fluids, energy... consumption and production)
    
*   Machine components (capacity, max/min inputs/outputs)
    
*   Cores amount of the machine processor.
    

circle-check

You can define any item registered in the game as machine upgrade.

The machine upgrade must be defined in a json file placed in a datapack, such as machines and recipes json.

The path of the machine upgrade json file must be : `[datapack_name]/data/[namespace]/upgrade/my_upgrade.json`

You can use whatever you want as \[datapack_name_\] but \[namespace\] and json file name must be all lowercase without spaces or special characters except `___`

circle-info

Upgrades can also be created using [KubeJS](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#properties)

Properties

The upgrade json has 2 mandatory properties and 5 optional properties.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

chevron-rightItem[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#item)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#name-item)

Name : `item`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#description)

Description :

The item you want to use as upgrade, you can define only one item per upgrade json file (but you can make as many file as you want).

The item can be any vanilla or modded item.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#example)

Example :

Copy

    "item": "minecraft:diamond"

The upgrade will be a vanilla diamond.

chevron-rightMachines[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#machines)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#name-machines)

Name : `machines`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#description-1)

Description :

A list of custom machines where this upgrade is allowed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#example-1)

Example :

This upgrade can be applied to the magic spawner and power crusher machines.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightRequirements[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#requirements)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#name-requirements)

Name : `requirements`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#description-2)

Description :

A list of [recipe modifiers](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers)
. These are used to define how the upgrade will influence the recipe processing.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#example-2)

Example :

This modifier will half the energy input required to process the recipe.

chevron-rightComponents[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#components)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#name-components)

Name : `components`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#description-3)

Description :

A list of [component modifiers](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers)
. These are used to define how the upgrade will influence the recipe processing.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#example-3)

Example :

This modifier will add 1000FE to the machine's energy capacity.

chevron-rightCore[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#core)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#name-core)

Name : `core`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#description-4)

Description :

A single core modifier, used to modify the amount of cores the machine can use to process recipes.

A core modifier has the following properties:

*   `operation` : addition, multiplication or exponential
    
*   `modifier` : The value applied to the operation.
    
*   `max` : The max amount of cores the machine can have after applying the upgrade.
    
    *   Optional (default = 32).
        
    
*   `min` : The min amount of cores the machine can have after applying the upgrade.
    
    *   Optional (default = 1).
        
    
*   `tooltip` : The tooltip displayed on the upgrade item.
    
    *   Optional (A default tooltip will be displayed).
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#example-4)

Example :

This core modifier will add 2 cores to the machine processor.

chevron-rightMax[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#max)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#name-max)

Name : `max`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#description-5)

Description :

A positive integer that define the maximum amount of upgrades of this type that can be applied in a machine at a time.

Each item in a stack count as a separate upgrade.

This does not limit the stack size in the upgrade slot, but upgrades in excess won't be taken in account.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#default-64)

Default : 64

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#example-5)

Example :

Only 4 upgrades can be applied in the machine.

chevron-rightTooltip[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#tooltip)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#name-tooltip)

Name : `tooltip`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#description-6)

Description :

The tooltip that will render when a player hover any machine upgrade item in a gui. This is a [text component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#default)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#example-6)

Example :

The tooltip will be "Speed upgrade MK1" in orange.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades#example-7)

Example

The machine upgrade json below make a vanilla diamond item half the recipe duration in the Custom Machinery Power Crusher included in the test datapack.

The upgrade below will double the machine's energy buffer, and add a second core to the machine.

[NextRecipe modifierschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers)

Last updated 5 months ago

            "operation": "addition",

# Datapack | Custom Machinery 1.21

A datapack is a folder (or Zip archive) containing Json files that will be parsed by Minecraft and mods to configure various gameplay elements (recipes, tags, advancements, worldgen etc...)

This wiki covers only the basics, that you need to make custom machines and recipes, for more detailed information about datapacks see [the vanilla wikiarrow-up-right](https://minecraft.fandom.com/wiki/Data_pack)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/datapack#how-to-make-a-datapack)

How to make a datapack

1.  Create a new folder, name it as you want, there are no restrictions on the name of that folder.
    
2.  Inside that folder create a new folder named `data`
    
3.  Next to the `data` folder create a new text file named exactly `pack.mcmeta` (the .mcmeta is the file extension, be sure that your file isn't named `pack.mcmeta.txt`
    
4.  Open the `pack.mcmeta` file with the text editor of your choice and paste the following :
    

Copy

    {
        "pack": {
            "pack_format": 9,
            "description": "A description for my datapack"
        }
    }

That's it, your folder is now a datapack.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/datapack#how-to-load-your-datapack)

How to load your datapack

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/datapack#the-vanilla-way)

The vanilla way

circle-exclamation

This method won't work if you want to publish your modpack on Curseforge, as it require the world to be generated first.

In vanilla datapacks must be placed in the `datapacks` folder, which can be found in the `world` folder.

*   Singleplayer : `<instance>/saves/<save_name>/datapacks/<datapack_folder>`
    
*   Server : `<instance>/<world_name>/datapacks/<datapack_folder>`
    

circle-info

If you're playing on a server you don't need to install datapacks in your game (they will be ignored anyway).

The datapacks installed on the server are synched automatically when you connect.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/datapack#using-open-loader)

Using Open Loader

1.  Install [Open Loaderarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/open-loader)
     like any other mods.
    
2.  Place your datapack folder here : `<instance>/config/openloader/data/<datapack_folder>`
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/datapack#using-kubejs)

Using KubeJS

If you already have [KubeJSarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/kubejs)
 installed (don't install it only for loading datapacks).

The `<instance>/kubejs/data` folder is already a datapack, any json files here will be loaded as they would be in a datapack.

You don't need any `pack.mcmeta` file.

[PreviousCrafting your machinechevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/crafting-your-machine)
[NextRangechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/range)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [How to make a datapack](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/datapack#how-to-make-a-datapack)
    
*   [How to load your datapack](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/datapack#how-to-load-your-datapack)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Toggle Config | Custom Machinery 1.21

Some components have a `config` property that you can define in the machine json.

Unlike the I/O config, the toggle config only support 2 states per sides : `enabled` and `disabled` .

Supported components :

*   [Heat component (Mekanism)](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism)
    
*   [Pressure component (PNC)](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc)
    

circle-info

This property will define the default toggle mode of the component for each side of the machine, but these toggle modes can be changed later in game by the player if you add a [config element](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element)
 to the machine GUI.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/toggle-config#side-modes)

Side modes

You can configure the toggle mode of a specific component for each sides of the machine.

Available sides are : top, bottom, front, back, right, left

circle-info

The machine `front` side is the side that faced the player when the machine was placed.

You can also use `default` to configure each sides that aren't specified.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/toggle-config#available-i-o-modes)

Available I/O modes :

*   `enabled`
    
*   `disabled`
    

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/toggle-config#disabling-gui-config)

Disabling gui config

By default any player can change the side mode of a component by using the config button (only if a [config gui element](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element)
 is present in the machine GUI).

You can prevent player to config a specific component by adding in the config :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/toggle-config#color)

Color

By default when the config button is clicked, all configurable slots will turn blue. This can be changed using `color` property.

Color property support various formats, pick one of these :

Example of a config gui with a few colored slots.

![](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3380432015-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZznnGu8KvEhqjN3qmLqp%252Fuploads%252FwvOgHCSQTCGWjcpR2Sub%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deaeb4541-3ed6-4417-9bc1-5ae32c75a8e3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c76af38&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/toggle-config#example)

Example :

A component config that has the following properties :

*   Enable the left and right sides.
    
*   Disable all other sides.
    
*   The config can't be modified by the player with the gui config button.
    

All sides are optional.

`default` will act for all sides that are not specified.

If `default` is not specified `enabled` mode will be used.

[PreviousI/O Configchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config)
[NextCrafting your machinechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/crafting-your-machine)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Side modes](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/toggle-config#side-modes)
    
*   [Disabling gui config](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/toggle-config#disabling-gui-config)
    
*   [Color](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/toggle-config#color)
    
*   [Example :](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/toggle-config#example)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    "enabled": false

Copy

    //Full json object, values between 0 and 1
    "color": {
        "alpha": 0.5,
        "red": 1,
        "green": 0,
        "blue": 0
    }
    
    //Array of color, the order is alpha, red, green, blue. Values between 0 and 1
    "color": [0.5, 1, 0, 0]
    
    //ARGB 32bit integer
    "color": 2147418112
    
    //Minecraft color names, only support a few colors listed here : https://minecraft.fandom.com/wiki/Formatting_codes
    "color": "red"

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:heat",
        "config": {
            "default": "disabled",
            "right": "enabled",
            "left": "enabled",
            "enabled": false
        }
    }

# Chunkload | Custom Machinery 1.21

**Use one of these methods to add a** [**Chunkload Requirement**](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chunkload)
 **to the recipe.**

Copy

    .chunkload()
    
    .chunkload(radius)

*   The `radius` param must be an integer between 1 and 32. Default to 1 if not specified.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/chunkload#example)

Example

This recipe will chunkload an area of 3x3 chunks around the machine in exchange of 10FE/t :

Copy

    <recipetype:custommachinery:custom_machine>.create("custommachinery:dynamo", 1)
    .chunkload(2)
    .requireEnergyPerTick(10)
    .build();

[PreviousChemical (Mekanism)chevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/chemical-mekanism)
[NextContraption (Create)chevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/contraption-create)

# Comparator | Custom Machinery 1.21

Some requirements have a `comparator` property, those are used to compare a value checked by the requirement to a value specified by the recipe maker.

Available comparators are :

*   `>>` Strictly greater
    
*   `>=` Greater or equals
    
*   `==` Strictly equals
    
*   `<=` Lesser or equals
    
*   `<<` Strictly lesser
    

[PreviousCore modifierchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades/core-modifier)
[NextI/O Configchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Background element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The background gui element work mostly the same way as the [texture gui element](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element)
.

It is used to display a background texture for the machine gui.

circle-exclamation

By default the machine gui doesn't have a background texture, meaning that the gui will be transparent if no background element are specified.

It can also be used to change the size of the gui.

The default machine gui size is 256x192px and the maximum size is 3840x2160px.

If a texture is specified the width/height of the gui will use the width/height of that texture (unless these properties are specified in the background element).

Background elements are defined in json with `"type": "custommachinery:background"`.

circle-exclamation

You can only define 1 background element for a machine gui, if more than 1 background elements are added only the first will be used and the other ignored.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#properties)

Properties

The background element has 1 mandatory property and 3 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#mandatory-property)

Mandatory property

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:background" //Mandatory to define a background element.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightTexture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#name-texture)

Name : `texture`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#description)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#default)

Default :

Copy

    "texture": "custommachinery:textures/gui/base_background.png"

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#example)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_background_texture.png` will be used for the slot element.

Copy

    "texture": "namespace:textures/my_background_texture.png"

chevron-rightWidth[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#width)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#name-width)

Name : `width`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer that define the width of the machine gui.

Maximum allowed value : 3840

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#default-256)

Default : `256`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#example-1)

Example :

chevron-rightHeight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#height)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#name-height)

Name : `height`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#description-2)

Description :

A positive integer that define the height of the machine gui.

Maximum allowed value : 2160

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#default-192)

Default : `192`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#example-2)

Example :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/background-element#example-3)

# Component modifier | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-info

Find all component types and targets that can be modified [here](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#list-of-properties-that-can-be-modified)
.

Copy

    //Create a modifier that add/multiply a value to any machine component.
    //component must be specified using its id: "namespace:component"
    //Value can be any numerical value.
    //Id can be empty "" if the component doesn't have an id (like energy).
    //Pick one of the 3 methods below :
    CMComponentModifierBuilder.add(component, id, value)
    CMComponentModifierBuilder.mul(component, id, value)
    CMComponentModifierBuilder.exp(component, id, value)
    
    //Specifying a target is mandatory
    .target(String target)
    
    //All methods below are optional
    
    //Specify the maximum value that can be obtained after applying this modifier.
    //It can be any numerical value.
    //Default is POSITIVE_INFINITY.
    .max(double max)
    
    //Specify the minimum value that can be obtained after applying this modifier.
    //It can be any numerical value.
    //Default is NEGATIVE_INFINITY.
    .min(double max)
    
    //Change the tooltip displayed when holding shift while hovering the upgrade item.
    //Default : a short string that describe the effect of this modifier.
    .tooltip(String tooltip)
    //Use Text.of("text here") for more formating options.
    //See https://kubejs.com/wiki/kubejs/Text/
    .tooltip(Text tooltip)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades/component-modifier#example)

Example

A modifier that double the machine energy capacity

A modifier that add 50mB max input to the fluid component with id "input1"

[PreviousRecipe modifierchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades/recipe-modifier)
[NextCore modifierchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades/core-modifier)

Last updated 5 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    CMComponentModifierBuilder.mul("custommachinery:energy", "", 2)
    .target("capacity")

Copy

    CMComponentModifierBuilder.add("custommachinery:fluid", "input1", 50)
    .target("max_input")

sun-brightdesktopmoon

 to be installed.

 **to the recipe.**

     `tank` property.

# Function | Custom Machinery 1.21

**Use one of these methods to add a function that must be processed by the machine to continue the recipe.**

Note: This has nothing to do with MC functions (or commands), this requirement allow you to make your own code in ZenScript and pass it to be executed by the machine.

Copy

    //These imports are needed, put these 2 lines on top of the script.
    import mods.custommachinery.Context;
    import mods.custommachinery.Machine;
    
    //Executed when the machine is idle and search a recipe to process.
    //Returning success will allow the machine to process this recipe (if all other requirements allow it as well).
    //Returning error will prevent the machine to process this recipe (the machine will keep searching for another valid recipe).
    .requireFunctionToStart((ctx as Context) => {return ctx.success()})
    
    //Executed the first tick of the crafting process.
    //Returning success will allow the machine to continue to process this recipe.
    //Returning error will put the machine in error status and display the provided error message.
    .requireFunctionOnStart((ctx as Context) => {return ctx.success()})
    
    //Executed each tick of the crafting process.
    //Returning success will allow the machine to continue to process this recipe.
    //Returning error will put the machine in error status and display the provided error message.
    .requireFunctionEachTick((ctx as Context) => {return ctx.success()})
    
    //Executed the last tick of the crafting process.
    //Returning success will allow the machine to continue to process this recipe.
    //Returning error will put the machine in error status and display the provided error message.
    .requireFunctionOnEnd((ctx as Context) => {return ctx.success()})

*   The passed function MUST return a Result.
    
*   Valid results are : `ctx.success()` and `ctx.error("Error message")`
    
*   Context has various methods for interacting with the machine, see [it's wiki page](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context)
    
*   The function can be delayed, put `.delay(delay)` directly after any `.requireFunctionXXX()` call to make the function be executed at the specified delay.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function#example)

Example

[PreviousExperiencechevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/experience)
[NextContextchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    import mods.custommachinery.Context;
    import mods.custommachinery.Machine;
    
    mods.custommachinery.CMRecipeBuilder.create("custommachinery:power_crusher", 100)
    	.requireFunctionOnEnd((ctx as Context) => {
    		var machine = ctx.machine as Machine;
    		var output = machine.addItemToSlot("output1", <item:minecraft:diamond>, false);
    		if(!output.empty)
    			return ctx.error("Couldn't put a diamond in output slot.");
    		else
    		    return ctx.success();
    	})
    	.build();

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Core modifier | Custom Machinery 1.21

A core modifier can be used to modify the amount of cores a machine can use for processing recipe.

Each core can process a single recipe at a time, but not necessarily the same recipe as the other cores.

circle-exclamation

This only works for machines using a [machine processor](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/processor/machine)
 (all machines by default).

Copy

    //Create a modifier that add/multiply the machine processor core amount
    //Value can be any numerical value.
    //Pick one of the 3 methods below :
    CMCoreModifierBuilder.add(value)
    CMCoreModifierBuilder.mul(value)
    CMCoreModifierBuilder.exp(value)
    
    //All methods below are optional
    
    //Specify the maximum value that can be obtained after applying this modifier.
    //It can be any numerical value.
    //Default is POSITIVE_INFINITY.
    .max(double max)
    
    //Specify the minimum value that can be obtained after applying this modifier.
    //It can be any numerical value.
    //Default is NEGATIVE_INFINITY.
    .min(double max)
    
    //Change the tooltip displayed when holding shift while hovering the upgrade item.
    //Default : a short string that describe the effect of this modifier.
    .tooltip(String tooltip)
    //Use Text.of("text here") for more formating options.
    //See https://kubejs.com/wiki/kubejs/Text/
    .tooltip(Text tooltip)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades/core-modifier#example)

Example

A modifier that double the machine core amount

A modifier that add 1 core to the machine

[PreviousComponent modifierchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades/component-modifier)
[NextComparatorchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/comparator)

Last updated 5 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    CMCoreModifierBuilder.mul(2)

Copy

    CMCoreModifierBuilder.add(1)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Contraption (Create) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

 to be installed.

 **to the recipe.**

Copy

    .requireSU(speed)
    .requireSU(speed, stressImpact)
    
    .requireScalingSU(speed)
    .requireScalingSU(speed, stressImpact)
    
    .produceSU(speed)
    .produceSU(speed, stressCapacity)

*   The `speed`, `stressImpact` and `stressCapacity` params must be a positive decimal value.
    
*   The `scaling` methods will make the recipe processing speed scale with the speed provided to the machine.

    <recipetype:custommachinery:custom_machine>.create("custommachinery:boiler", 20)
    .requireSU(64, 2)
    .build();

# Heat (Mekanism) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This requirement requires [Custom Machinery Mekanismarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-mekanism)
 to be installed.

**Use one of these methods to add a** [**heat requirement**](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/heat-mekanism)
 **or** [**temperature requirement**](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/temperature-mekanism)
 **to the recipe.**

Copy

    .requireHeat(amount)
    .requireHeatPerTick(amount)
    
    .produceHeat(amount)
    .produceHeatPerTick(amount)
    
    .requireTemp("range", "unit")
    .requireTempKelvin("range")
    .requireTempCelsius("range")
    .requireTempFahrenheit("range")
    .requireTempRankine("range")
    .requireTempAmbient("range")

*   The `amount` param must be a positive integer.
    
*   The `range` param must be a valid [Range](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/range)
    .
    
*   The `"unit"` param must be a valid temperature unit, valid values are : `kelvin`, `celsius`, `fahrenheit`, `rankine` and `ambient`. It is recommended to use the specific methods for each unit thought.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/heat-mekanism#example)

Example

The following recipe will run only if the machine temperature is above 100°C and will produce 1000 heat.

[PreviousMachinechevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine)
[NextItem filterchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/item-filter)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    <recipetype:custommachinery:custom_machine>.create("custommachinery:boiler", 20)
    .requireTempCelsius("(100,)")
    .produceHeat(1000)
    .build();

# Structure | Custom Machinery 1.21

**Use one of these methods to add a** [**Structure Requirement**](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/structure)
 **to the recipe.**

Copy

    //Only requires the structure
    .requireStructure(String[][] pattern, Map<char, String> keys)
    
    //Destroys the structure (DON'T drop the blocks)
    .destroyStructure(String[][] pattern, Map<char, String> keys)
    
    //Break the structure (drops the blocks)
    .breakStructure(String[][] pattern, Map<char, String> keys)
    
    //Place the structure (drops the replaced blocks)
    .placeStructure(String[][] pattern, Map<char, String> keys, true)
    
    //Place the structure (DON'T drop the replaced blocks)
    .placeStructure(String[][] pattern, Map<char, String> keys, false)

*   The `pattern` param must be an array of array of strings. See `pattern` property of structure requirement. Example: `[["aaa", "aaa", "aaa"], ["aaa", "ama", "aaa"], ["aaa", "aaa", "aaa"]]` Define a 3x3x3 box around the machine `m`
    
*   The `keys` param must be a map of string -> string. See `keys` property of structure requirement. The keys of the map must be single characters (except `m` which is reserved for the machine) and the values must be a block ID with the format: `namespace:block_id[state1=value,state2=value]` (states are optional). Example: `{"a": "minecraft:stone", "b": "minecraft:diamond_block"}`
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/structure#example)

Example

Copy

    .requireStructure([[\
        "aaa",\
        "a a",\
        "aaa",\
        " m "\
    ]], {"a": "minecraft:stone"})

A 3x1x3 hollow ring of stone behind the machine.

[PreviousSkychevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/sky)
[NextUpgradeschevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/upgrades)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Upgrades | Custom Machinery 1.21

Custom Machine upgrades can be made with KubeJS script.

Create a .js file in the `kubejs\server_scripts` folder (ex: custom\_machine\_upgrades.js) and look at the example below to see all the available methods to create a Custom Machine upgrade with KubeJS.

If you're not familiar about custom machine upgrades see [the wiki page](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades)
.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades#creating-custom-machine-upgrade-with-kubejs)

Creating custom machine upgrade with KubeJS

Copy

    //Use the 'cm_upgrades' event to register custom machine upgrades.
    CustomMachineryEvents.upgrades(event => {
    
        //Create the upgrade builder and give it the item that will act as upgrade.
        //Use Item.of("item_id") to create the item.
        event.create(Item item)
        //If maxAmount is not specified the default is 64.
        event.create(Item item, int maxAmount)
        
        //Add a machine or a list of machines that will accept this upgrade, 
        //the machine ID must be "namespace:id" like "custommachinery:my_machine",
        //if the json is located in (my_datapack)/data/custommachinery/machines/my_machine.json
        .machine(String... machineID)
        
        //You can add a custom tooltip to the machine upgrade item.
        .tooltip(String... tooltips)
        //Use Text.of("text here") for more formatting options,
        //See https://kubejs.com/wiki/kubejs/Text/
        .tooltip(Text... tooltips)
        
        //Add a recipe modifier to this upgrade.
        .requirement(CMRecipeModifierBuilder modifier)
        
        //Add a component modifier to this upgrade.
        .component(CMRecipeModifierBuilder modifier)
        
        //Add a core modifier to this upgrade.
        .core(CMCoreModifierBuilder modifier)
    })

[Recipe modifierchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades/recipe-modifier)
[Component modifierchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades/component-modifier)
[Core modifierchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades/core-modifier)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades#examples)

Examples

A gold ingot put inside the Power Crusher will double it's energy consumption with a maximum of 1000FE but also half it's duration time with a minimum of 100 ticks.

[PreviousWorking corechevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/recipes/working-core)
[NextRecipe modifierchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades/recipe-modifier)

Last updated 5 months ago

*   [Creating custom machine upgrade with KubeJS](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades#creating-custom-machine-upgrade-with-kubejs)
    
*   [Examples](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades#examples)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    CustomMachineryEvents.upgrades(event => {
        event.create(Item.of('minecraft:gold_ingot'))
            .machine("custommachinery:power_crusher")
            .modifier(CMRecipeModifierBuilder.mulInput('custommachinery:energy', 2).max(1000))
            .modifier(CMRecipeModifierBuilder.mulInput('custommachinery:speed', 1.5).min(100))
    })
