# Recipe modifier | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-info

Find all requirement types and targets that can be modified [here](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#list-of-properties-that-can-be-modified)
.

triangle-exclamation

When multiplying values between 0 and 1 you will almost always prefer to use 'exp' instead of 'mul'

Copy

    //Create a modifier that add/multiply a value to any input/output requirement of the specified type.
    //requirement must be specified using its id: "namespace:requirement"
    //Value can be any numerical value.
    //Pick one of the 6 methods below :
    CMRecipeModifierBuilder.addInput(requirement, value)
    CMRecipeModifierBuilder.mulInput(requirement, value)
    CMRecipeModifierBuilder.expInput(requirement, value)
    CMRecipeModifierBuilder.addOutput(requirement, value)
    CMRecipeModifierBuilder.mulOutput(requirement, value)
    CMRecipeModifierBuilder.expOutput(requirement, value)
    
    //All methods below are optional
    
    //Specify a target, in case the requirement have several values that can be modified.
    //Only 1 target can be defined for a modifier, default is none.
    .target(String target)
    
    //Specify a chance for this modifier to be applied.
    //Must be a value between 0 and 1, 0 is never applied and 1 is 100% chance to be applied.
    //Default is 1.
    .chance(double chance)
    
    //Specify the maximum value that can be obtained after applying this modifier.
    //It can be any numerical value.
    //Default is POSITIVE_INFINITY.
    .max(double max)
    
    //Specify the minimum value that can be obtained after applying this modifier.
    //It can be any numerical value.
    //Default is NEGATIVE_INFINITY.
    .min(double max)
    
    //Change the tooltip displayed when holding shift while hovering the upgrade item.
    //Default : a short string that describe the effect of this modifier.
    .tooltip(String tooltip)
    //Use Text.of("text here") for more formating options.
    //See https://kubejs.com/wiki/kubejs/Text/
    .tooltip(Text tooltip)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades/recipe-modifier#example)

Example

A modifier that double the per-tick energy input

A modifier that half the processing time

[PreviousUpgradeschevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades)
[NextComponent modifierchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/upgrades/component-modifier)

Last updated 5 months ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    CMRecipeModifierBuilder.mulInput("custommachinery:energy_per_tick", 2)

Copy

    CMRecipeModifierBuilder.expInput("custommachinery:speed", 0.5)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# I/O Config | Custom Machinery 1.21

Some components have a `config` property that you can define in the machine json.

This property can be used to define the default Input/Output (I/O) sides for the component.

Supported components :

*   [Energy component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component)
    
*   [Fluid component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component)
    
*   [Item component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component)
    
*   [Chemical component (Mekanism)](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism)
    
*   [Contraption component (Create)](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/contraption-component-create)
    

circle-info

This property will define the default I/O mode of the component for each side of the machine, but these I/O modes can be changed later in game by the player if you add a [config element](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element)
 to the machine GUI.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config#side-modes)

Side modes

You can configure the I/O mode of a specific component for each sides of the machine.

Available sides are : top, bottom, front, back, right, left

circle-info

The machine `front` side is the side that faced the player when the machine was placed.

You can also use `default` to configure each sides that aren't specified.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config#available-i-o-modes)

Available I/O modes :

*   `input` : only input
    
*   `output` : only output
    
*   `both` : input and output
    
*   `none` : neither input nor output
    

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config#auto-input-output)

Auto input/output

Starting from CM 0.7.0 the machines now have the ability to auto input/output items, fluids and energy from/to blocks next to the machine.

By default this behavior is disabled for items and fluids.

For energy components the default behavior is to auto input from all sides.

To enable or disable auto I/O simply use :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config#disabling-gui-config)

Disabling gui config

By default any player can change the side mode of a component, or activate auto I/O by using the config button (only if a [config gui element](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element)
 is present in the machine GUI).

You can prevent player to config a specific component by adding in the config :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config#color)

Color

By default when the config button is clicked, all configurable slots will turn blue. This can be changed using `color` property.

Color property support various formats, pick one of these :

Example of a config gui with a few colored slots.

![](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3380432015-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FZznnGu8KvEhqjN3qmLqp%252Fuploads%252FwvOgHCSQTCGWjcpR2Sub%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deaeb4541-3ed6-4417-9bc1-5ae32c75a8e3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c76af38&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config#example)

Example :

A component config that has the following properties :

*   Allow input from the left side.
    
*   Allow output to the right side.
    
*   All other sides (top, bottom, front and back) can't input or output.
    
*   Auto input and output are enabled.
    
*   The config can't be modified by the player with the gui config button.
    

All sides are optional.

`default` will act for all sides that are not specified.

If `default` is not specified `both` mode will be used.

[PreviousComparatorchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/comparator)
[NextToggle Configchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/toggle-config)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Side modes](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config#side-modes)
    
*   [Auto input/output](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config#auto-input-output)
    
*   [Disabling gui config](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config#disabling-gui-config)
    
*   [Color](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config#color)
    
*   [Example :](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/i-o-config#example)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    "config": {
        "input": true, //Enable auto-input
        "output": false, //Disable auto-output
    }

Copy

    "enabled": false

Copy

    //Full json object, values between 0 and 1
    "color": {
        "alpha": 0.5,
        "red": 1,
        "green": 0,
        "blue": 0
    }
    
    //Array of color, the order is alpha, red, green, blue. Values between 0 and 1
    "color": [0.5, 1, 0, 0]
    
    //ARGB 32bit integer
    "color": 2147418112
    
    //Minecraft color names, only support a few colors listed here : https://minecraft.fandom.com/wiki/Formatting_codes
    "color": "red"

Copy

    {
        "type": "item",
        "mode": "input",
        "id": "slot1",
        "config": {
            "default": "none",
            "right": "output",
            "left": "input",
            "input": true,
            "output": true,
            "enabled": false
        }
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Config element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The config gui element is used to add an I/O side config button on the Machine GUI.

Config elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:config"`.

circle-info

If you don't add this element the players won't be able to configurate I/O of the machine, that can be useful if you want to make a machine with defined I/O sides.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#properties)

Properties

The config element has 3 mandatory properties and 7 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:config" //Mandatory to define a config element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "y": 100

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightTexture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#name-texture)

Name : `texture`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#description-2)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#default)

Default :

Copy

    "texture": "custommachinery:textures/gui/base_config.png"

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#example-2)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

Copy

    "texture": "namespace:textures/my_texture.png"

chevron-rightTexture hovered[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#texture-hovered)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#name-texture_hovered)

Name : `texture_hovered`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#description-3)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI, only when the element is hovered by the player mouse cursor.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#default-1)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#example-3)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

chevron-rightWidth[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#width)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#name-width)

Name : `width`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#description-4)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the width of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#default-2)

Default :

The same width as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#example-4)

Example :

The width of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightHeight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#height)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#name-height)

Name : `height`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#description-5)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the height of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#default-3)

Default :

The same height as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#example-5)

Example :

The height of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#description-6)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#example-6)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#description-7)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#example-7)

Example :

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#description-8)

Description :

The id of this gui element. By default it does nothing and can be omitted.

This is really only useful if you intend to make a recipe that replace this element.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#default-empty)

Default : `empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#example-8)

Example :

The id of this element will be `config`

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/config-element#example-9)

# Context | Custom Machinery 1.21

Context is the object provided in the function requirement using the Crafttweaker integration.

It contains various methods for interacting with the machine.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#methods)

Methods

chevron-rightSet the result of the function[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#set-the-result-of-the-function)

Every function **MUST** return a result, which is either a success or an error.

Copy

    //Get a success result
    ctx.success();
    
    //Get an error result
    ctx.error("Some error message");

chevron-rightGet the remaining crafting time[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#get-the-remaining-crafting-time)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#name-remainingtime)

Name : `remainingTime`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#description)

Description :

Return a decimal value that represent the time in ticks before the end of the current recipe process. This value does not take into account any speed modifiers applied to the machine.

Note : This method won't work when used inside `requireFunctionToStart`, the other 3 function requirements are fine to use.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#example)

Example

Copy

    .requireFunctionEachTick((ctx as Context) => {
    		var time = ctx.remainingTime;
                    //Use time here
    	})

chevron-rightGet the crafting process base speed[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#get-the-crafting-process-base-speed)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#name-basespeed)

Name : `baseSpeed`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#description-1)

Description :

Return a decimal value that represent the base speed (before upgrades are applied) of the crafting process.

By default it returns 1

Note : This method won't work when used inside `requireFunctionToStart`, the other 3 function requirements are fine to use.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#example-1)

Example

Copy

    .requireFunctionEachTick((ctx as Context) => {
    		var baseSpeed = ctx.baseSpeed;
                    //Use baseSpeed here
    	})

chevron-rightSet the crafting process base speed[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#set-the-crafting-process-base-speed)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#name-basespeed-1)

Name : `baseSpeed`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#description-2)

Description :

Set a decimal value as the base speed (before upgrades are applied) of the crafting process.

The new speed must not be negative.

Note : This method won't work when used inside `requireFunctionToStart`, the other 3 function requirements are fine to use.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#example-2)

Example :

Copy

    .requireFunctionOnStart((ctx as Context) => {
    		ctx.baseSpeed = 2;
    	})

chevron-rightGet the crafting process modified speed[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#get-the-crafting-process-modified-speed)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#name-modifiedspeed)

Name : `modifiedSpeed`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#description-3)

Description :

Return a decimal value that represent the modified speed (after upgrades are applied) of the crafting process.

Note : This method won't work when used inside `requireFunctionToStart`, the other 3 function requirements are fine to use.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#example-3)

Example

chevron-rightGet the machine as a tile entity[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#get-the-machine-as-a-tile-entity)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#name-tile)

Name : `tile`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#description-4)

Description :

Return a [BlockEntityarrow-up-right](https://docs.blamejared.com/1.18/en/vanilla/api/block/entity/BlockEntity)
, you can use it to get various information about the machine, see the linked CT wiki page.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#example-4)

Example

chevron-rightGet the machine as a custom machine[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#get-the-machine-as-a-custom-machine)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#name-machine)

Name : `machine`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#description-5)

Description :

Return a [Machine](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine)
, you can use it to check, input and output energy, fluids and items from/to the machine.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context#example-5)

Example

[PreviousFunctionchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function)
[NextMachinechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    .requireFunctionEachTick((ctx as Context) => {
    		var modifiedSpeed = ctx.modifiedSpeed;
                    //Use modifiedSpeed here
    	})

Copy

    .requireFunctionEachTick((ctx as Context) => {
    		var tile = ctx.tile;
                    //Use tile here
    	})

Copy

    .requireFunctionEachTick((ctx as Context) => {
    		var machine = ctx.machine;
                    //Use machine here
    	})

# Dump element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The dump element is a button used to void the content of one or several fluid tanks.

When clicked, the dump button will find the specified fluid component in the machine and void it's content.

Dump elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:dump"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#properties)

Properties

The dump gui element has 4 mandatory properties and 8 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:dump" //Mandatory to define a dump element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "y": 100

chevron-rightTanks[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#tanks)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#name-tanks)

Name : `tanks`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#description-2)

Description :

The id of the [Fluid Component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#mandatory-properties)
 you want to void. It must be the exact same id specified in the fluid component json `id` property. You can specify a list of tank id \`\["tank1", "tank2"...\] in which case all specified tanks will be voided when the dump element is clicked.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#example-2)

Example :

The element will void the fluid component with id `tank1`, if no fluid component has this id it will do nothing.

Copy

    "tanks": "tank1"

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightWidth[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#width)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#name-width)

Name : `width`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#description-3)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the width of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#default)

Default :

The same width as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#example-3)

Example :

The width of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightHeight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#height)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#name-height)

Name : `height`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#description-4)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the height of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#default-1)

Default :

The same height as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#example-4)

Example :

The height of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#description-5)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#example-5)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

chevron-rightTexture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#name-texture)

Name : `texture`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#description-6)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#default-2)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#example-6)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used for the dump element.

chevron-rightTexture hovered[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#texture-hovered)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#name-texture_hovered)

Name : `texture_hovered`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#description-7)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI when the players mouse cursor is hovering the element.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#default-3)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#example-7)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

chevron-rightComponent[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#component)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#name-component)

Name : `component`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#description-8)

Description :

The type of component to dump contents.

Must be specified as a machine component type id e.g: `"custommachinery:item"`

This can be a list if you need to dump the content of multiple component types : `["custommachinery:item", "custommachinery:fluid"]`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#default-custommachinery-fluid)

Default : `"custommachinery:fluid"`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#example-8)

Example :

This will make the dump gui element void content from item slots only.

chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#description-9)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#example-9)

Example :

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#description-10)

Description :

The id of this gui element. By default it does nothing and can be omitted.

This is really only useful if you intend to make a recipe that replace this element.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#default-empty)

Default : `empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#example-10)

Example :

The id of this element will be `dump`

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/dump-element#example-11)

# Component modifiers | Custom Machinery 1.21

Component modifiers are used to tweak some properties of a machine component.

They are defined in json inside of the `components` property of the machine upgrade item json.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#list-of-properties-that-can-be-modified)

List of properties that can be modified

Component

Needs id

Target

Modified property

[Chunkload](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component)

No

"radius"

`radius`

[Energy](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component)

No

"capacity"

`capacity`

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#properties)

Properties

The component modifier has 4 mandatory properties and 4 optional property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

chevron-rightComponent[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#component)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#name-component)

Name : `component`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#description)

Description :

The type of the componentyou want to apply the modifier to. This is the same type as the one you specify in the `type` property when defining the component in the machine json.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#example)

Example :

This modifier will be applied to the energy component.

chevron-rightTarget[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#target)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#name-target)

Name : `target`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#description-1)

Description :

The `target` property can be used to define which one of the component property you want to modify.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#example-1)

Example :

Modify the capacity property of the component :

chevron-rightOperation[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#operation)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#name-operation)

Name : `operation`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#description-2)

Description :

The mathematical operation that will be applied to the targeted component property by the modifier. The available operations are :

*   `addition` : The resulting value will be the sum of the base component value and the modifier value multiplied by the amount of upgrades. `final_value = base_value + upgrade_modifier * upgrade_amount`
    

*   `multiplication` : The resulting value will be the multiplication of the base component value and the modifier value multiplied by the amount of upgrades. `final_value = base_value * upgrade_modifier * upgrade_amount`
    

*   exponential : The resulting value will be the multiplication of the base component value and the modifier value powered to the amount of upgrades. `final_value = base_value * upgrade_modifier ^ upgrade_amount`
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#example-2)

Example :

The base component value (defined in the machine json) will be multiplicated by the value defined in this modifier.

chevron-rightModifier[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#modifier)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#name-modifier)

Name : `modifier`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#description-3)

Description :

The value (double) to add or multiply to the base component value. It can be positive or negative and support decimal numbers.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#example-3)

Example :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#description-4)

Description :

Some components (fluids and items in CM, more in addons) have an id property that must be specified in the modifier so it know which specific component to modify.

If a component is single (energy, experience, chunkload in CM) the id can be omitted.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#default-empty)

Default : `empty`

The modifier will be applied to the single component of the specified type.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#example-4)

Example :

The modifier will be applied to a component with id "input1" :

chevron-rightMax[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#max)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#name-max)

Name : `max`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#description-5)

Description :

A positive integer that define the maximum value obtained after applying this upgrade.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#default-positive_infinity)

Default : `POSITIVE_INFINITY`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#example-5)

Example :

Whatever the modifier does, the resulting value won't be greater than 42.

chevron-rightMin[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#min)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#name-min)

Name : `min`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#description-6)

Description :

A positive integer that define the minimum value obtained after applying this upgrade.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#default-negative_infinity)

Default : `NEGATIVE_INFINITY`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#example-6)

Example :

Whatever the modifier does, the resulting value won't be lower than 42.

chevron-rightTooltip[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#tooltip)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#name-tooltip)

Name : `tooltip`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#description-7)

Description :

The tooltip that will render when a player hover any machine upgrade item in a gui while holding shift. This is a [text component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#default)

Default :

A short string that describe what the modifier does like : `-50% Energy capacity`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/component-modifiers#example-7)

Example :

# Chemical element (Mekanism) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This element requires [Custom Machinery Mekanismarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-mekanism)
 to be installed.

The chemical elements are used to display the content of a chemical component in the Machine GUI.

A chemical element must be associated with a [chemical component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism)
 using the id property. It will display the fluid stored in the component on the machine GUI.

If the element cannot find the component (usually because of an error in the id) the element will still be rendered but it will always be empty.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#all-of-mekanism-chemicals-types-are-supported)

All of Mekanism chemicals types are supported :

*   Gas
    
*   Infusion
    
*   Pigment
    
*   Slurry
    

Chemical elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:chemical"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#properties)

Properties

The chemical element has 4 mandatory properties and 7 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:chemical" //Mandatory to define a chemical element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#description-2)

Description :

The id of the [Chemical Component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chemical-component-mekanism)
 you want to link to this element. It must be the exact same id specified in the chemical component json `id` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#example-2)

Example :

The element will display the chemical component with id `tank1`, if no chemical component has this id it will do nothing.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightWidth[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#width)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#name-width)

Name : `width`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#description-3)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the width of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#default)

Default :

The same width as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#example-3)

Example :

The width of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightHeight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#height)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#name-height)

Name : `height`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#description-4)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the height of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#default-1)

Default :

The same height as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#example-4)

Example :

The height of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#description-5)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#example-5)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

chevron-rightTexture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#name-texture)

Name : `texture`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#description-6)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#default-2)

Default :

The default fluid element texture :

`custommachinery:textures/gui/base_fluid_storage.png`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#example-6)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_tank_texture.png` will be used for the fluid element.

chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#description-7)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#example-7)

Example :

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

chevron-rightOrientation[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#orientation)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#name-orientation)

Name : `orientation`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#description-8)

Description :

The direction the bar will be filled to.

Valid values are : `top`, `right`, `bottom` and `left`.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#default-top)

Default : `top`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#example-8)

Example :

The bar will fill towards the right for the machine gui.

chevron-rightHighlight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#highlight)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#name-highlight)

Name : `highlight`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#description-9)

Description :

A boolean property, if true the element will highlight (become slightly brighter) when the player mouse hover it. If false the element will not highlight on mouse hover.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#default-true)

Default : true

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/chemical-element-mekanism#example-9)

# Bar element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The bar gui element can be used to display a number in the form of a fillable bar (the default texture is the same one as the energy gui element).

The number value must be stored in the machine data, which is accessible only by using Crafttweaker or KubeJS scripts.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#example-setting-a-number-in-the-data-from-a-script)

Example: setting a number in the data from a script

KubeJS

Crafttweaker

Copy

    .requireFunctionEachTicks(ctx => {
        //Set the variable named "amount" to 10
        //"amount" can be replaced by anything else,
        //as long as it match the ID specified in the bar gui element properties.
        ctx.machine.data.amount = 10;
        
        return ctx.success()
    })

Copy

    .requireFunctionEachTicks((ctx as Context) => {
        //Set the variable named "amount" to 10
        //"amount" can be replaced by anything else,
        //as long as it match the ID specified in the bar gui element properties.
        ctx.machine.data.amount = 10;
        
        return ctx.success();
    });

Bar elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:bar"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#properties)

Properties

The bar gui element has 4 mandatory properties and 10 optional properties.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:bar" //Mandatory to define a bar element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#description-2)

Description :

A string that define the name of the number variable in the machine data that should be used for filling the bar.

If the machine data doesn't contain any number value with this id the number shown by the bar will always be 0.

The number variable must be at the higher level of the machine data :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#example-2)

Example :

The bar gui element will show the number variable named "amount" from the machine data :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#optional-properties)

Optional properties

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#name-width)

Name : `width`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#description-3)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the width of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#default)

Default :

The same width as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#example-3)

Example :

The width of the element will be 100px.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#description-4)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the height of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#default-1)

Default :

The same height as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#example-4)

Example :

The height of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#description-5)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#example-5)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

chevron-rightEmpty texture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#empty-texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#name-texture_empty)

Name : `texture_empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#description-6)

Description :

Point to a texture to use as the empty element texture. The texture must be loaded in-game with a resource pack or a loader mod.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the `width` and `height` properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the `width` and/or `height` properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#default-2)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#example-6)

Example :

The element will search for a texture located in `assets/namespace/textures/energy_element_texture_empty.png`

**The .png extension is mandatory**.

chevron-rightFilled texture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#filled-texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#name-texture_filled)

Name : `texture_filled`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#description-7)

Description :

Point to a texture to use as the filled element texture. The texture must be loaded in-game with a resource pack or a loader mod.

The filled texture will be rendered on top on the empty texture, how much the filled texture overlap the empty texture is relative to the amount of energy inside the energy component.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#default-3)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#example-7)

Example :

The element will search for a texture located in `assets/namespace/textures/energy_element_texture_filled.png`

**The .png extension is mandatory**.

chevron-rightHighlight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#highlight)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#name-highlight)

Name : `highlight`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#description-8)

Description :

A boolean property, if true the element will highlight (become slightly brighter) when the player mouse hover it. If false the element will not highlight on mouse hover.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#default-true)

Default : true

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#example-8)

Example :

The element will not highlight on mouse hover :

chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#description-9)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

chevron-rightOrientation[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#orientation)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#name-orientation)

Name : `orientation`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/bar-element#description-12)

Description :

The direction the bar will be filled to.

Valid values are : `top`, `right`, `bottom` and `left`.

The bar will fill towards the right for the machine gui.

# Reset element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The reset gui element is a button used to reset the machine to it's idle state.

When clicked, the reset button will stop the current process and put the machine in it's idle state, all already used inputs will be lost.

Reset elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:reset"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#properties)

Properties

The reset gui element has 3 mandatory properties and 7 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:reset" //Mandatory to define a reset element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

####

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

####

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#description-4)

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

chevron-rightTexture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#name-texture)

Name : `texture`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#description-5)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#default-2)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#example-5)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used for the reset element.

chevron-rightTexture hovered[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#texture-hovered)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#name-texture_hovered)

Name : `texture_hovered`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#description-6)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI when the players mouse cursor is hovering the element.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#default-3)

Default :

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#description-7)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#example-6)

Example :

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#description-8)

Description :

The id of this gui element. By default it does nothing and can be omitted.

This is really only useful if you intend to make a recipe that replace this element.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#default-empty)

Default : `empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/reset-element#example-7)

Example :

The id of this element will be `reset`
