# Fluid element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The fluid elements are used to display the content of a fluid component in the Machine GUI.

A Fluid element must be associated with a [Fluid Component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component)
 using the id property. It will display the fluid stored in the Fluid Component on the Machine GUI.

Fluid elements are defined in json with `"type": "custommachinery:fluid"`.

If the fluid element cannot find the fluid Component (usually because of an error in the id) the fluid element will still be rendered but it will always be empty.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#properties)

Properties

The fluid element has 4 mandatory properties and 7 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:fluid" //Mandatory to define a fluid element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "y": 100

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#description-2)

Description :

The id of the [Fluid Component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/fluid-component#mandatory-properties)
 you want to link to this element. It must be the exact same id specified in the fluid component json `id` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#example-2)

Example :

The element will display the fluid component with id `tank1`, if no fluid component has this id it will do nothing.

Copy

    "id": "tank1"

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#optional-properties)

chevron-rightWidth[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#width)

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#description-3)

Description :

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#default)

Default :

The same width as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#example-3)

The width of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightHeight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#height)

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#description-5)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#example-5)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

chevron-rightTexture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#name-texture)

Name : `texture`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#description-6)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#default-2)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#example-6)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_tank_texture.png` will be used for the fluid element.

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI when the players mouse cursor is hovering the element.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fluid-element#default-3)

# PNC Heat element (PNC) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This gui element requires [Custom Machinery Pneumaticcraftarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-pneumaticcraft)
 to be installed.

The heat gui element is used to display the content of a [heat component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc)
 present in the machine.

Heat elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:pnc_heat"`.

Note that if you didn't set a heat component in the machine json the heat element will still work but will always show a value of 0.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#properties)

Properties

The heat element has 3 mandatory properties and 5 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:pnc_heat" //Mandatory to define a PNC heat element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#description-1)

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "y": 100

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightWidth[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#width)

The same width as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

Example :

The width of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightHeight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#height)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#name-height)

Name : `height`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#description-3)

A positive integer value that define the height of the element on the Machine GUI.

####

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#description-4)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#default-0)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#example-4)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#description-5)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pnc-heat-element-pnc#example-5)

Example :

# Pressure element (PNC) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This gui element requires [Custom Machinery Pneumaticcraftarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-pneumaticcraft)
 to be installed.

The pressure gui element is used to display the content of a [pressure component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pressure-component-pnc)
 present in the machine.

Pressure elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:pressure"` .

Note that if you didn't set a pressure component in the machine json the pressure element will still work but will always show a value of 0.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#properties)

Properties

The pressure element has 3 mandatory properties and 5 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:pressure"

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "y": 100

####

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#default)

Default :

The same width as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

Description :

A positive integer value that define the height of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#default-1)

Default :

The same height as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#example-3)

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#description-4)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#example-4)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

####

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/pressure-element-pnc#example-5)

Example :

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

# Fuel element | Custom Machinery 1.21

Fuel element is used to render a fuel bar on the Machine GUI.

Fuel elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:fuel"`.

You can add as many fuel element as you want to the machine GUI but they will all show the same burn time and be filled the same.

By default the texture is the same as the vanilla furnace little flame but you can change it if wanted.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#properties)

Properties

The fuel element has 3 mandatory properties and 8 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:fuel" //Mandatory to define a fuel element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "y": 100

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#optional-properties)

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#example-3)

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Example :

chevron-rightEmpty texture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#empty-texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#name-texture_empty)

Name : `texture_empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#description-5)

Description :

Point to a texture to use as the empty element texture. The texture must be loaded in-game with a resource pack or a loader mod.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the `width` and `height` properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the `width` and/or `height` properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#default-2)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#example-5)

Example :

The element will search for a texture located in `assets/namespace/textures/fuel_element_texture_empty.png`

**The .png extension is mandatory**.

chevron-rightFilled texture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#filled-texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#name-texture_filled)

Name : `texture_filled`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#description-6)

Description :

Point to a texture to use as the filled element texture. The texture must be loaded in-game with a resource pack or a loader mod.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the `width` and `height` properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the `width` and/or `height` properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#default-3)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#example-6)

Example :

The element will search for a texture located in `assets/namespace/textures/fuel_element_texture_filled.png`

**The .png extension is mandatory**.

chevron-rightOrientation[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#orientation)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#name-orientation)

Name : `orientation`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#description-8)

Description :

The direction the bar will be filled to.

####

Default : `empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/fuel-element#example-9)

Example :

The id of this element will be `fuel`

# Machine | Custom Machinery 1.21

Machine is one of the object provided in the [function requirement context](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context)
.

It contains various methods for interacting with the machine.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#methods)

Methods

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#id)

Get the id of the machine, the id is a String of the format : `namespace:path`.

You can also change the machine id, the machine will switch to the specified machine, inventory will be preserved as long as machines have similar inventories.

Copy

    var machine = ctx.machine;
    
    //Return the machine id as a string.
    var id = machine.id;
    
    //Change the machine ID
    machine.id = "namespace:machine_id"

chevron-rightData[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#data)

Add a way to store custom data in the machine.

The stored data will be stored in the machine as NBT and saved when the machine is unloaded, preventing loosing the data, for example, when the game is quitted.

In a CT script the data is retrieved as a [MapDataarrow-up-right](https://docs.blamejared.com/1.18/en/vanilla/api/data/MapData)
.

Copy

    var machine = ctx.machine;
    
    //Get the MapData from the machine.
    var data = machine.data;
    
    //Put something in the data : 
    data.put("power", 2)

chevron-rightOwner[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#owner)

Copy

    var machine = ctx.machine;
    
    //Get the machine owner name as a Component, or null if the machine doesn't have an owner.
    var ownerName = machine.ownerName;
    
    //Get the machine owner UUID, or null if the machine doesn't have an owner.
    var ownerId = machine.ownerId;
    
    //Check if an entity is the owner of the machine.
    var isOwner = machine.isOwner(entity);
    
    //Get the owner as a LivingEntity, or null if the machine doesn't have an owner.
    //This only works if the entity that own the machine is loaded.
    //If the owner is a player they must be connected.
    //IF the owner is a mob it must be in a loaded chunk.
    var owner = machine.owner;
    
    //Set a LivingEntity as the new machine owner.
    machine.owner = entity;

chevron-rightPause[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#pause)

Allow to check if the machine is paused, and pause or resume it.

Copy

    var machine = ctx.machine;
    
    //Return true if the machine is paused, false otherwise
    var paused = machine.paused;
    
    //Pause the machine
    machine.paused = true;
    
    //Resume the machine
    machine.pause = false;

chevron-rightEnergy[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#energy)

chevron-rightFluids[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#fluids)

chevron-rightItems[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#items)

chevron-rightChunkload[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#chunkload)

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#mekanism-support)

Mekanism support

circle-info

The following methods are only available if [Custom Machinery Mekanismarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-mekanism)
 addon is installed.

chevron-rightChemicals[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#chemicals)

All chemicals used here must be a Crafttweaker [ChemicalStackarrow-up-right](https://docs.blamejared.com/1.16/en/mods/Mekanism/api/chemical/stack/ChemicalStack)
.

Examples :

Put 500mB of steam gas in the first available tank.

Remove all the slurry stored in the "slurry" tank.

chevron-rightHeat/Temperature[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#heat-temperature)

chevron-rightRadiations[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#radiations)

[PreviousContextchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/context)
[NextHeat (Mekanism)chevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/heat-mekanism)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Methods](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#methods)
    
*   [Mekanism support](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function/machine#mekanism-support)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    var machine = ctx.machine;
    
    //Return the energy stored in the machine internal buffer.
    var energy = machine.energyStored;
    
    //Return the maximum capacity of the machine energy storage.
    var energyCapacity = machine.energyCapacity;
    
    //Return the amount of energy that was successfully added to the machine (or amountToAdd if all the energy was inserted).
    //If simulate is `false` the energy will really be inserted, otherwise it wont.
    //amountToAdd MUST be a positive value.
    var addedEnergy = machine.addEnergy(amountToAdd, simulate);
    
    //Return the amount of energy that was successfully removed from the machine (or amountToRemove if all the energy was extracted).
    //If simulate is `false` the energy will really be extracted, otherwise it wont.
    //amountToRemove MUST be a positive value.
    var removedEnergy = machine.removeEnergy(amountToRemove, simulate);

Copy

    var machine = ctx.machine;
    
    //Return the fluid stored in the specified tank.
    //The returned fluid is a CT IFluidStack, see docs : https://docs.blamejared.com/1.16/en/vanilla/api/fluid/IFluidStack
    var fluid = machine.getFluidStored("tankID");
    
    //Return the capacity of the specified tank.
    var capacity = machine.getFluidCapacity("tankID");
    
    //Add the specified fluid to the first available tank.
    //Return the amount of fluid that was added.
    //The passed fluid must be a CT IFluidStack, see docs : https://docs.blamejared.com/1.16/en/vanilla/api/fluid/IFluidStack
    //If simulate is `false` the fluid will really be inserted, otherwise it wont.
    var remaining = machine.addFluid(fluid, simulate);
    
    //Add the specified fluid to the specified tank.
    //Return the amount of fluid that was added.
    //The passed fluid must be a CT IFluidStack, see docs : https://docs.blamejared.com/1.16/en/vanilla/api/fluid/IFluidStack
    //If simulate is `false` the fluid will really be inserted, otherwise it wont.
    var remaining = machine.addFluidToTank("tankID", fluid, simulate);
    
    //Remove the specified fluid from the first available tank.
    //Return the fluid that was successfully removed.
    //Both passed and returned fluids must be a CT IFluidStack, see docs : https://docs.blamejared.com/1.16/en/vanilla/api/fluid/IFluidStack
    //If simulate is `false` the fluid will really be removed, otherwise it wont.
    var removedFluid = machine.removeFluid(fluid, simulate);
    
    //Remove the specified amount of fluid from the specified tank.
    //Return the fluid that was successfully removed.
    //The returned fluid is a CT IFluidStack, see docs : https://docs.blamejared.com/1.16/en/vanilla/api/fluid/IFluidStack
    //The specified amount MUST be a positive integer value.
    //If simulate is `false` the fluid will really be removed, otherwise it wont.
    var remaining = machine.removeFluidFromTank("tankID", amount, simulate);

Copy

    var machine = ctx.machine;
    
    //Return the item stored in the specified slot.
    //The returned item is a CT IItemStack, see docs : https://docs.blamejared.com/1.16/en/vanilla/api/items/IItemStack
    var item = machine.getItemStored("slotID");
    
    //Return the capacity of the specified slot.
    var capacity = machine.getItemCapacity("slotID");
    
    //Add the specified item to the specified slot.
    //Return the item that couldn't be added, or an empty ItemStack if all items were successfully added.
    //The passed item must be a CT IItemStack, see docs : https://docs.blamejared.com/1.16/en/vanilla/api/items/IItemStack
    //If simulate is `false` the item will really be inserted, otherwise it wont.
    var remaining = machine.addItemToSlot("slotID", itemToAdd, simulate);
    
    //Remove the specified amount of item from the specified slot.
    //Return the item that were successfully removed, or an empty ItemStack if the slot was empty.
    //The returned item is a CT IItemStack, see docs : https://docs.blamejared.com/1.16/en/vanilla/api/items/IItemStack
    //The specified amount MUST be a positive integer value.
    //If simulate is `false` the item will really be extracted, otherwise it wont.
    var extracted = machine.removeItemFromSlot("slotID", amountToRemove, simulate);
    
    //Lock a slot (players won't be able to place or take items from the GUI but automation will still work.
    machine.lockSlot("slotID");
    //Unlock a slot
    machine.unlockSlot("slotID");
    //Return true if the slot is locked, false otherwise
    var locked = slot.isSlotLocked();

Copy

    let machine = ctx.machine
    
    //Enable chunkloading with a radius of 1
    machine.enableChunkloading(1)
    
    //Disable chunkloading
    machine.disableChunkload()
    
    //Check if chunkloading is active
    let active = machine.isChunkloadEnabled()
    
    //Get the current chunkload radius
    let radius = machine.getChunkloadRadius()

Copy

    //Get the machine from the context.
    var machine = ctx.machine;
    
    //Return the chemical stored in the specified tank.
    var fluid = machine.getChemicalStored("tankID");
    
    //Set a the content of a tank.
    //Doesn't return anything.
    machine.setChemicalStored(chemical);
    
    //Return the capacity of the specified tank.
    var capacity = machine.getChemicalCapacity("tankID");
    
    //Add the specified chemical to the first available tank.
    //Return the chemical that couldn't be added.
    //If simulate is `false` the chemical will really be inserted, otherwise it wont.
    var remaining = machine.addChemical(chemical, simulate);
    
    //Add the specified chemical to the specified tank.
    //Return the chemical that couldn't be added.
    //If simulate is `false` the chemical will really be inserted, otherwise it wont.
    var remaining = machine.addChemicalToTank("tankID", chemical, simulate);
    
    //Remove the specified chemical from the first available tank.
    //Return the chemical that was successfully removed.
    //If simulate is `false` the chemical will really be removed, otherwise it wont.
    var removedFluid = machine.removeChemical(chemical, simulate);
    
    //Remove the specified amount of chemical from the specified tank.
    //Return the chemical that was successfully removed.
    //The specified amount MUST be a positive integer value.
    //If simulate is `false` the chemical will really be removed, otherwise it wont.
    var remaining = machine.removeChemicalFromTank("tankID", amount, simulate);

Copy

    machine.addChemical(<chemical:mekanism:steam> * 500, false);

Copy

    var removedSlurry = machine.removeChemicalFromTank("slurry", machine.getChemicalCapacity("slurry"), false);

Copy

    //Get the machine from the context.
    var machine = ctx.machine;
    
    //Get the heat stored in the machine (as raw decimal value).
    var heat = machine.heat;
    
    //Get the temperature of the machine (in Kelvin I guess).
    var temperature = machine.temperature;
    
    //Add some heat to the machine (you can use negative values to actually remove heat).
    machine.addHeat(amount);
    
    //Set the heat of the machine to a specified value.
    machine.heat = amount;

Copy

    //Get the machine from the context.
    var machine = ctx.machine;
    
    //Get the radiations amount at the machine position.
    var radiations = machine.radiations;
    
    //Add some radiations to the machine position.
    machine.addRadiations(amount);
    
    //Remove radiations in a radius (in blocks) around the machine.
    machine.removeRadiations(amount, radius);

# Energy element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The energy gui element is used to display the content of an [Energy Component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/energy-component)
 present in the machine.

Energy elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:energy"`.

Note that if you didn't set an energy component in the machine json the Energy Element will still work but will always show a value of 0FE.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#properties)

Properties

The energy element has 3 mandatory properties and 9 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:energy" //Mandatory to define an energy element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "y": 100

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightWidth[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#width)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#name-width)

Name : `width`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#description-2)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the width of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#default)

Default :

The same width as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#example-2)

Example :

The width of the element will be 100px.

Copy

    "width": 100

chevron-rightHeight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#height)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#name-height)

Name : `height`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#description-3)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the height of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#default-1)

Default :

The same height as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#example-3)

Example :

The height of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#description-4)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#example-4)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

chevron-rightEmpty texture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#empty-texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#name-texture_empty)

Name : `texture_empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#description-5)

Description :

Point to a texture to use as the empty element texture. The texture must be loaded in-game with a resource pack or a loader mod.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the `width` and `height` properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the `width` and/or `height` properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#default-2)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#example-5)

Example :

The element will search for a texture located in `assets/namespace/textures/energy_element_texture_empty.png`

**The .png extension is mandatory**.

chevron-rightFilled texture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#filled-texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#name-texture_filled)

Name : `texture_filled`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#description-6)

Description :

Point to a texture to use as the filled element texture. The texture must be loaded in-game with a resource pack or a loader mod.

The filled texture will be rendered on top on the empty texture, how much the filled texture overlap the empty texture is relative to the amount of energy inside the energy component.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#default-3)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#example-6)

Example :

The element will search for a texture located in `assets/namespace/textures/energy_element_texture_filled.png`

**The .png extension is mandatory**.

chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#description-7)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#example-7)

Example :

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

chevron-rightHighlight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#highlight)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#name-highlight)

Name : `highlight`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#description-8)

Description :

A boolean property, if true the element will highlight (become slightly brighter) when the player mouse hover it. If false the element will not highlight on mouse hover.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#default-true)

Default : true

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#example-8)

Example :

The element will not highlight on mouse hover :

chevron-rightOrientation[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#orientation)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#name-orientation)

Name : `orientation`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#description-9)

Description :

The direction the bar will be filled to.

Valid values are : `top`, `right`, `bottom` and `left`.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#default-top)

Default : `top`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#example-9)

Example :

The bar will fill towards the right for the machine gui.

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#description-10)

Description :

The id of this gui element. By default it does nothing and can be omitted.

This is really only useful if you intend to make a recipe that replace this element.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#default-empty)

Default : `empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/energy-element#example-10)

Example :

The id of this element will be `energy`

# Experience element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The experience gui element is used to display the amount of xp stored in the machine's [experience component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/experience-component)
.

It can also be used as a button that will take/give xp from/to the player when pressed.

The behavior of the experience element depends of its `mode` property (see below).

Experience elements are defined in json with `"type": "custommachinery:experience"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#properties)

Properties

The experience gui element has 4 mandatory properties and 8 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:experience" //Mandatory to define an experience gui element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "y": 100

chevron-rightMode[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#mode)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#name-mode)

Name : `mode`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#description-2)

Description :

The mode define the behavior of the element, valid values are :

*   "input\_one" : The player who press the button will give 1 level of their xp to the machine.
    
*   "input\_ten" : The player who press the button will give 10 levels of their xp to the machine.
    
*   "input\_all" : The player who press the button will give all their xp to the machine.
    
*   "output\_one" : The player who press the button will be given 1 level from the machine.
    
*   "output\_ten" : The player who press the button will be given 10 levels from the machine.
    
*   "output\_all" : The player who press the button will be given all the xp in the machine.
    
*   "display" : The element will only display a texture and, when hovered, will show the amount of xp stored in the machine.
    
*   "display\_bar" : The element will show a bar representing the amount of xp stored in the machine.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#example-2)

Example :

When pressing this gui element the player will give one level of xp to the machine.

Copy

    "mode": "input_one"

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightWidth[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#width)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#name-width)

Name : `width`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#description-3)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the width of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#default)

Default :

The same width as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#example-3)

Example :

The width of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightHeight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#height)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#name-height)

Name : `height`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#description-4)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the height of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#default-1)

Default :

The same height as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#example-4)

Example :

The height of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#description-5)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#example-5)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

chevron-rightTexture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#name-texture)

Name : `texture`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#description-6)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#default-2)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#example-6)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used for the dump element.

chevron-rightTexture hovered[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#texture-hovered)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#name-texture_hovered)

Name : `texture_hovered`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#description-7)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI when the players mouse cursor is hovering the element.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#default-3)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#example-7)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#description-8)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#example-8)

Example :

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

chevron-rightDisplay[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#display)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#name-display)

Name : `display`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#description-9)

Description :

Only used when the `mode` property is set to `display` or `` display_bar` ``.

This define if the tooltips of this component should show the stored amount of xp as literal or level xp values.

Valid values are :

*   "literal" : Display the amount of xp points stored in the machine.
    
*   "level" : Display the equivalent amount of xp levels stored in the machine, rounded down.
    
*   "both" : Display both.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#default-level)

Default : `level`

The experience gui element's tooltip will display the stored xp as levels.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#example-9)

Example :

The experience gui element's tooltip will display the stored xp as xp points.

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#description-10)

Description :

The id of this gui element. By default it does nothing and can be omitted.

This is really only useful if you intend to make a recipe that replace this element.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#default-experience)

Default : `experience`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#example-10)

Example :

The id of this element will be `experience`

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/experience-element#example-11)

# Player inventory element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The player inventory element is used to render the player inventory into the Machine GUI (only the 4 row of items).

Player inventory elements are defined in json with :

`"type": "custommachinery:player_inventory"`.

circle-info

There can be only one player inventory element per Machine GUI, if you define several Player Inventory Elements only the first will be used.

While you can change the default texture of the player inventory element you can't change the position of it's slots. See the default texture of the player inventory to see how the slots are placed.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#properties)

Properties

The player inventory element has 3 mandatory properties and 7 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:player_inventory" //Mandatory to define a player inventory element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

    "x": 100

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#priority)

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#example-4)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

chevron-rightTexture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#name-texture)

Name : `texture`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#description-5)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#default-2)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#example-5)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/player_inventory.png` will be used for the dump element.

chevron-rightTexture hovered[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#texture-hovered)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#name-texture_hovered)

Name : `texture_hovered`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#description-6)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI when the players mouse cursor is hovering the element.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#default-3)

Default :

None, the element will use the texture defined in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#example-6)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#description-7)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#example-7)

Example :

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#description-8)

Description :

The id of this gui element. By default it does nothing and can be omitted.

This is really only useful if you intend to make a recipe that replace this element.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/player-inventory-element#default-empty)

# Text element | Custom Machinery 1.21

Text element is used to render a text on the Machine GUI.

Text elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:text"`.

The text must be a single [text component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 and can't have multiple lines (use multiple text elements for that).

You can change the size of text using `width` and `height` property.

circle-info

By default all text gui elements are hidden in jei, to make them show up see the "jei" property below.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/text-element#properties)

Properties

The text element has 4 mandatory properties and 7 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/text-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:text" //Mandatory to define a text element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/text-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/text-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/text-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/text-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/text-element#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/text-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/text-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/text-element#example-1)

    "y": 100

 to be rendered on the GUI.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.
