# Button element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The button gui element is used to add a clickable button to the machine gui.

All button elements have a unique string id (that you must specify in the elements properties), when the button is pressed a boolean flag will be written in the machine data. This data can be accessed using [Crafttweaker](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/crafttweaker-deprecated/recipes/function)
 or [KubeJS](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/mod-integrations/kubejs/recipes/function)
 Function requirement.

Simply using `data.buttonID` will give you a boolean that represent the current state of the button (true for pressed, false for released).

A [Button requirement](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button)
 can also be used to make the recipe start only if the button is pressed.

Button elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:button"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#properties)

Properties

The button gui element has 4 mandatory properties and 12 optional properties.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:button" //Mandatory to define a button element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "y": 100

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#description-2)

Description :

A string representing the id of the button, can be used in a Function requirement to check the state of the button, or in a [Button requirement](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button)
 to make the recipe start only when the button is pressed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#example-2)

Example :

The id of the button will be `button1` :

Copy

    "id": "button1"

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightTexture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#name-texture)

Name : `texture`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#description-3)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#default)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#example-3)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

chevron-rightTexture toggle[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#texture-toggle)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#name-texture_toggle)

Name : `texture_toggle`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#description-4)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI when the button is toggled and pressed.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#default-1)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#example-4)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

chevron-rightTexture hovered[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#texture-hovered)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#name-texture_hovered)

Name : `texture_hovered`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#description-5)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI when the players mouse cursor is hovering the element.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#default-2)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#example-5)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

chevron-rightTexture toggle hovered[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#texture-toggle-hovered)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#name-texture_toggle_hovered)

Name : `texture_toggle_hovered`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#description-6)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI when the button is toggled and the player mouse cursor is hovering it.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#default-3)

Default :

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

chevron-rightWidth[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#width)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#name-width)

A positive integer value that define the width of the element on the Machine GUI.

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#default-4)

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#description-9)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#example-8)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#description-10)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

Description :

A text component that will be rendered on top of the button texture.

Note that by default the button texture is 20x20px square so a text too big will overflow from the button texture.

chevron-rightHold time[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#hold-time)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#name-hold_time)

Name : `hold_time`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#description-14)

Description :

A positive integer value that represent the time (in ticks) that the button will stay pressed when a player press it in the machine GUI.

Visually the button will not look pressed but internally the machine will keep it pressed until this hold time is expired.

This can be used when a machine need a button to be pressed to start a recipe, but since the machine check recipes only every 20 ticks the player would have to press the button exactly that tick or the recipe won't start.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#default-1-1)

Default : `1`

The button only stay pressed for 1 tick.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element#example-13)

Example :

The button will stay pressed for 20 ticks (1 second).

sun-brightdesktopmoon

---

# Status element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The status element is used to shown the crafting status of the custom machine in the Machine GUI.

Status element must be defined in json like : `"type": "custommachinery:status"`.

The crafting status of a custom machine can be `IDLE`, `RUNNING` or `ERRORED`.

![](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FZznnGu8KvEhqjN3qmLqp%2Fblobs%2Fu9jeLtoElCw8Atwtqngz%2Fbase_status_idle.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7bb157f&sv=2)`IDLE` mean the machine can't craft any recipes (because of missing inputs)

![running_texture](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FZznnGu8KvEhqjN3qmLqp%2Fblobs%2FgHk6ECTrN3mPtQLs49Nt%2Fbase_status_running.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=65b3352a&sv=2)`RUNNING` mean the machine is currently processing a recipe

![errored_texture](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FZznnGu8KvEhqjN3qmLqp%2Fblobs%2FPQdRDnsAQ9oyWBlltc1E%2Fbase_status_errored.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a3a4a684&sv=2)`ERRORED` mean the machine encountered an error while processing a recipe, the error message will be displayed as a tooltip when you hover the Status Element with your mouse.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/status-element#properties)

Properties

The status element has 3 mandatory properties and 9 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/status-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:status" //Mandatory to define a status element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/status-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/status-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/status-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/status-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/status-element#description-8)

Description :

An integer property which define which status the element will display.

If set to 0 the element will show the general status of the machine.

If set to another value it will show the status of only that specific core.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/status-element#default-5)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/status-element#example-8)

Example :

The status gui element will show the status of core 3 only:

Description :

 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/status-element#example-9)

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

Name : `id`

####

Description :

The id of this gui element. By default it does nothing and can be omitted.

This is really only useful if you intend to make a recipe that replace this element.

# Slot element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The slot elements is used to render an item slot into the Machine GUI.

Slot elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:slot"`.

A slot must be associated with an [Item Component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component)
 using the `id` property. It will display the item stored in the Item Component and allow you to put or remove the item trough the Machine GUI.

If the slot element cannot find the item component (usually because of an error in the id) the slot will still be rendered but it will be empty and you will not be able to put or remove items.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#properties)

Properties

The slot element has 4 mandatory properties and 6 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:slot" //Mandatory to define a slot element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "y": 100

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#description-2)

Description :

The id of the [Item Component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component#mandatory-properties)
 you want to link to this element. It must be the exact same id specified in the item component json `id` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#example-2)

Example :

The element will void the item component with id `slot1`, if no item component has this id it will do nothing.

Copy

    "id": "slot1"

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#optional-properties)

Optional properties

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#name-width)

Name : `width`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#description-3)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the width of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#default)

Default :

The same width as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#example-3)

Example :

The width of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightHeight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#height)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#name-height)

Name : `height`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#description-4)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the height of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#default-1)

Default :

The same height as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#example-4)

Example :

The height of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#description-5)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#example-5)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

chevron-rightTexture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#name-texture)

Name : `texture`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#description-6)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#default-2)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#example-6)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_slot_texture.png` will be used for the slot element.

chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#description-7)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#example-7)

Example :

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

chevron-rightGhost[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#ghost)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#name-ghost)

Name : ghost

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#description-8)

Description :

If specified the slot will render a "ghost item" (slightly transparent item). The item will not be physically present on the slot (aka the player can't take it out). This can be used, for example, to show a filter.

The item must be referenced by it's registry name like `"minecraft:stone"` or `modid:item_name` in general.

This can be a single item, a tag (using "#namespace:id", for example "#forge:stone") or a list of both combined : \["minecraft:diamond", "#forge:stone"\].

All possible items will be cycled in the slot as ghost items, the time between each items can be changed in the config file (default : 1 second).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#default-no-item)

Default : no item

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#extra-properties)

Extra properties :

If needed, a custom color/transparency can be applied to the ghost item (default is white with half transparency). The color must be specified as an ARGB array which value are between 0 and 1.

By default the ghost item will only render if no item are present in the slot, this behavior can be changed by setting `"always_render": true` in the ghost property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#example-8)

Example :

A transparent coal will be displayed in the slot.

An opaque (no transparency) stone, colored in full red will be always displayed in the slot :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element#example-9)

Example :

A basic slot element linked to an item component using the id "slot1" and using the default texture :

Result :

![](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2FFrinn38%2FCustom-Machinery%2Fraw%2F1.16.5%2Fwiki%2Fslot_element.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=274980d9&sv=2)

Slot element base texture

(Here the item component contains 32 diamonds, you can add and remove them through the Slot Element like in any other GUI)

If you add `"item": "minecraft:coal"` to the slot element json the slot will be rendered like this

![](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2FFrinn38%2FCustom-Machinery%2Fraw%2F1.16.5%2Fwiki%2Fslot_element_item.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b4de1f4f&sv=2)

Ghost item in slot element

# Heat element (Mekanism) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This element requires [Custom Machinery Mekanismarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-mekanism)
 to be installed.

The heat gui element is used to display the content of a [heat component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/heat-component-mekanism)
 present in the machine.

Heat elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:heat"`.

Note that if you didn't set a heat component in the machine json the heat element will still work but will always show a value of 0.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#properties)

Properties

The heat element has 3 mandatory properties and 11 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:heat" //Mandatory to define a heat element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

chevron-rightEmpty texture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#empty-texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#name-texture_empty)

Name : `texture_empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#description-5)

Description :

Point to a texture to use as the empty element texture. The texture must be loaded in-game with a resource pack or a loader mod.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the `width` and `height` properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the `width` and/or `height` properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#default-2)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#example-5)

Example :

The element will search for a texture located in `assets/namespace/textures/heat_element_texture_empty.png`

**The .png extension is mandatory**.

chevron-rightFilled texture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#filled-texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#name-texture_filled)

Name : `texture_filled`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#description-6)

Description :

Point to a texture to use as the filled element texture. The texture must be loaded in-game with a resource pack or a loader mod.

The filled texture will be rendered on top on the empty texture, how much the filled texture overlap the empty texture is relative to the amount of heat inside the heat component.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#default-3)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#example-6)

Example :

The element will search for a texture located in `assets/namespace/textures/heat_element_texture_filled.png`

**The .png extension is mandatory**.

chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#description-7)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#example-7)

Example :

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

chevron-rightOrientation[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#orientation)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#name-orientation)

Name : `orientation`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#description-8)

Description :

The direction the bar will be filled to.

Valid values are : `top`, `right`, `bottom` and `left`.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#default-top)

Default : `top`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#example-8)

chevron-rightMin[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#min)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#name-min)

Name : `min`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#description-9)

Description :

A positive decimal value that represent the minimal temperature displayed in the gui element.

If the machine temperature is below this specified value the heat bar will appear empty.

The value is in Kelvin so the minimal accepted value is 0.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#default-300.0)

Default : `300.0`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#example-9)

Example :

The bar will start to fill when the machine temperature is above 400K

chevron-rightMax[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#max)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#name-max)

Name : `max`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#description-10)

Description :

A positive decimal value that represent the maximal temperature displayed in the gui element.

If the machine temperature is above this specified value the heat bar will appear full.

The value is in Kelvin and the minimal accepted value is 1.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#default-400.0)

Default : 4`00.0`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/heat-element-mekanism#example-10)

Example :

The bar will appear full when the machine temperature is at 1000K

# Texture element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The texture gui element is the most basic element, it is used to render a texture on the Machine GUI.

Texture elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:texture"`.

The texture must be loaded into the game by either a resourcepack or a resource loader mod.

Note : By default the Machine GUI don't have any textures, not even a background. If you want a background four your Custom Machine GUI you need to use a Texture Element and set the x/y properties to 0/0.

circle-info

By default all texture gui elements are hidden in jei, to make them show up see the "jei" property below.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#properties)

Properties

The texture element has 4 mandatory properties and 7 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:texture" //Mandatory to define a texture element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "y": 100

chevron-rightTexture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#name-texture)

Name : `texture`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#description-2)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#example-2)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

Copy

    "texture": "namespace:textures/my_texture.png"

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightWidth[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#width)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#name-width)

Name : `width`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#description-3)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the width of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#default)

Default :

The same width as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#example-3)

Example :

The width of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightHeight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#height)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#name-height)

Name : `height`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#description-4)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the height of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#default-1)

Default :

The same height as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#example-4)

Example :

The height of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#description-5)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#example-5)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

chevron-rightJei[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#jei)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#name-jei)

Name : `jei`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#description-6)

Description :

A boolean that define if the element should render in jei.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#default-false)

Default : `false`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#example-6)

Example :

The element will render in jei :

chevron-rightZLevel[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#zlevel)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#name-zlevel)

Name : `zlevel`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#description-7)

Description :

An integer that define the depth (z coordinate) in which the texture will be rendered in the machine gui.

Higher values will make the texture render above anything else, including items, fluids, tooltips etc...

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#default-0-1)

Default : `0`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#example-7)

Example :

By default fluids render at z=100 so this will make the texture render above them :

chevron-rightTexture hovered[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#texture-hovered)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#name-texture_hovered)

Name : `texture_hovered`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#description-8)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI when the players mouse cursor is hovering the element.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#default-2)

Default :

None, the element will use the texture provided in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#example-8)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#description-9)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#example-9)

Example :

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#name-id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/texture-element#description-10)

# Progress bar element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The progress bar element is used to render a progress bar in the Machine GUI (see the arrow that is slowly filled in the furnace GUI while smelting ? That's a progress bar).

Progress bar elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:progress"`.

circle-exclamation

You can add as much Progress Bar Elements as you want but they will all be filled at the same time since the machine can only process 1 recipe at a time.

When hovering the progress bar in jei with advanced item tooltips enabled (F3 + H), the progress bar tooltip will display the recipe ID. You can disable the need of enabling item tooltips in the config by setting `needAdvancedInfoForRecipeID` to false.

circle-info

If JEI is installed you can click on the progress bar element in the machine gui to display in JEI all the recipes for this machine.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#properties)

Properties

The progress bar element has 3 mandatory properties and 10 optional properties :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:progress" //Mandatory to define a progress bar element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "y": 100

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightWidth[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#width)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#name-width)

Name : `width`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#description-2)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the width of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#default)

Default :

The same width as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#example-2)

Example :

The width of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightHeight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#height)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#name-height)

Name : `height`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#description-3)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the height of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#default-1)

Default :

The same height as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#example-3)

Example :

The height of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#description-4)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#example-4)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

chevron-rightEmpty texture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#empty-texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#name-texture_empty)

Name : `texture_empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#description-5)

Description :

Point to a texture to use as the empty element texture. The texture must be loaded in-game with a resource pack or a loader mod.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the `width` and `height` properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the `width` and/or `height` properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#default-2)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#example-5)

Example :

The element will search for a texture located in `assets/namespace/textures/progress_element_texture_empty.png`

**The .png extension is mandatory**.

chevron-rightFilled texture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#filled-texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#name-texture_filled)

Name : `texture_filled`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#description-6)

Description :

Point to a texture to use as the filled element texture. The texture must be loaded in-game with a resource pack or a loader mod.

The filled texture will be rendered on top on the empty texture, how much the filled texture overlap the empty texture is relative to the amount of energy inside the energy component.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#default-3)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#example-6)

Example :

The element will search for a texture located in `assets/namespace/textures/progress_element_texture_filled.png`

**The .png extension is mandatory**.

chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#description-7)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#example-7)

Example :

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

chevron-rightOrientation[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#orientation)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#name-orientation)

Name : `orientation`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#description-8)

Description :

The orientation (right/left/top/bottom) of the arrow. When the recipe is processing the arrow will fill to this direction (from the opposite).

If using custom textures they will not be rotated, but they will be filled according to the specified direction.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#default-right)

Default : `right`

The arrow point to the right and is filled from the left to the right.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#example-8)

Example :

The arrow point to the bottom and is filled from the top to the bottom.

chevron-rightStart[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#start)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#name-start)

Name : `start`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#description-9)

Description :

A positive decimal value that represent at which percentage of the recipe progress the bar should start rendering.

The specified value must be between 0.0 (start of the recipe) and 1.0 (end of the recipe).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#default-0.0)

Default : `0.0`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#example-9)

Example :

The progress bar will start rendering at 30% of the recipe progress :

chevron-rightEnd[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#end)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#name-end)

Name : `end`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#description-10)

Description :

A positive decimal value that represent at which percentage of the recipe progress the bar should stop rendering.

The specified value must be between 0.0 (start of the recipe) and 1.0 (end of the recipe).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#default-1.0)

Default : `1.0`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/progress-bar-element#example-10)

Example :

The progress bar will stop rendering at 80% of the recipe progress :

The id of this gui element. By default it does nothing and can be omitted.

This is really only useful if you intend to make a recipe that replace this element.

# Split element | Custom Machinery 1.21

The split gui element is used to add a clickable button to the machine gui. When clicked, all items present in one of the machine's input slots will be sorted to fill all slots.

circle-info

The behavior is very similar to Mekanism's machines auto-sort button

All split elements must have a unique string id (that you must specify in the elements properties).

Split elements are defined in json with : `"type": "custommachinery:split"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#properties)

Properties

The split gui element has 4 mandatory properties and 9 optional properties.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:button" //Mandatory to define a button element.

chevron-rightX[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#x)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#name-x)

Name : `x`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#description)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the x axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#example)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the right from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "x": 100

chevron-rightY[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#y)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#name-y)

Name : `y`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#description-1)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the y axis position of the element to be displayed on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#example-1)

Example :

The element will be rendered 100px to the bottom from the top-left corner of the gui.

Copy

    "y": 100

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#description-2)

Description :

A string representing the id of the button, can be used in a Function requirement to check the state of the button, or in a [Button requirement](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button)
 to make the recipe start only when the button is pressed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#example-2)

Example :

The id of the button will be `button1` :

Copy

    "id": "button1"

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightTexture[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#texture)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#name-texture)

Name : `texture`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#description-3)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#default)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#example-3)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

chevron-rightTexture toggle[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#texture-toggle)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#name-texture_toggle)

Name : `texture_toggle`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#description-4)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI when the button is toggled and pressed.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#default-1)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#example-4)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

chevron-rightTexture hovered[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#texture-hovered)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#name-texture_hovered)

Name : `texture_hovered`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#description-5)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI when the players mouse cursor is hovering the element.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#default-2)

Default :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#example-5)

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#description-6)

Description :

The location of the texture that will be rendered into the GUI when the button is toggled and the player mouse cursor is hovering it.

The location must be referenced by : `namespace:path/file.png` The texture loader will search for textures in the `assets/namespace` folder, the .png extension is required or the file will not be found.

The texture can be any size, if the texture size is different from the default size the width and height properties of the element will be automatically changed to fit the texture size if not provided.

If the width and/or height properties of the element are provided, the texture will be stretched to fit the dimensions of the element (it can render weirdly in that case).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#default-3)

Default :

Example :

The file `assets/textures/my_texture.png` will be used.

chevron-rightWidth[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#width)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#name-width)

Name : `width`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#description-7)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the width of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#default-4)

Default :

The same width as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#example-6)

Example :

The width of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightHeight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#height)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#name-height)

Name : `height`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#description-8)

Description :

A positive integer value that define the height of the element on the Machine GUI.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#default-5)

Default :

The same height as the texture specified in the `texture` property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#example-7)

Example :

The height of the element will be 100px.

chevron-rightPriority[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#priority)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#name-priority)

Name : `priority`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#description-9)

Description :

An integer property that define the priority of the Element to be rendered.

Elements with higher priority will be rendered first. If 2 elements are at the same position the first to be rendered will be under and the last will be above.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#example-8)

Example :

The element will be rendered under each element that have a priority lower than 1000.

chevron-rightTooltips[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#tooltips)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#name-tooltips)

Name : `tooltips`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#description-10)

Description :

A list of [Text components](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
 that will be shown as tooltips when the player mouse cursor hover the element.

Each tooltips of the list will be a new line.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#example-9)

Example :

Replace the default tooltips with a single line that say "Click me !" :

chevron-rightSlots[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#slots)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#name-slots)

Name : `slots`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#description-11)

Description :

A list of slot ids which are the slots that will be sorted while this split button is active.

The slots ids must be the same as specified in the [Item component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component)
 and [Slot element](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/slot-element)
 `id`property.

If the list is empty then any normal slot (not fuel, upgrade, etc) in `input`mode will be sorted.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#default-empty)

Default : `empty`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/split-element#example-10)

Example :

While this split element is active, only slots with ids `input1`, `input2`, `input3` will be sorted.

# Recipe modifiers | Custom Machinery 1.21

Requirement modifiers are used to tweak some properties of a recipe requirement.

They are defined in json inside of the `requirements` property of the machine upgrade item json.

###
