### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#properties)

Properties

The requirement modifier has 4 mandatory properties and 2 optional property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

chevron-rightRequirement[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#requirement)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#name-requirement)

Name : `requirement`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#description)

Description :

The type of the requirement you want to apply the modifier to. This is the same type as the one you specify in the `type` property when defining the requirement in the recipe json.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#example)

Example :

This modifier will be applied to the energy requirement.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#note)

Note :

The recipe duration can also be modified with this system.

Use `custommachinery:speed` to target it.

Warning : Using this as a requirement will alter the recipe process duration, which is the opposite of the speed (the lower the duration the faster the speed).

chevron-rightMode[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#mode)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#name-mode)

Name : `mode`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#description-1)

Description :

The mode of the requirement you want to apply the modifier to. It can be either `input` or `output` but not both.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#example-1)

Example :

This modifier will be applied only on input requirements.

chevron-rightOperation[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#operation)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#name-operation)

Name : `operation`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#description-2)

Description :

The mathematical operation that will be applied to the targeted requirement property by the modifier. The available operations are :

*   `addition` : The resulting value will be the sum of the base requirement value and the modifier value multiplied by the amount of upgrades. `final_value = base_value + upgrade_modifier * upgrade_amount`
    
*   `multiplication` : The resulting value will be the multiplication of the base requirement value and the modifier value multiplied by the amount of upgrades. `final_value = base_value * upgrade_modifier * upgrade_amount`
    
*   exponential : The resulting value will be the multiplication of the base requirement value and the modifier value powered to the amount of upgrades. `final_value = base_value * upgrade_modifier ^ upgrade_amount`
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#example-2)

Example :

The base requirement value (defined in the recipe) will be multiplicated by the value defined in this modifier.

chevron-rightModifier[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#modifier)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#name-modifier)

Name : `modifier`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#description-3)

Description :

The value (double) to add or multiply to the base requirement value. It can be positive or negative and support decimal numbers.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#example-3)

Example :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightTarget[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#target)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#name-target)

Name : `target`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#description-4)

Description :

Some requirement have more than one value that can be modified.

In that case the `target` property can be used to define which one of the requirement property you want to modify.

For example some requirement have a `chance` property that can be modified by the upgrade, simply use `"target": "chance"` to target the chance property instead of the default one.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#default-empty)

Default : `empty`

The modifier will be applied to the default property of the defined requirement.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#example-4)

Example :

In case of the [Entity Requirementarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Frinn38/Custom-Machinery/wiki/Entity-Requirement)
 the default property is `amount` so if you want to modify the `radius` property you can do :

chevron-rightChance[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#chance)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#name-chance)

Name : `chance`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#description-5)

Description :

The chance the modifier will be applied to the requirement, this have nothing to do with the `chance` property some requirement have and will be applied independently.

This value must be between 0 and 1 where 0 is 0% chance to be applied and 1 is 100% chance.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#default-1)

Default : 1

The modifier have 100% chance to be applied on the requirement.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#example-5)

Example :

The modifier have 40% chance to be applied on the requirement.

chevron-rightMax[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#max)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#name-max)

Name : `max`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#description-6)

Description :

A positive integer that define the maximum value obtained after applying this upgrade.

Fox example if the modifier multiply all energy output by 2 and the max is set to 1000, the maximum energy output by the recipe will be 1000FE, even if it should be greater after the multiplication.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#default-positive_infinity)

Default : `POSITIVE_INFINITY`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#example-6)

Example :

Whatever the modifier does, the resulting value won't be greater than 42.

chevron-rightMin[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#min)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#name-min)

Name : `min`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#description-7)

Description :

A positive integer that define the minimum value obtained after applying this upgrade.

Fox example if the modifier divide all items consumed by 2 and the min is set to 1, the recipe will always consume 1 item.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#default-negative_infinity)

Default : `NEGATIVE_INFINITY`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#example-7)

Example :

Whatever the modifier does, the resulting value won't be lower than 42.

chevron-rightTooltip[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#tooltip)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#name-tooltip)

Name : `tooltip`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#description-8)

Description :

The tooltip that will render when a player hover any machine upgrade item in a gui while holding shift. This is a [text component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/text-component)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#default)

Default :

A short string that describe what the modifier does : `-50% Energy input`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#example-8)

Example :

The tooltip will be "Overclock: Recipe time divided by 2" in orange.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/upgrades/recipe-modifiers#example-9)

# Requirements | Custom Machinery 1.21

Recipe requirements are what make a recipe do things, should it be inputs, outputs, world interaction etc...

A recipe can take an unlimited amount of requirements.

When processing a recipe, the machine will check all requirements and execute their actions, if one or several requirement couldn't be processed, the machine will switch to error status, display an error and try again later.

Requirements are defined in a recipe json using the `"requirement"` property to specify an array of requirements :

recipe.json

Copy

    {
        "requirements": [\
            {\
                //Requirement 1\
            },\
            {\
                //Requirement 2\
            }\
        ]
    }

The `"requirement"` property is optional but the recipe will do nothing if no requirements are specified.

circle-info

You can add or change the [display info](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/requirement-display-info)
 of any requirement.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements#available-requirements)

Available requirements

There are currently 23 requirement types implemented, each one of them have a specific goal and can be configured as you need.

[Biomechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome)
[Blockchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/block)
[Commandchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command)
[Dimensionchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension)

# Biome | Custom Machinery 1.21

Biome requirement is used to make the custom machine recipe work only in some biomes of the world.

The biome requirement is an input only requirement, meaning that you don't have to define the `mode` property. It is used only to restrict or allow the usage of a recipe in certain biomes of the world.

The type of biome requirement is : `"custommachinery:biome"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#properties)

Properties

The biome requirement has 2 mandatory properties and 1 optional property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:biome" //Mandatory to define a biome requirement.

chevron-rightFilter[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#filter)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#name-filter)

Name : `filter`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#description)

Description :

A single or array of Biome ID to check if the machine is in or not. The biomes ID must must be like "minecraft:plains" or any custom biomes. This list may be a whitelist or a blacklist depending of the "blacklist" property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#default)

Default :

Empty, so any biomes will be allowed if the filter is a whitelist.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#example)

Example :

Copy

    "filter": ["minecraft:savanna"]

The recipe will only run if the machine is in a Savanna biome.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightBlacklist[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#blacklist)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#name-blacklist)

Name: `blacklist`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#description-1)

Description :

A Boolean value used to define if the "filter" property should be a blacklist instead of a whitelist.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#default-false)

Default : `false`

The "filter" property will act as a whitelist.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#example-1)

Example :

Copy

    "blacklist": true

The "filter" property will act as a blacklist.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#example-2)

Example

A biome requirement that will make the recipe works in all biomes but the vanilla plains :

[PreviousRequirementschevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements)
[NextBlockchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/block)

*   [Properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#properties)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/biome#example-2)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:biome",
        "filter": "minecraft:plains",
        "blacklist": true
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Chunkload | Custom Machinery 1.21

The chunkload requirement can be used to make the machine chunkload an area around it.

Unlike the [Chunkload machine component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/chunkload-component)
, this requirement will chunkload the area only while the recipe is processing.

If the recipe containing this requirement stop processing (because some other requirement aren't valid for example) the chunkload will stop too.

The type of chunkload requirement is : `"custommachinery:chunkload"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chunkload#properties)

Properties

The button requirement only has 1 mandatory property and 1 optional property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chunkload#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:chunkload" //Mandatory to define a chunkload requirement.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chunkload#optional-property)

Optional property

chevron-rightRadius[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chunkload#radius)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chunkload#name-radius)

Name : `radius`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chunkload#description)

Description :

The radius (in chunks) of the chunkloading area. The radius include the center chunk (where the machine is placed) so a radius of 2 means an area of 3x3 chunks.

Must be between 1 and 32.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chunkload#default-1)

Default : `1`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chunkload#example)

Example :

The machine will chunkload an area of 3x3 chunks.

Copy

    "radius": 2

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chunkload#example-1)

Example

A chunkload requirement that will make the machine chunkload an area of 3x3 chunks around it as long as the recipe is processing :

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:chunkload",
        "radius": 2
    }

[PreviousChemical (Mekanism)chevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chemical-mekanism)
[NextContraption requirement (Create)chevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create)

*   [Properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chunkload#properties)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/chunkload#example-1)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Dimension | Custom Machinery 1.21

Dimension requirement is used to make the custom machine recipe work only in some dimensions of the world.

The dimension requirement is an input only requirement, meaning that you don't have to define the "mode" property. It is used only to restrict or allow the usage of a recipe in certain dimensions of the world.

The type of dimension requirement is : `"custommachinery:dimension"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#properties)

Properties

The dimension requirement has 2 mandatory properties and 1 optional property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:dimension" //Mandatory to define a dimension requirement.

chevron-rightFilter[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#filter)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#name-filter)

Name : `filter`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#description)

Description :

A single or array of dimensions ID to check if the machine is in or not. The dimensions ID must mus be like "minecraft:overworld" or any custom dimensions. This list may be a whitelist or a blacklist depending of the "blacklist" property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#default-empty)

Default : `empty`

Any biomes will be allowed if the filter is a whitelist.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#example)

Example :

Copy

    "filter": ["minecraft:overworld"]

The recipe will only run if the machine is in the overworld.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightBlacklist[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#blacklist)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#name-blacklist)

Name : `blacklist`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#description-1)

Description :

A Boolean value used to define if the "filter" property should be a blacklist instead of a whitelist.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#default-false)

Default : `false`

The "filter" property will act as a whitelist.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#example-1)

Example :

Copy

    "blacklist": true

The "filter" property will act as a blacklist.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension#example-2)

Example

A dimension requirement that will make the recipe works in all dimensions but the overworld :

[PreviousCommandchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command)
[NextDropchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/drop)

        "type": "custommachinery:dimension",
        "filter": "minecraft:overworld",
        "blacklist": true

# Sky | Custom Machinery 1.21

This requirement will only check if the machine has clear access to the sky.

The check occurs every tick so if the machine stop having access to the sky during a process (for example if a player place a block above it), it will stop and wait for sky to be visible again.

The requirement type of sky requirement is : `"custommachinery:sky"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/sky#properties)

Properties

The sky requirement has 1 mandatory property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/sky#mandatory-property)

Mandatory property

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:sky" //Mandatory to define a sky requirement.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/sky#example)

Example

How to define a sky requirement:

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:sky"
    }

[PreviousPressure (PNC)chevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/pressure-pnc)
[NextStructurechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/structure)

*   [Properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/sky#properties)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/sky#example)

# Fuel | Custom Machinery 1.21

Fuel requirement is used to make the recipe need a fuel to be processed (like a furnace).

The fuel item must be provided with an [Item Component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/item-component)
 with the `"variant": "custommachinery:fuel"` property.

This requirement will only check if the machine is burning fuel. The check occurs every tick so if the machine run out of fuel during a process it will stop and wait for the player to add some fuel.

The requirement type of fuel requirement is : `"custommachinery:fuel"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/fuel#properties)

Properties

The fuel requirement has 1 mandatory property and 1 optional property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/fuel#mandatory-property)

Mandatory property

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:fuel" //Mandatory to define a fuel requirement.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/fuel#optional-property)

Optional property

chevron-rightAmount[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/fuel#amount)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/fuel#name-amount)

Name : `amount`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/fuel#description)

Description :

A positive integer that define the amount of fuel burn each tick of the recipe process.

If the machine don't have enough burn time remaining a fuel item will be consumed and it's corresponding burn time will be added. If no fuel item is found the machine will stop and error.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/fuel#default-1)

Default : 1

The requirement will consume 1 burn time each recipe process tick (same as the vanilla furnace).

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/fuel#example)

Example :

Copy

    "amount": 2

The requirement will consume 2 burn time each tick, meaning the fuel will be consumed 2 times faster than in a vanilla furnace.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/fuel#example-1)

Example

How to define a fuel requirement:

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:fuel"
    }

[PreviousFluid per tickchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/fluid-per-tick)
[NextHeat (Mekanism)chevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/heat-mekanism)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/fuel#properties)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/fuel#example-1)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Light | Custom Machinery 1.21

Light requirement is used to check the sky or block light level at the machine position.

This requirement is INPUT only, you don't have to specify a `mode` property.

This requirement will block the start of the recipe if the required light level is not met, but it will never consume or produce anything.

The requirement type of light requirement is : `"custommachinery:light"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#properties)

Properties

The light requirement has 2 mandatory properties and 1 optional property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:light" //Mandatory to define a light requirement.

chevron-rightLight[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#light)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#name-light)

Name : `light`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#description)

Description :

A [Range](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/range)
 that define the valid light level the machine need to process the recipe.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#example)

Example :

Copy

    "light": "8"

Require a light level of 8.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightSky[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#sky)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#name-sky)

Name : `sky`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#description-1)

Description :

A boolean, if true the requirement will check the sky light level, if false it will check the block light level.

The maximum sky light level the machine can see is 14.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#default-false)

Default : `false`

Check the block light level.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#example-1)

Example :

Copy

    "sky": true

The machine will check the sky light level.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#example-2)

Example

A light requirement that will make the recipe start only if the sky light level is below 7 :

[PreviousItem filterchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/item-filter)
[NextLoot tablechevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table)

*   [Properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#properties)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light#example-2)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:light",
        "light": "(,7)",
        "sky": true
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Contraption requirement (Create) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This requirement requires [Custom Machinery Createarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-create)
 to be installed.

The contraption requirement is used to make a recipe able to require or produce some Create kinetic speed and stress.

This requirement is available in both `input` and `output` modes.

The requirement type of contraption requirement is : `"custommachinery:contraption"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#properties)

Properties

The block requirement has 3 mandatory properties and 1 optional property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:contraption" //Mandatory to define a contraption requirement.

chevron-rightMode[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#mode)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#name-mode)

Name : `mode`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#description)

Description :

Define the mode (input or output) of this requirement.

*   Input : The recipe will requires the specified amount of kinetic speed to start. If a stress value is specified the recipe will add a stress impact of `speed * stress` to the kinetic network.
    
*   Output : The recipe will produce the specified amount of kinetic speed while the machine is running. If a stress value is specified the recipe will add a stress capacity of `speed * stress` to the kinetic network.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#example)

Example :

The recipe will produce SU :

Copy

    "mode": "output"

chevron-rightSpeed[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#speed)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#name-speed)

Name : `speed`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#description-1)

Description :

A positive decimal value that define the amount of kinetic speed (in RPM)that the recipe will require or produce.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#example-1)

Example :

The recipe will require or produce 64rpm :

Copy

    "speed": 64

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#optional-property)

Optional property

chevron-rightStress[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#stress)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#name-stress)

Name : `stress`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#description-2)

Description :

A positive decimal value that define the kinetic stress capacity or impact (depending on the mode property) that the recipe will add to the kinetic network.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#default-0)

Default : 0

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#example-2)

Example :

Add a kinetic stress impact/capacity of 2 times the machine speed :

chevron-rightScaling[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#scaling)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#name-scaling)

Name : `scaling`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#description-3)

Description :

A boolean that define if the recipe processing speed should be scaled to the rotation speed provided to the machine.

For example if the recipe requires a speed of 128 and a speed of 256 is provided the recipe will be processed 2x faster.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#default-false)

Default : `false`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#example-3)

Example :

The processing speed will be scaled to the rotation speed :

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create#example-4)

Example

A contraption requirement that will make the recipe require at least 64rpm to start and add a stress impact of 2 times its speed to the network :

        "mode": "input",

# Redstone | Custom Machinery 1.21

Redstone requirement is used to make the recipe work only when the machine receive a specific redstone signal.

This requirement is an **input only** requirement, meaning that you don't have to define the `mode` property.

It is used only to block or allow the usage of a recipe under certain conditions but don't have any real inputs or outputs.

The requirement type of redstone requirement is : `"custommachinery:redstone"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/redstone#properties)

Properties

The redstone requirement has 2 mandatory properties.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/redstone#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:redstone" //Mandatory to define a redstone requirement.

chevron-rightPower[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/redstone#power)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/redstone#name-power)

Name : `power`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/redstone#description)

Description :

A [range](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/range)
 that define the valid redstone signal (between 0 and 15) the machine need to process the recipe.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/redstone#example)

Example :

The recipe will only start if the machine receive a redstone signal of exactly 1.

Copy

    "power": "1"

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/redstone#example-1)

Example

A redstone requirement that will make the recipe start only if the machine received redstone signal is lower or equals than 8.

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:redstone",
        "power": "(,8)"
    }

[PreviousRadiation (Mekanism)chevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism)
[NextTemperature (Mekanism)chevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/temperature-mekanism)

*   [Properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/redstone#properties)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/redstone#example-1)

# Button | Custom Machinery 1.21

Button requirement is used to make the custom machine recipe start only when the player press a button in the machine gui.

The button requirement is an input only requirement, meaning that you don't have to define the `mode` property.

The type of button requirement is : `"custommachinery:button"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button#properties)

Properties

The button requirement has 2 mandatory properties and 1 optional property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:button" //Mandatory to define a button requirement.

chevron-rightId[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button#id)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button#name-id)

Name : `id`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button#description)

Description :

The string id of the [button element](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-gui/button-element)
 that must be pressed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button#example)

Example :

The recipe will start only if the button with id `button1` is pressed by the player.

Copy

    "id": "button1"

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button#optional-property)

Optional property

chevron-rightInverse[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button#inverse)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button#name-inverse)

Name : `inverse`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button#description-1)

Description :

A boolean that will make the recipe require the button to **not** be pressed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button#default-false)

Default : `false`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button#example-1)

Example :

The recipe will start if the button is not pressed :

Copy

    "inverse": true

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/button#example-2)

# PNC Temperature (PNC) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This requirement requires [Custom Machinery Pneumaticcraftarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-pneumaticcraft)
 to be installed.

The temperature requirement can be used to make a recipe start only if the machine's [heat component](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/creating-custom-machines/machine-components/pnc-heat-component-pnc)
 temperature is at a specific value.

This requirement doesn't consume or produce anything, it's only a condition for the recipe to start.

The requirement type of temperature requirement is : "`custommachinery:pnc_temperature"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/pnc-temperature-pnc#properties)

Properties

The temperature requirement has 2 mandatory properties.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/pnc-temperature-pnc#mandatory-property)

Mandatory property

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:pnc_temperature" //Mandatory to define a temperature requirement.

chevron-rightTemperature[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/pnc-temperature-pnc#temperature)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/pnc-temperature-pnc#name-temperature)

Name : `temperature`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/pnc-temperature-pnc#description)

Description :

A [Range](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/misc/range)
 of values that will allow the recipe to start.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/pnc-temperature-pnc#example)

Example :

The recipe will start only if the machine temperature is above 100°C

Copy

    "temperature": "(100,)"

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/pnc-temperature-pnc#example-1)

Example

A temperature requirement that will allow the recipe to run only if the machine temperature is higher than 100°C :

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:pnc_temperature",
        "temperature": "(100,)"
    }

[PreviousPNC Heat (PNC)chevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/pnc-heat-pnc)
[NextPositionchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/position)

# Command | Custom Machinery 1.21

Command requirement is used to make the custom machine execute commands while crafting.

This requirement doesn't have a mode and will not stop the processing of a recipe even if the command fail.

The command can be executed at the start, at the end or every tick of the crafting process (see the `phase` property below).

The requirement type of command requirement is : `"custommachinery:command"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#properties)

Properties

The command requirement has 2 mandatory properties and 5 optional properties.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:command" //Mandatory to define a command requirement.

chevron-rightCommand[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#command)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#name-command)

Name : `command`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#description)

Description :

A string which represent the command to run, it must have the same syntax as when you run command in the chat (so begin with "/").

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#example)

Example :

Copy

    "command": "/time set 0"

The machine's world time will be set to 0.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#optional-properties)

Optional properties

chevron-rightPermission level[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#permission-level)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#name-permissionlevel)

Name : `permissionlevel`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#description-1)

Description :

An integer that define the permission level the machine can run the command. In vanilla a player have a permission level of 1 and an op player have 4, see [herearrow-up-right](https://nodecraft.com/support/games/minecraft/how-to-set-a-player-as-op-admin)
 for more infos.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#default-2)

Default : 2

Should be good enough to execute most commands.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#example-1)

Example :

Copy

    "permissionlevel": 4

The machine will run the command as an op.

chevron-rightLog[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#log)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#description-2)

Description :

A boolean (true/false) that define if the machine should log the command when executed, if true a system message in the chat, console and logs will be shown. It can be used for debug.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#default-false)

Default : `false`

No logs, the machine will print a message in the logs only when it fail to execute a command but never in the chat.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#example-2)

Example :

Will print the command result in the chat/console/logs when executed.

chevron-rightTick[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#tick)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#description-3)

Description :

A boolean (true/false) that define if the command should be executed each tick or just once.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#default-false-1)

Default : `false`

The command will be executed once.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#example-3)

Example :

The command will be executed each tick.

chevron-rightChance[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#chance)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#name-chance)

Name : `chance`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#description-4)

Description :

A double between 0.0 and 1.0 that define the chance of the command to be run.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#default-1)

Default : 1

The command will always be run.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#example-4)

Example :

The command will have 70% chance to be run.

chevron-rightDelay[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#delay)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#name-delay)

Name : `delay`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#description-5)

Description :

A double value, between 0.0 and 1.0 that represents at which time of the recipe the command must be executed. A delay of 0.5 represent half of the recipe, 0.25 a quarter etc...

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#default-1-1)

Default : `1`

The command will be executed at the end of the recipe process.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#example-5)

Example :

The command will be executed when the recipe progress time is at (approximatively) a third of the recipe total duration.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#example-6)

Example

A command requirement that will spawn a Zombie when the recipe finish with 50% chance:

[PreviousContraption requirement (Create)chevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/contraption-requirement-create)
[NextDimensionchevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/dimension)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [Properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#properties)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/command#example-6)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    "log": "true"

Copy

    "tick": true

Copy

    "chance": 0.7

Copy

    "delay": 0.33

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:command",
        "command": "/summon minecraft:zombie",
        "permission": 4,
        "chance": 0.5
    }

# Loot table | Custom Machinery 1.21

Loot table requirement is used to generate item outputs based on a vanilla, modded or custom loot table.

This requirement is OUTPUT only, you don't have to specify a `mode` property.

This requirement will block the end of the recipe if the generated items can't be put in a slot (because all slots are full for example).

The requirement type of loot table requirement is : "`custommachinery:loot_table"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#properties)

Properties

The loot table requirement has 2 mandatory properties and 1 optional property.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:loot_table" //Mandatory to define a loot table requirement.

chevron-rightTable[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#table)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#name-table)

Name : `table`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#description)

Description :

Define the path of the loot table file to use.

The path must be of the format: `namespace:path/from/the/loot_tables/folder`.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#example)

Example :

Copy

    "table": "custommachinery:my_loot_table"

The requirement will use a loot table located in `data/custommachinery/loot_tables/my_loot_table.json`.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#optional-property)

Optional property

chevron-rightLuck[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#luck)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#name-luck)

Name : `luck`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#description-1)

Description :

A float that can be used in the loot table to affect the number of generated items.

See [vanilla wikiarrow-up-right](https://minecraft.fandom.com/wiki/Loot_table)
 for more info about loot tables.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#default-0)

Default : `0`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#example-1)

Example :

Copy

    "luck": 1.0

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#example-2)

Example

A loot table requirement that will make the recipe output either 28 diamonds or a stone in the #forge:stones tag.

In `data/custommachinery/loot_tables/test_loot_table.json`

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#notes)

Notes

Minecraft loot tables are a very complex system, which is made to be used in many ways (block and mobs drops, dungeon chests, plant harvest etc...) and that would be a hell to support and test all possibilities of loot tables. So some things may break, other may not work.

Loot tables have a `type` property, when possible use `"type": "custommachinery:custom_machine"`. It may not be needed thought.

If you have any issues with the loot table requirement and you seek support in the github issues or in the discord, please include the loot table file and describe the most precisely possible what it should do. I am not a loot tables expert and I can't spend hours on the wiki just to understand what your loot table does.

[PreviousLightchevron-left](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/light)
[NextPNC Heat (PNC)chevron-right](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/pnc-heat-pnc)

*   [Properties](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#properties)
    
*   [Example](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#example-2)
    
*   [Notes](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/loot-table#notes)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommachinery:loot_table",
        "table": "custommachinery:text_loot_table"
    }

test\_loot\_table.json

Copy

    {
        "type": "custommahinery:custom_machine",
        "pools": [\
    	{\
    	    "rolls": 1,\
    	    "entries": [\
    		{\
    		    "functions": [\
    			{\
    			    "function": "set_count",\
    			    "count": 25\
    		        }\
    		    ],\
    		    "type": "minecraft:item",\
    		    "name": "minecraft:diamond"\
    		},\
    		{\
    		    "type": "tag",\
    		    "name": "forge:stone",\
    		    "expand": true\
    	        }\
    	    ]\
    	}\
        ]
    }

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Radiation (Mekanism) | Custom Machinery 1.21

circle-exclamation

This requirement requires [Custom Machinery Mekanismarrow-up-right](https://www.curseforge.com/minecraft/mc-mods/custom-machinery-mekanism)
 to be installed.

The radiation requirement and its per-tick variant can be used to make a recipe absorb or emit radiations near the machine.

All radiation amounts are expressed in Sievert (Sv).

[Herearrow-up-right](https://github.com/mekanism/Mekanism/blob/1.19.x/src/api/java/mekanism/api/radiation/IRadiationManager.java#L21-L37)
 is a link to the Mekanism javadoc description about radiation amounts.

The requirement type of radiation requirement is `"custommachinery:radiation"` and for the radiation per tick requirement : `"custommachinery:radiation_per_tick"`.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#properties)

Properties

The radiation requirement has 3 mandatory properties and 1 optional property :

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#mandatory-properties)

Mandatory properties

Copy

    "type": "custommachinery:radiation" //Mandatory to define a radiation requirement.
    OR
    "type": "custommachinery:radiation_per_tick" //Mandatory to define a radiation per tick requirement.

chevron-rightMode[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#mode)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#name-mode)

Name : `mode`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#description)

Description :

A property that define if the recipe will absorb or emit radiations.

*   `input` : The recipe will absorb radiations.
    
*   `output` : The recipe will emit radiations.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#example)

Example :

The recipe will absorb radiations :

Copy

    "mode": "input"

chevron-rightAmount[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#amount)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#name-amount)

Name : `amount`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#description-1)

Description :

A positive, decimal value that represent the amount (in Sv) of radiations to emit or absorb.

Keep in mind that 1Sv is a **very** high value, in most case you will need to use mSv (0.001Sv) or even µSv (0.000001Sv) except of course if you need the equivalent of a nuclear reactor meltdown.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#example-1)

Example :

The recipe will absorb/emit 0.001Sv.

Copy

    "amount": 0.001

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#optional-property)

Optional property

chevron-rightRadius[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#radius)

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#name-radius)

Name : `radius`

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#description-2)

Description :

**Use only in input mode.**

A positive integer that represent the radius (in blocks) that the machine will search for radiation sources to absorb.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#default)

Default :

The value of Mekanism config `radiationChunkCheckRadius` (5 by default) x16.

#### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#example-2)

Example :

The machine will search for radiation sources to absorb in a 10 blocks radius.

### 

[hashtag](https://frinn.gitbook.io/custom-machinery-1.21/recipes/requirements/radiation-mekanism#example-3)

Example

A radiation per tick requirement that will make the recipe absorb 0.001Sv each tick :

    "radius": 10

    {
        "type": "radiation_per_tick",
        "amount": 0.001
